　　You temporarily link the fates of any two creatures, if both fail their saving throws. If either linked creature experiences pain, both feel it. When one loses hit points, the other loses the same amount. If either dies, the other must immediately succeed at a Fortitude save or gain a number of negative levels equal to the character level of the creature that died (minimum one). All other effects are not transferred by the fate link. You could attempt to create a chain of fate linked creatures, if desired.
　
逆天术(Fate of One)
　　心灵预言系(感知)
　　等级：心灵术士4
　　异象：精神、视觉
　　显能时间：见说明
　　距离：个人
　　目标：自己
　　持续时间：立即
　　灵能点：7
　　你有限的全知能力让你可以重掷豁免检定、攻击检定或技能检定并使用两次掷骰结果中较好的一个。
　　你可以即时展现本异能，快到足够紧要关头带来好处。展现本异能是即时动作，如同展现瞬发异能，这将计入每轮可使用的瞬发异能限制。
　
Fate of One
　　Clairsentience (Wis)
　　Level: Psion 4
　　Display: Me, Vi
　　Manifestation Time: See text
　　Range: Personal
　　Target: You
　　Duration: Instantaneous
　　Power Points: 7
　　Your limited omniscience allows you to reroll a saving throw, attack roll, or skill check, and use the better of the two rolls for your result.
　　You can manifest this power instantly, quickly enough to gain its benefits in a clutch situation. Manifesting the power is a free action, like manifesting a quickened power, and it counts toward the normal limit of one quickened power per round.
　
羽落术(Feather Fall)
　　心灵传送系(敏捷)
　　等级：心灵术士1
　　异象：听觉
　　显能时间：见说明
　　距离：近距 (25+5/2等级)
　　目标群：半径10漳诘淖杂陕湎碌淖苤夭怀过300磅/等级的物体或生物
　　持续时间：直到落地，或经过1轮/等级
　　豁免检定：意志，通过则无效 (物体)
　　异能抗力：可 (物体)
　　灵能点：1
　　受影响的生物或物体会在空中缓慢落下，落下的速度立即变为每轮约60眨ㄓ氪邮章湎碌乃俣认嗳簦。在异能持续时间内落地不会受伤，超过持续时间後就恢复正常下落的速度。
　　你可以即时展现本异能，快到足够在失足跌落时挽救你自己。展现本异能是即时动作，如同展现瞬发异能，这将计入每轮可使用的瞬发异能限制。
　　本异能对远程武器没有影响，除非它是从高空坠落。如果异能目标是从高出正在坠落的物品，例如从城堡上掷下的大石，物品只对下面的生物造成一半伤害（每400磅造成1d6伤害），且没有坠落高度加值。
　　本异能只对自由下落的物体起效。它不能影响剑的挥砍或飞行生物的冲锋。
　
Feather Fall
　　Psychoportation (Dex)
　　Level: Psion 1
　　Display: Au
　　Manifestation Time: See text
　　Range: Close (25 ft. + 5 ft./2 levels)
　　Targets: Any free-falling objects or creatures in a 10-ft. radius whose weight does not total more than 300 lb./level
　　Duration: Until landing or 1 round/level
　　Saving Throw: Will negates (object)
　　Power Resistance: Yes (object)
　　Power Points: 1
　　The creatures or objects affected fall slowly. The rate of fall is instantly changed to a mere 60 feet per round (equivalent to the end of a fall from a few feet), with no damage incurred upon landing while the power is in effect. However, when the duration expires, a normal rate of fall occurs.
　　You can manifest this power instantly, quickly enough to save yourself if you unexpectedly fall. Manifesting the power is a free action, like manifesting a quickened power, and it counts toward the normal limit of one quickened power per round.
　　This power has no special effect on ranged weapons unless they are falling quite a distance. If manifested on a falling item, such as a boulder dropped from the top of a castle wall, the item does half normal damage based on weight (1d6 per 400 pounds) with no bonus for the height of the drop.
　　The power works only upon free-falling objects. It does not affect a sword blow or a charging or flying creature.
　
感光术(Feel Light)
　　心灵自塑系(力量)
　　等级：心灵术士1、心灵武士1
　　异象：物质
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：个人
　　目标：自己
　　持续时间：10分钟/等级 (解消)
　　灵能点：1
　　你能够透过触觉（触到）感受光。你的整个身体都变为视觉器官。换句话说，你的身体代替了你的眼睛。你能“看见”通常你的眼睛能够看见的事物。你的视野范围没有变化，但如果你有黑暗视觉，“感光术”不会把此视觉转变为触觉。
　　如果你的视力正常，扩展後的视觉给予你的“搜索”和“侦察”技能+1增强加值。如果本异能与“听光术”共用，则增强加值为+2。
　
Feel Light
　　Psychometabolism (Str)
　　Level: Psion 1/Psychic Warrior 1
　　Display: Ma
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: Personal
　　Target: You
　　Duration: 10 minutes/level (D)
　　Power Points: 1
　　You experience light translated through tactile sensation (by touch). Your entire body becomes a receiver for light. In effect, your body replaces your eyes. You can “see” what your eyes would normally reveal. Your field of vision does not change, but if you have darkvision, sight is not translated to touch via feel light.
　　If your eyes are working normally, the expanded view gives you a +1 enhancement bonus on all Spot and Search checks. If this power is used in conjunction with hear light, the bonus is +2.
　
感声术(Feel Sound)
　　心灵自塑系(力量)
　　等级：心灵术士1、心灵武士1
　　异象：物质
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：个人
　　目标：自己
　　持续时间：10分钟/等级 (解消)
　　灵能点：1
　　如同“感光术”，但你透过触觉（触到）听到声音。你的整个身体都变为听觉器官。换句话说，你的身体代替了你的耳朵。你能“听见”通常你的耳朵能够听见的事物。你的听力范围没有变化。
　　如果你的耳朵正常，扩展後的听觉给予你的“聆听”技能+1增强加值。如果本异能与“观声术”共用，则增强加值为+2。
　
Feel Sound
　　Psychometabolism (Str)
　　Level: Psion 1/Psychic Warrior 1
　　Display: Ma
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: Personal
　　Target: You
　　Duration: 10 minutes/level (D)
　　Power Points: 1
　　As feel light, except you experience sound translated through tactile sensation (by touch). Your entire body becomes a receiver for sound. In effect, your body replaces your ears. You can “hear” what your ears would normally reveal. Your range of hearing does not change.
　　If your ears are working normally, the expanded reception gives you a +1 enhancement bonus on all Listen checks. If this power is used in conjunction with see sound, the bonus is +2.
　
燃烧一指(Finger of Fire)
　　心灵创造系(智力)[火焰]
　　等级：心灵术士0
　　异象：视觉 (见说明)
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：近距 (25+5/2等级)
　　效果：射线
　　持续时间：立即
　　豁免检定：无
　　异能抗力：可
　　灵能点：1
　　一道不稳定的燃着的星质射线从你的指尖射出，你必须通过远程接触攻击检定来使射线对目标造成伤害。此射线造成1d3点火焰伤害。
　
Finger of Fire
　　Metacreativity (Int) [Fire]
　　Level: Psion 0
　　Display: Vi (see text)
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: Close (25 ft. + 5 ft./2 levels)
　　Effect: Ray
　　Duration: Instantaneous
　　Saving Throw: None
　　Power Resistance: Yes
　　Power Points: 1
　　A ray of unstable, burning ectoplasm projects from your pointing finger. You must succeed at a ranged touch attack with the ray to deal damage to a target. The ray deals 1d3 points of fire damage.
　
落炎术(Firefall)
　　心灵创造系(智力)[火焰]
　　等级：心灵术士1
　　异象：视觉 (见说明)
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：20
　　区域：半径10盏谋发范围
　　持续时间：立即
　　豁免检定：反射，通过则效果减半
　　异能抗力：可
　　灵能点：1
　　不稳定的星质微粒忽然爆炸，在你指定的范围内爆开。在此范围内的所有生物都受到1d4点火焰伤害。易燃材料如布料，纸张，羊皮纸，薄木板等等，在被火焰接触到的时候会燃着。人物可以用一个全回合动作熄灭燃烧物上的火。
　
Firefall
　　Metacreativity (Int) [Fire]
　　Level: Psion 1
　　Display: Vi (see text)
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: 20 ft.
　　Area: 10-ft. radius burst
　　Duration: Instantaneous
　　Saving Throw: Reflex half
　　Power Resistance: Yes
　　Power Points: 1
　　Motes of unstable ectoplasm flare and dissipate explosively within the area you designate. Any creature in the area takes 1d4 points of fire damage. Flammable materials such as cloth, paper, parchment, thin wood, and so on, burn if the flames touch them. A character can extinguish burning items as a full-round action.
　
分身术(Fission)
　　心灵自塑系(力量)
　　等级：心灵术士7
　　异象：嗅觉
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：个人
　　目标：自己
　　持续时间：1轮/等级 (解消)
　　灵能点：13
　　你能够把自己分开，在5站嗬肽诖丛煲桓龈北尽Ｄ愀北镜乃嘉和举止和你完全一样，并听从你的命令，尽管它不会去做你不愿自己去做的事情。你的副本具有你的属性但没有任何装备。你的副本拥有与你相同的生命值，你一半（扣除本异能的费用之後再行计算）的灵能点数，以及你在展现此异能时所有的其他的身体特征。异能、法术或其他影响你的效果并不影响到你的副本。
　　当异能效果结束或你解除这个异能，你与你的副本重新聚合，无论你们相距多远。聚合时你受到你的副本所受伤害的一半。这有可能把你的生命值降至0或者更低，但这不会把你的生命值降至-10或更少。同样，你失去你的副本所用去的灵能点数的一半。如果其中一个你在异能结束前死亡，那么将不发生聚合；然而你（无论是本体还是副本）获得一个负向等级。
　
Fission
　　Psychometabolism (Str)
　　Level: Psion 7
　　Display: Ol
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: Personal
　　Target: You
　　Duration: 1 round/level (D)
　　Power Points: 13
　　You can divide yourself, creating a duplicate up to 5 feet away. Your duplicate thinks and acts exactly as you do and follows your orders, although it will not do anything you wouldn’t do yourself. Your duplicate has all your abilities but none of your equipment. Your duplicate has all your hit points, half your power points (figured after you deduct the cost of this power), and other physical traits you had at the time you manifested the power. Powers, spells, or other effects affecting you do not affect your duplicate.
　　When the duration expires or when you dismiss the power, you and your duplicate rejoin, no matter how far from each other you are. You take half of the damage your duplicate has suffered at the time of rejoining. This could potentially put you at 0 hit points or lower, but it can’t bring you to -10 hit points or less. Also, you lose half of the power points your duplicate used up. If one of you dies before the duration expires, there is no rejoining; however, you (either in your original flesh or that of your duplicate) gain one negative level.
　
烈焰帷幕(Flaming Shroud)
　　心灵创造系(智力)
　　等级：心灵术士6
　　异象：物质 (见说明)
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：中距 (100+10/等级)
　　目标：一个体型不超过大型的生物
　　持续时间：立即
　　豁免检定：反射，通过则无效
　　异能抗力：可
　　灵能点：11
　　你从星界抽出扭动的丝把受术者绑缚在地狱般的火幕中。如果目标未通过敏捷豁免检定，则会受到11d6点火焰伤害。
　
Flaming Shroud
　　Metacreativity (Int)
　　Level: Psion 6
　　Display: Ma (see text)
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: Medium (100 ft. + 10 ft./level)
　　Target: One creature of Large size or smaller
　　Duration: Instantaneous
　　Saving Throw: Reflex negates
　　Power Resistance: Yes
　　Power Points: 11
　　You draw writhing strands of unstable ectoplasm from the Astral Plane and wrap the subject in a shroud of hellish fire. If the target fails its Reflex save, it suffers 11d6 points of fire damage.
　
漂浮术(Float)
　　心灵传送系(敏捷)
　　等级：心灵术士0、心灵武士0
　　异象：听觉
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：近距 (25+5/2等级)
　　目标群：任何重量不超过300磅/等级的物体或生物
　　持续时间：专注
　　豁免检定：无
　　异能抗力：不可
　　灵能点：1
　　你可以用精神力支撑一个在附近的水或类似液体中的生物或物体。你无法移动漂浮物，但如果本异能的受术者是活物，他可以不用担心沉没（或溺死，如果受术者不擅长游泳）地在水中移动。一旦受术者与显能者的距离超过异能有效距离，则本异能结束。
　
Float
　　Psychoportation (Dex)
　　Level: Psion 0/Psychic Warrior 0
　　Display: Au
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: Close (25 ft. + 5 ft./2 levels)
　　Targets: Any object or creature whose weight does not total more than 300 lb./level
　　Duration: Concentration
　　Saving Throw: None
　　Power Resistance: No
　　Power Points: 1
　　You can mentally support one creature or object in water or similar liquid at will from a distance. You cannot move the floating object, but if the subject of the power is animate, it can move through the water without fear of submerging (or drowning, if an unskilled swimmer). The power ends if the distance between you and the subject ever exceeds the power’s range.
　
飞行术(Fly)
　　心灵传送系(敏捷)
　　等级：心灵术士3
　　异象：视觉
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：接触
　　目标：接触到的生物
　　持续时间：10分钟/等级
　　豁免检定：无
　　异能抗力：可 (无害)
　　灵能点：5
　　受术者可以以90盏乃俣确尚校ㄈ绻穿着中甲或重甲则只能以60账俣确尚校。他能以一半速度上升，或者以两倍速度下降。他的机动性为良好。使用“飞行术”飞行的专注程度与行走相同，所以受术者可以正常攻击或显能。受术者可以冲刺但不能奔跑。物品加上防具负重不能超过最大负重限制（参见《玩家手册》第九章）。
　　超过持续时间後，若受术者仍在空中，灵能效果会渐渐消失。受术者会先以60/轮的速度下降1d6轮。如果在这段时间内落地则算平安降落。如果没有落地，剩下高度就会自由落下。（每10赵斐1d6摔伤）。如果“飞行术”被某种消解灵能的方式所解除，受术者将立即跌落{Andor注:这点和对应法术不同}。
　
Fly
　　Psychoportation (Dex)
　　Level: Psion 3
　　Display: Vi
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: Touch
　　Target: Creature touched
　　Duration: 10 minutes/level
　　Saving Throw: None
　　Power Resistance: Yes (harmless)
　　Power Points: 5
　　The power’s subject can fly at a speed of 90 feet (60 feet if the creature wears medium or heavy armor). The subject can fly up at half speed and descend at double speed. The flying subject’s maneuverability is good. Using the fly power requires as much concentration as walking, so the subject can attack or manifest powers normally. The subject of fly can charge but not run, and it cannot carry aloft more weight than its maximum load (see Chapter 9 of the Player’s Handbook), plus any armor it wears.
　　Should the duration expire while the subject is still aloft, the psionic effect fails slowly. The subject drops 60 feet per round for 1d6 rounds. If it reaches the ground in this time, it is safe. If not, it falls the rest of the distance (falling damage is 1d6 per 10 feet of fall). Since negating a power effectively ends it, the subject falls immediately if fly is negated.
　
强制连心术(Forced Mindlink)
　　心灵附魔系(魅力)
　　等级：心灵术士4
　　豁免检定：意志，通过则无效
　　异能抗力：可
　　灵能点：7
　　如同“次级连心术”，但你可以尝试与不情愿的生物建立心灵链接。不过即使你成功的与不情愿的生物建立了心灵链接，它也可以选择不通过心灵链接对你“说话”。
　
Forced Mindlink
　　Telepathy (Cha)
　　Level: Psion 4
　　Saving Throw: Will negates
　　Power Resistance: Yes
　　Power Points: 7
　　As lesser mindlink, except you can attempt to create a telepathic bond with a creature who is not willing. Even if you create a bond with an unwilling creature, it can still decide not to “speak” with you through the telepathic bond.
　
预警术(Foresight)
　　心灵预言系(感知)
　　等级：心灵术士8
　　异象：视觉、物质
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：个人 或 接触
　　目标：见说明
　　持续时间：10分钟/等级
　　豁免检定：无 或 意志，通过则无效 (见说明)
　　异能抗力：不可 或 可 (无害)
　　灵能点：15
　　你获得关于自己或他人的强大第六感。当异能展现後，只要有人想危害受术者，你就会立刻警觉。因此，如果本异能目标是自己，如果有游荡者企图偷袭你，或有生物将从你没注意到的方向跳出，或有攻击者正用异能、法术或远程武器瞄准你，你都会事先警觉。你不会被突袭或措手不及。此外，本异能可使你以直觉行动保护自己――弯腰、向右跳、闭眼等等――并给你的AC和反射豁免以+2洞察加值。只要你失去对AC的敏捷加值，你就失去该洞察加值。
　　当异能目标是其他生物时，你会得到关于该生物的警报。你必须与之沟通才能传达有用的警报，否则他可能在无预警的情况下中埋伏。你得到警报後，及时大声警告、将他拉住，甚至心灵感应沟通（通过相应异能），都可以达到预警目的。然而，目标并无AC或反射检定的洞察加值。
　
Foresight
　　Clairsentience (Wis)
　　Level: Psion 8
　　Display: Vi, Ma
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: Personal or touch
　　Target: See text
　　Duration: 10 minutes/level
　　Saving Throw: None or Will negates (see text)
　　Power Resistance: No or Yes (harmless)
　　Power Points: 15
　　You gain a powerful sixth sense in relation to yourself or another. Once the power is manifested, you receive instantaneous warnings of impending danger or harm to the subject of the power. Thus, if you are the subject of the power you would be warned in advance if a rogue were about to attempt a sneak attack on you, or if a creature were about to leap out from an unexpected direction, or if an attacker were specifically targeting you with a power, spell, or ranged weapon. You are never surprised or flat-footed. In addition, the power gives you a general idea of what action you might take to best protect yourself―duck, jump right, close your eyes, and so on―and gives you a +2 insight bonus to AC and Reflex saves. This insight bonus is lost whenever you would lose a Dexterity bonus to AC.
　　When another creature is the object of the power, you receive warnings about that creature. You must communicate what you learn to the other creature for the warning to be useful, and it can be caught unprepared in the absence of such a warning. Shouting a warning, yanking a person back, and even telepathically communicating (via an appropriate power) can all be accomplished before some danger befalls me power’s subject, provided you act on the warning without delay. The subject, however, does not gain the insight bonus to AC or Reflex saves.
　
行动自如(Freedom of Movement)
　　心灵传送系(敏捷)
　　等级：心灵术士4
　　异象：听觉
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：个人 或 接触
　　目标：自己 或 接触到的生物
　　持续时间：10分钟/等级
　　豁免检定：无
　　异能抗力：不可 或 可 (无害)
　　灵能点：7
　　即使处于妨碍行动的灵能（例如“星质茧”）的影响下，你或你碰触的受术者仍然能正常移动和攻击。
　　本异能同样可以令受术者在水中如常移动和攻击，只要武器是手持挥舞而非投掷的，无论是挥砍武器（比如斧和剑）或钝击武器（比如链枷、战锤和硬头锤）都可如常进行攻击。但是，本异能并不能使受术者得到水下呼吸的能力，受术者需要从其他的灵能中得到这个能力。
　
Freedom of Movement
　　Psychoportation (Dex)
　　Level: Psion 4
　　Display: Au
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: Personal or touch
　　Target: You or creature touched
　　Duration: 10 minutes/level
　　Saving Throw: None
　　Power Resistance: No or Yes (harmless)
　　Power Points: 7
　　This power enables you or the creature you touch to move and attack normally for the duration of the power, even under the influence of psionics that usually impedes movement, such as ectoplasmic cocoon.
　　The power also allows a character to move and attack normally while underwater, even with cutting weapons such as axes and swords and with smashing weapons such as flails, hammers, and maces, provided that the weapon is wielded in the hand rather than hurled. The power does not, however, allow water breathing without further appropriate psionic adaptation.
异能详述-G、H、I字头系列
 起源术(Genesis)
　　心灵创造系(智力)
　　等级：心灵术士9
　　异象：物质
　　显能时间：1周 (每天8小时)
　　距离：10瞻刖/等级 (见说明)
　　效果：见说明
　　持续时间：立即
　　豁免检定：无
　　异能抗力：不可
　　灵能点：17
　　你创造出一个出入受限的有限位面：一个半位面。被本异能创造的半位面是非常小的非常不成熟的位面。
　　本异能应在以太位面或星界展现。展现本异能後，你所在位置的密度将迅速增加直至生成这个半位面的起始点。最初，新生的位面以每天1瞻刖兜乃俣仍龀ぶ撩肯阅苷叩燃10瞻刖兜某跏即笮。这被看作是它极快的汲取周围的以太虚体或者星质。新建的半位面达到它的最大尺寸後，它并不真的停止增长，但它的增长速度锐减至每星期1/2及刖叮每年只有两斩啵。
　　半位面内部的环境由显能者在显能时确定，反映出显能者所能想象的最强的愿望，只要DM允许（尽管半位面内的环境效果无法复制高于三级异能的效果）。固体地面、水、空气以及温度等要素也必须由显能者决定。本异能无法创造生命，也无法创造诸如房屋、道路、井、地城等建筑物。这些个别部分必须以其他方式引入半位面。所有以“起源术”创造的半位面都与星界和以太位面相连。
　　反起源术：“起源术”可以在普通的位面和半位面展现，但只有最变态或最邪恶的创形者会考虑这样做。如果“起源术”被展现在普通的位面或半位面内，本异能按照上述的速度产生效果；然则，新位面的能量将精确地被原位面的能量抵消掉，在原位面造成一个像毒瘤一样不断扩大的死区。死区不断扩张的边界彻底的抹去所有的构造，粉碎正常的地形并且蒸发水源。留下一片毫无生气的灰土之原。穿过死区边界的生物并不受到直接伤害，但植物无法从死区的灰土中找到养分，水生生物在水变为灰土时死得比植物更快，走兽明白需要立即离开这个区域。一个“反起源术”将在10d100年後消散，或者被另一个“起源术”抵消。
　
Genesis
　　Metacreativity (Int)
　　Level: Psion 9
　　Display: Ma
　　Manifestation Time: 1 week (8 hours/day)
　　Range: 10-ft. radius/level (see text)
　　Effect: See text
　　Duration: Instantaneous
　　Saving Throw: None
　　Power Resistance: No
　　Power Points: 17
　　You create a finite plane with limited access: a demiplane. Demiplanes created by this power are very small, very minor planes.
　　This power should be manifested only while you are on the Ethereal or Astral Plane. Manifestation of the power creates a local density fluctuation that precipitates the creation of a demiplane. At first, the fledgling plane grows at a rate of 1 foot in radius per day to an initial maximum radius of 10 feet per manifester level as it rapidly draws substance from surrounding ethereal vapors and protomatter or astral ectoplasm. Once the new demiplane reaches its maximum size, it doesn’t really stop growing, but its growth rate decreases dramatically to only 1/2 inch in radius per week (just over 2 feet per year).
　　The environment within the demiplane is determined by the manifester when genesis is first manifested, reflecting most any desire the psion can visualize, as long as the DM approves (although no environmental effect within the plane can duplicate effects greater than those of 3rd-level powers). Factors such as solid ground, air, water, and temperature must be determined by the manifester. This power cannot create life, nor can it create construction such as buildings, roads, wells, dungeons, and so forth; such particulars must be introduced to the demiplane in some other fashion. All demiplanes created with genesis are in contact with the Astral and Ethereal Planes.
　　Antigenesis: It is possible to manifest genesis on normal planes and demiplanes, but only the most perverse or evil shaper would consider doing so. If genesis is manifested within a normal plane or demiplane, the power takes effect according to the speed noted above; however, the energies of the new plane are exactly canceled by the energies of the original plane, creating a growing dead spot like a cancer on the original plane. The expanding boundary of the dead spot utterly wipes away all construction, crumbles natural land forms, and evaporates water, leaving behind a uniformly level plain of inert dust. Living things that pass the boundary of the growing dead spot are not directly harmed. But plants can find no sustenance in the dust of the dead spot, marine creatures die even more quickly when water turns to dust, and mobile animals know enough to leave the area alone. An antigenesis wave dies out after 100d10 years, or can be canceled by yet another manifestation of genesis.
　
滑翔术(Glide)
　　心灵传送系(敏捷)
　　等级：心灵术士2
　　异象：视觉
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：接触
　　目标：接触到的生物
　　持续时间：1分钟/等级
　　豁免检定：无
　　异能抗力：可 (无害)
　　灵能点：3
　　本异能的受术者能在空中以20眨ㄈ绻穿着中甲或重甲则为10眨┑乃俣然翔。受术者只能以5盏乃俣认蛏戏尚械可以以50账俣雀┏濉；翔中的受术者的机动性为不良。使用“滑翔术”飞行的专注程度与奔跑相同，所以受术者无法正常攻击或显能。受术者所带物品加上防具负重不能超过中载限制（参见《玩家手册》第九章）。
　　持续时间结束後，若受术者仍在空中，灵能效果会渐渐消失。受术者会先以60/轮的速度下降1d6轮。如果在这段时间内落地则算平安降落。如果没有落地，剩下高度就会自由落下。（每10赵斐1d6摔伤）。如果“滑翔术”被某种消解灵能的方式所解除，受术者将立即跌落。
　
Glide
　　Psychoportation (Dex)
　　Level: Psion 2
　　Display: Vi
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: Touch
　　Target: Creature touched
　　Duration: 1 minute/level
　　Saving Throw: None
　　Power Resistance: Yes (harmless)
　　Power Points: 3
　　The power’s subject can glide through the air with a speed of 20 feet (10 feet if the creature wears medium or heavy armor). The subject can only fly upward at a speed of 5 feet but may descend at a speed of 50 feet. The gliding subject’s maneuverability is poor. Using the glide power requires as much concentration as running, so the subject cannot attack or manifest powers normally. The subject of glide cannot carry aloft more weight than its medium load carrying capacity (see Chapter 9 of the Player’s Handbook), plus any armor it wears.
　　Should the duration expire while the subject is still aloft, the psionic effect fails slowly. The subject drops 50 feet per round for 1d6 rounds. If it reaches the ground in that time, it is safe. If not, it falls the rest of the distance (falling damage is 1d6 per 10 feet of fall). Since negating a power effectively ends it, the subject falls immediately if glide is negated.
　
武器嫁接(Graft Weapon)
　　心灵自塑系(力量)
　　等级：心灵术士5、心灵武士5
　　异象：嗅觉
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：个人
　　目标：自己
　　持续时间：立即
　　灵能点：9
　　你将一把武器任何种类的武器（普通的、附魔的或者灵能的）永久的接在你的一只胳臂前端。这把武器从此成为你胳臂的一部分，而手则消失不见。如果你擅长此武器，你在使用此武器的时候攻击检定和伤害检定得到+1加值（这项加值与所有其他加值累加，包括“专攻武器”与“武器专精”提供的）。被嫁接的武器能受一些通常不会影响装备的异能，例如“膨胀术”。更重要的，由于武器成为你身体的一部分，通常只能增强你徒手攻击的异能现在也可以用于被嫁接的武器（例如“锤击术”、“手刀”甚至是“腐蚀之触”）。
　　但是，你失去了一只可用的手，因此你的所有用到手的技能将受到-2能力减值。暂时将你（或者仅仅是你的手）变形或者变化的异能可以不改变嫁接的武器或将其正常改变，这由你来决定。如果武器受到伤害，你也受到伤害。如果你被治疗，嫁接的武器也得到治疗。如果你的武器被毁，你会失去两点体质，直到你嫁接另一把武器或者恢复你原有的组织结构（见下文）。
　　你可以通过再次施展本异能来重新得到你的双手。如果你空手施展本异能，便会恢复你原有的身体结构（但是你无法通过本异能来恢复由其他不幸导致的肢体残损）。
　
Graft Weapon
　　Psychometabolism (Str)
　　Level: Psion 5/Psychic Warrior 5
　　Display: Ol
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: Personal
　　Target: You
　　Duration: Instantaneous
　　Power Points: 9
　　You permanently attach any weapon― mundane, psionic, or magical―onto the end of one of your arms. The weapon becomes a natural extension of your arm, and that hand is nowhere to be seen. If you are proficient with the weapon, you add +1 to all attack and damage rolls while using the weapon (this stacks with all other bonuses, including those granted by Weapon Focus and Weapon Specialization). The grafted weapon becomes subject to powers that normally do not effect equipment, such as expansion. More importantly, since the weapon is a natural part of your body, powers that normally only enhance unarmed attacks and touch attacks now apply to your grafted weapon (such as hammer, duodimensional hand, or even dissolving touch).
　　However, you lose the use of one hand and receive a -2 competence penalty on all skill checks requiring the use of hands. Powers that temporarily polymorph or metamorphose you (or just your hands) can ignore the grafted weapon or alter it normally, at your discretion. If the weapon takes damage, you take the damage as well. If you are healed, so is your grafted weapon. If your weapon is destroyed, you lose 2 points of Constitution; the ability damage persists until you can graft another weapon or restore your natural anatomy (see below).
　　You can change out weapons by using this power again. If you manifest this power without any weapon, your natural anatomy returns (but you can’t use this power to recover a limb lost through some other mishap).
　
油腻术(Grease)
　　心灵创造系(智力)
　　等级：心灵术士1
　　异象：嗅觉
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：近距 (25+5/2等级)
　　目标或区域：单一物体 或 10铡10盏那域
　　持续时间：1轮/等级 (解消)
　　豁免检定：见说明
　　异能抗力：不可
　　灵能点：1
　　异能“油腻术”可使平面附上一层滑溜的油脂。任何进入或陷入此区域的生物，都必须进行反射检定，失败者会打滑，滑行或滑倒。通过检定者可在此平面上半速移动，但每一轮都必须再进行反射检定，以决定是否能够移动或滑倒。DM应视情况调整豁免检定值。
　　本异能也可以在物体表面创造一个滑溜的覆膜，例如针对绳索，阶梯或武器把手。
　　目标物品只要不是正被人使用，异能便一定成功。但若正被人装备或持有，则该生物需要进行反射检定，检定失败的物品将立刻从该生物身上滑落。若该生物试图捡起或使用此物品，则每轮都要进行反射检定。
　
Grease
　　Metacreativity (Int)
　　Level: Psion 1
　　Display: Ol
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: Close (25 ft. + 5 ft./2 levels)
　　Target or Area: One object or a 10-ft. x 10-ft. square
　　Duration: 1 round/level (D)
　　Saving Throw: See text
　　Power Resistance: No
　　Power Points: 1
　　A grease power covers a solid surface with a layer of slippery grease. Any creature entering the area or caught in it when the power is manifested must make a successful Reflex save or slip, skid, and fall. Those who successfully save can move at half speed across the surface. However, those who remain in the area must each make a new saving throw each round to avoid falling and to be able to move. The DM should adjust saving throws by circumstance.
　　The power can also be used to create a greasy coating on an item―a rope, ladder rungs, weapon handle, and so on.
　　Material objects not in use are always affected by this power, while objects wielded or employed by creatures receive a Reflex save to avoid the effect. If the initial saving throw fails, the creature immediately drops the item. A saving throw must be made each round the creature attempts to pick up or use the greased item.
　
高等生物电流(Greater Biocurrent)
　　心灵转化系(体质)
　　等级：心灵术士6
　　目标：四个相距不超过15盏幕钗
　　灵能点：11
　　如同“生物电流”，但每轮对满足条件的目标造成6d6点电击伤害。电流除了主要目标外还会弧击开始时在主要目标15漳诘模或者在异能持续期内进入主要目标15漳诘娜个额外敌人。次要敌人在持续期内也受到每轮6d6点电击伤害。如果主要或次要敌人生命值降到0以下，仍在持续期内的“高等生物电流”会随机选定新的主要和次要敌人予以电击。目标敌人每轮都可以移动或通过豁免检定使伤害减半（仅针对当轮），但只要他们待在异能有效距离内就会持续受到影响。
　
Greater Biocurrent
　　Psychokinesis (Con)
　　Level: Psion 6
　　Target: Any four living creatures that are no more than 15 ft. apart
　　Power Points: 11
　　As bicurrent except you deal 6d6 points of electricity damage per round you meet the requirements. Electricity also arcs off the primary target to strike three additional foes initially within 15 feet of the primary foe, or who subsequently move within 15 feet of the primary foe while the duration lasts. Secondary foes also take 6d6 points of damage per round the duration lasts. Should any of the primary or secondary foes fall to below 0 hit points, greater biocurrent’s electrical arc randomly retargets another primary and other secondary foes while the duration continues. Targeted foes may move or make a saving throw each round for half damage (on that round only), but as long as they remain in range, they continue to be affected.
　
高等冲击波(Greater Concussion)
　　心灵转化系(体质)
　　等级：心灵术士3
　　灵能点：5
　　如同“冲击波”，但“高等冲击波”造成5d6点伤害。你可以选择让本异能造成淤伤而非正常伤害。
　
Greater Concussion
　　Psychokinesis (Con)
　　Level: Psion 3
　　Power Points: 5
　　As concussion, except greater concussion deals 5d6 points of damage. You may choose to have the power deal an equal amount of subdual damage instead.
　
高等支配术(Greater Domination)
　　心灵附魔系(魅力)[胁迫、影响心灵]
　　等级：心灵术士5
　　灵能点：9
　　如同“支配术”，但你可以控制一个没有共通语言的受术者。
　
Greater Domination
　　Telepathy (Cha) [Compulsion, Mind-Affecting]
　　Level: Psion 5
　　Power Points: 9
　　As domination, except you can control a subject with whom you do not share a common language.
　
高等异能仿效(Greater Emulation)
　　心灵预言系(感知)
　　等级：心灵术士9
　　异象：物质
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：见说明
　　目标、效果或区域：见说明
　　持续时间：见说明
　　豁免检定：无
　　异能抗力：可
　　灵能点：17，消耗经验值
　　如同“异能仿效”，但你能选择任何一道不超过八级的其他异能，不论能系或者是否已知。
　　经验值费用：5000点经验值和被仿效异能所需经验值中的较高者。
　
Greater Emulation
　　Clairsentience (Wis)
　　Level: Psion 9
　　Display: Ma
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: See text
　　Target, Effect, or Area: See text
　　Duration: See text
　　Saving Throw: None
　　Power Resistance: Yes
　　Power Points: 17, XP cost
　　As emulate power, except that you can duplicate the effect of any other power, regardless of its discipline or whether you know the power, of 8th level or lower.
　　XP Cost: 5,000 XP or the XP requirement of the emulated power, whichever is greater.
　
锤击术(Hammer)
　　心灵自塑系(力量)
　　等级：心灵术士1
　　异象：听觉、物质
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：接触
　　目标：接触到的生物或物体
　　持续时间：能量散发
　　豁免检定：无
　　异能抗力：可 (物体)
　　灵能点：1
　　本异能给予你的接触以重锤下击的力量。一次成功的近战接触攻击检定将造成1d8点钝击伤害。被灵能强化的接触攻击被视为武装攻击。
　
Hammer
　　Psychometabolism (Str)
　　Level: Psion 1
　　Display: Au, Ma
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: Touch
　　Target: Creature or object touched
　　Duration: Until discharged
　　Saving Throw: None
　　Power Resistance: Yes (object)
　　Power Points: 1
　　This power charges your mere touch with the force of a sledgehammer. A successful melee touch attack deals 1d8 points of bludgeoning damage. Your touch attack, charged with a psionic power, is treated as an armed attack.
　
听光术(Hear Light)
　　心灵自塑系(力量)
　　等级：心灵术士1、心灵武士1
　　异象：物质
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：个人
　　目标：自己
　　持续时间：10分钟/等级 (解消)
　　灵能点：1
　　如同“感光术”，但你能够透过听觉（听到）感受光。你能够用你的耳朵去“看到”光，因为到达你耳朵的光将被转化成声音，于是你“听到”了影像。你能“看见”通常你的眼睛能够看见的事物，但如果你有黑暗视觉，“感光术”不会把此视觉转变为触觉。
　　如果你的视力正常，扩展後的视觉给予你的“搜索”和“侦察”技能+1增强加值。如果本异能与“感光术”共用，则增强加值为+2。
　
Hear Light
　　Psychometabolism (Str)
　　Level: Psion 1/Psychic Warrior 1
　　Display: Ma
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: Personal
　　Target: You
　　Duration: 10 minutes/level (D)
　　Power Points: 1
　　As feel light, except you experience light translated through auditory sensation (by hearing). You can “see” with your ears because any light waves that reach you are converted to sound, and you “hear” the image. You can see what your eyes would normally reveal, but if you have darkvision, sight is not translated to sound via hear light.
　　If your eyes are working normally, the expanded view gives you a +1 enhancement bonus on all Spot and Search checks. If this power is used in conjunction with feel light, the bonus is +2.
　
急速术(Hustle)
　　心灵自塑系(力量)
　　等级：心灵武士1
　　异象：听觉
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：个人
　　目标：自己
　　效果：一个额外的部分动作
　　灵能点：1
　　在你的下个回合，你可以多做一个部分动作。也就是说，你放弃施展本异能的回合的标准动作，并在下一回合得到一个额外的部分动作。这视作增强加值。
　
Hustle
　　Psychometabolism (Str)
　　Level: Psychic Warrior 1
　　Display: Au
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: Personal
　　Target: You
　　Effect: 1 extra partial action
　　Power Points: 1
　　You can take an extra partial action, but you must wait until your next round’s worth of actions to do so. In effect, you give up a standard action on the round you manifest this power, but gain an extra partial action on the following round. This benefit counts as an enhancement bonus.
　
极化认知(Hypercognition)
　　心灵预言系(感知) 以及
　　心灵自塑系(力量)
　　等级：心灵术士8
　　异象：精神
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：个人
　　目标：自己
　　持续时间：立即
　　豁免检定：无
　　异能抗力：不可
　　灵能点：15
　　你根据头脑中最细小的线索，模型或记忆的片断作出闪电般的推理。你可以从非常少的认识出发，得到关于一个人、地点或物件的合理推论。不过，这实际上是你强迫你的心智深入发掘每一条与此相关的信息（甚至可能是从星界汲取的信息）并使之建立关联，完成极其严谨的逻辑推理过程後得到的结果。
　　你所得到的关于分析目标的知识由DM来决定，它可能包含一个谜语的答案、一个迷宫的出口、关于某个人的一小段信息、一个地点或物件的传奇，或者甚至是你的意识层面根本无法理解的一道难题的结论。
　　DM可能会要求你通过一个智力检定来得到你想要的信息（由DM暗中确定DC）。由“极化认知”协助作出的智力检定得到+30加值。
　
Hypercognition
　　Clairsentience (Wis); and
　　Psychometabolism (Str)
　　Level: Psion 8
　　Display: Me
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: Personal
　　Target: You
　　Duration: Instantaneous
　　Saving Throw: None
　　Power Resistance: No
　　Power Points: 15
　　You make lightning-fast deductions based on only the slightest clue, pattern, or scrap of memory resident in your mind. You can make reasonable statements about a person, place, or object, seemingly from very little knowledge. However, it is in fact the result of a rigorously logical process you forced your mind to undertake, digging up and correlating every possible piece of knowledge bearing on the topic (possibly even extracting echoes from the Astral Plane).
　　The nature of the knowledge you gain concerning the subject of your analysis is subject to your DM’s discretion but might include the answer to a riddle, the way out of a maze, stray bits of information about a person, legends about a place or object, or even a conclusion concerning a dilemma that your conscious mind is unable to produce.
　　Your DM may ask for an Intelligence check to receive the desired information (DM secretly determines the DC). Intelligence checks made with the aid of hypercognition have a +30 bonus.
　
鉴定术(Identify)
　　心灵预言系(感知)
　　等级：心灵术士1
　　异象：精神、物质
　　显能时间：8小时
　　距离：接触
　　目标：接触到的至多每等级一个物体
　　持续时间：立即
　　豁免检定：无
　　异能抗力：不可
　　灵能点：1
　　本异能能确定灵能物品的最基本的一项功能，包括如何启动该功能（如果需要的话）以及还剩多少发（如果有的话）。
　　如果灵能物品有多个基本功能，“鉴定术”将确定最低级的功能。如果多个功能等级相同，DM随机决定鉴定出哪个。
　
Identify
　　Clairsentience (Wis)
　　Level: Psion 1
　　Display: Me, Ma
　　Manifestation Time: 8 hours
　　Range: Touch
　　Target: Up to 1 touched object per level
　　Duration: Instantaneous
　　Saving Throw: None
　　Power Resistance: No
　　Power Points: 1
　　This power determines the single most basic function of a psionic item, including how to activate that function (if appropriate), and how many charges are left (if any).
　　If a psionic item has multiple different functions that are equally basic, identify determines the lowest-level function. If these functions are also of equal level, the DM decides randomly which is identified.
　
固定术(Immovability)
　　心灵自塑系(力量)
　　等级：心灵术士4、心灵武士4
　　异象：视觉
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：个人
　　目标：自己
　　持续时间：1小时/等级 (解消)
　　灵能点：7
　　你几乎无法移动。这并不是由于你重量的改变，而是你用意志力把自己紧贴在所处的位面结构上。因此，你甚至能够令人难以置信将自己定在半空。你在对抗任何尝试移动你的力量检定中得到三倍于你的显能者等级的加值。因此，8级时你对抗移动的加值为+24。一旦被固定，你便无法移动到新的位置，除非你先解消本异能或等到持续时间结束。
　　在固定时，你失去AC的敏捷加值。你也不能进行攻击或者其他动作。不过，被固定的身体得到伤害减免20/+3。
　
Immovability
　　Psychometabolism (Str)
　　Level: Psion 4/Psychic Warrior 4
　　Display: Vi
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: Personal
　　Target: You
　　Duration: 1 hour/level (D)
　　Power Points: 7
　　You are almost impossible to move. Your weight does not vary; instead, you mentally attach yourself to the underlying fabric of the plane. Thus, you could conceivably anchor yourself in midair. You oppose any attempt to move you by a Strength check modified by a bonus equal to three times your manifester level Thus, at 8th level, your bonus to resist being moved is +24. Once immovable, you can’t move to a new location unless you first dismiss the power or its duration expires.
　　While you are immovable, you lose all Dexterity bonuses to AC. Neither can you attack or make any other movement. However, your anchored body gains damage reduction 20/+3.
　
高等导航术(Improved Anchored Navigation)
　　心灵预言系(感知)
　　等级：心灵术士7
　　持续时间：1天/等级
　　灵能点：13
　　如同“导航术”，但本异能的效果能越过所有位面的边界，并且对心灵传送系所有异能都有用（并且只需被使用的旅行方法的最短时间）。
　
Improved Anchored Navigation
　　Clairsentience (Wis)
　　Level: Psion 7
　　Duration: 1 day/level
　　Power Points: 13
　　As anchored navigation, except the effect of the power extends across all planar boundaries, and it is useful for all psychoportation powers (and in the minimum time for the method of travel utilized).
　
高等生物反馈(Improved Biofeedback)

Improved Biofeedback

　　Duration: 1 hour/level (D)

　　As biofeedback, except you take a portion of each damaging attack as subdual damage equal to twice your Strength modifier, and the duration is extended.
　
高等超距接触(Improved Clairtangency)
　　心灵转化系(体质)
　　等级：心灵术士8
　　灵能点：15
　　如同“超距接触”，但你可以仿效“心灵遥控”来配合“锐耳术/鹰眼术”效果（你无需展现“心灵遥控”即可使用该异能）。“高等超距接触”的持续时间在使用“心灵遥控”的持续发力效果时为最长1分钟/等级，但使用猛烈冲击後本异能将立即终止。
　
Improved Clairtangency
　　Psychokinesis (Con)
　　Level: Psion 8
　　Power Points: 15
　　As clairtangency, except you can emulate telekinesis in conjunction with a clairaudience/clairvoyance effect (you don’t need to manifest telekinesis to use this power). Improved clairtangency’s duration is up to 1 minute/level when the telekinesis effect is used as a sustained force, but it expires immediately after a violent thrust.
　
高等以太化(Improved Etherealness)

Improved Etherealness

　　Power Points: 15
　　As etherealness, except the duration is an order of magnitude greater.

高等飞行术(Improved Fly)

　　等级：心灵术士6
　　灵能点：11
　　如同“飞行术”，但受术者的速度变为180眨ù┳胖屑谆蛑丶自蛭150眨。
　
Improved Fly
　　Psychoportation (Dex)
　　Level: Psion 6
　　Power Points: 11
　　As fly, except the subject can fly at a speed of 180 feet (150 feet if the creature wears medium or heavy armor).
　
高等心灵遥控(Improved Telekinesis)
　　心灵转化系(体质)
　　等级：心灵术士7
　　持续时间：专注，最长10分钟/等级 或 立即 (见说明)
　　灵能点：13
　　如同“心灵遥控”，但力量更强，持续更久（对于持续发力）。当产生持续发力时，你可以将重量不超过每显能者等级100磅的生物或物体每轮移动50铡５辈生猛烈冲击时，物体造成的伤害如同“心灵遥控”，不超过重量限制的生物则受到6d6点伤害（如同从60崭叽ψ孤洌。
　
Improved Telekinesis
　　Psychokinesis (Con)
　　Level: Psion 7
　　Duration: Concentration, up to 10 minutes/level, or instantaneous (see text)
　　Power Points: 13
　　As telekinesis, except stronger and longer lasting (if a sustained force). When generating a sustained force, you move a creature or object weighing up to 100 pounds per manifester level up to 50 feet per round. When generating a violent thrust, objects cause damage as noted in telekinesis, and creatures within the weight range take 6d6 points of damage (as if they had fallen from 60 feet).
　
高等活力术(Improved Vigor)
　　心灵自塑系(力量)
　　等级：心灵术士6、心灵武士6
　　灵能点：11
　　如同“活力术”，但暂时生命值最大为60。
　
Improved Vigor
　　Psychometabolism (Str)
　　Level: Psion 6/Psychic Warrior 6
　　Power Points: 11
　　As vigor, except the maximum hit point cap is 60.
　
灵能恒定术(Incarnate)
　　心灵创造系(智力)
　　等级：心灵术士5
　　异象：物质
　　显能时间：2轮
　　距离：见说明
　　目标、效果或区域：见说明
　　持续时间：永久 (见说明)
　　豁免检定：无
　　异能抗力：不可
　　灵能点：9，消耗经验值
　　你将自持续的能量给予其他异能，使它们永远持续。你至少要达到展现本异能所要求的最低等级。本异能对已经恒定的异能不产生效果。你不能恒定一个没有持续时间或持续时间为立即的异能。你不能恒定一个需要花费经验值的异能，也不能恒定六级以上的异能。展现本异能时你必须花费经验值。你不能花费将使你下降一个或多个等级的经验值数量（虽然你可以放弃升级来恒定一个特别昂贵的异能）。经验值费用的浮动取决于其目标。
　　“灵能恒定术”可以被更高级的心灵术士所展现的“灵能恒定术”或者使用“心灵手术”所取消。
　　DM可能不允许一些异能被“灵能恒定术”恒定。（使用“魔法恒定术”的说明作为异能可与不可恒定的指南）。你在尝试恒定一个异能之前知道它是否能够被恒定。
　　经验值费用：要恒定一个自己身上的异能，你必须花费等于本异能的能级×300的经验值。要恒定其他生物身上的异能，你必须花费等于本异能能级×600的经验值，要恒定一个物品或一个地点上的异能，你必须花费等于本异能能级×900的经验值。
　
Incarnate
　　Metacreativity (Int)
　　Level: Psion 5
　　Display: Ma
　　Manifestation Time: 2 rounds
　　Range: See text
　　Target, Effect, or Area: See text
　　Duration: Permanent (see text)
　　Saving Throw: None
　　Power Resistance: No
　　Power Points: 9, XP cost
　　You invest other powers with self-sustaining energy so that they become permanent. You must be at least the minimum level required to manifest the power. This power has no affect on powers that already create a permanent effect. You can’t incarnate a power with no duration or a duration of instantaneous. You can’t incarnate a power that has an XP cost of its own, nor can you incarnate a power of level 6 or higher. You must expend XP when manifesting this power. You can never expend so much XP that doing so would drop you one or more levels (though you could forgo gaining a level in order to incarnate a particularly costly power). The XP costs vary depending on the target.
　　Incarnate can be negated by a higher-level psion who also manifests incarnate or by use of psychic chirurgery.
　　The DM may not allow some powers to become permanent through incarnate. (Use the permanency spell description for a guide to what can and cannot be made permanent.) You know before you attempt to incarnate a power if you can or cannot make it permanent.
　　XP Cost: To make a power permanent in regard to yourself, you must expend a number of XP equal to the power’s level x 300. To make a power permanent in regard to another creature, you must expend a number of XP equal to the power’s level x 600. To make a power permanent on an abject or location, you must expend a number of XP equal to the power’s level x 900.
　
惰性障壁(Inertial Barrier)
　　心灵转化系(体质)
　　等级：心灵术士4、心灵武士4
　　异象：听觉、精神
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：接触
　　目标：接触到的生物
　　持续时间：10分钟/等级 或 能量散发
　　豁免检定：意志，通过则无效 (无害)
　　异能抗力：可 (无害)
　　灵能点：7
　　你在目标的周围创造出念力障壁以提高其对殴打、切割、刺击和挥砍的抵抗力，还对坠落提供一些保护。目标获得伤害减免10/+5。本异能成功阻止每显能者等级10点伤害（最多150点）後即告消散。惰性障壁还吸收坠落的正常伤害。吸收的坠落伤害也算在以上消散的效果内。念力障壁将空气中的毒气效果延迟 2d4轮。
　
Inertial Barrier
　　Psychokinesis (Con)
　　Level: Psion 4/Psychic Warrior 4
　　Display: Au, Me
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: Touch
　　Target: Creature touched
　　Duration: 10 minutes/level or until discharged
　　Saving Throw: Will negates (harmless)
　　Power Resistance: Yes (harmless)
　　Power Points: 7
　　You create a psychokinetic barrier around the subject that resists blows, cuts, stabs, and slashes, as well as providing some protection against falling. The subject gains damage reduction 10/+5. Once the power has prevented a total of 10 points of damage per manifester level (maximum 150 points), it is discharged. Inertial barrier also absorbs up to half the damage from a fall. Damage absorbed from a fall counts toward discharging the effect. The psychokinetic barrier delays the effects of gases in the atmosphere for 2d4 rounds.
　
造成痛苦(Inflict Pain)
　　心灵附魔系(魅力)[影响心灵]
　　等级：心灵术士2
　　异象：听觉
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：远距 (400+40/等级)
　　目标：单一活物
　　持续时间：立即
　　豁免检定：意志，通过则无效
　　异能抗力：可
　　灵能点：3
　　你以传心术戳刺对手的精神，造成极度的痛苦。这种精神攻击造成3d6点伤害。
　
Inflict Pain
　　Telepathy (Cha) [Mind-Affecting]
　　Level: Psion 2
　　Display: Au
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: Long (400 ft. + 40 ft./level)
　　Target: One living creature
　　Duration: Instantaneous
　　Saving Throw: Will negates
　　Power Resistance: Yes
　　Power Points: 3
　　You telepathically stab the mind of your foe, causing horrible agony. The telepathic strike deals 3d6 points of damage.
　
模糊直觉(Inkling)
　　心灵预言系(感知)
　　等级：心灵术士0
　　灵能点：1
　　如果“卜筮”，但得到有意义的回答的基本几率是50%。
　　注意：你每天展现“模糊直觉”的次数不能超过你的感知调整值+1，即使你支付更多的灵能点，或是还剩有免费显能次数。该限制反映了尝试用如此低能级的异能获取未来的信息会让你的心灵疲惫。
　
Inkling
　　Clairsentience (Wis)
　　Level: Psion 0
　　Power Points: 1
　　As augury, except the base chance for receiving a meaningful reply is 50%.
　　Note: You may only manifest inkling a number of times per day equal to your Wisdom modifier +1, regardless of further payment of power points or number of free manifestations left in the day. This restriction reflects the strain you put on your mind by using such a low-level power to attempt to wrench information from the future.
　
摄魂术(Insanity)
　　心灵附魔系(魅力)[胁迫、影响心灵]
　　等级：心灵术士7
　　异象：精神
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：中距 (100+10/等级)
　　目标：单一活物
　　持续时间：立即
　　豁免检定：意志，通过则无效
　　异能抗力：可
　　灵能点：13
　　被本异能影响的生物将永久的疯掉并不断做出随机动作，如下表所示：
　
───────────────────
ｄ１０　动作
───────────────────
１　　　一分钟内四处乱走（除非被阻挡）
２─６　一轮内无行动
７─９　一轮内攻击最接近的生物
１０　　一轮内正常行动
───────────────────
　
　　除非掷出1，否则每轮都要掷骰来决定受术者本轮内的行动。四处乱走的生物将会若无其事的离开现场。攻击他们不会有任何加值。每个受术者的行动将在他们的回合开始时决定。任何疯狂的生物若受到攻击则会自动的在下回合反击攻击者。
　　只有“心灵手术”和其他极端的方法才能恢复受术者的神智。
　
Insanity
　　Telepathy (Cha) [Compulsion, Mind-Affecting]
　　Level: Psion 7
　　Display: Me
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: Medium (100 ft. + 10 ft./level)
　　Target: One living creature
　　Duration: Instantaneous
　　Saving Throw: Will negates
　　Power Resistance: Yes
　　Power Points: 13
　　Creatures affected by this power are permanently insane and constantly behave randomly, as indicated on the follow table:
　
───────────────────────────
d10 roll　Action
───────────────────────────
1　　　　 Wander away for 1 minute (unless prevented)
2-6　　　 Do nothing for 1 round
7-9　　　 Attack nearest creature for 1 round
10　　　　Act normally for 1 round
───────────────────────────
　
　　Except on a result of 1, roll again each round to see what the subject does that round. Wandering creatures leave the scene as if uninterested. Attackers are not at any special advantage when attacking them. Actions are checked at the beginning of each creature’s turn. Any insane creature that is attacked automatically attacks its attackers on its next rum.
　　Only psychic chirurgery and other extreme measures can restore the subject’s sanity.
　
感官入侵(Intrusive Sense Link)
　　心灵附魔系(魅力)[影响心灵]
　　等级：心灵术士2
　　灵能点：3
　　如同“感觉链接”，但改为受术者能感觉到你所感觉的（只对一种感官有效）。比如，如果你连接味觉然後吃一些显然腐败了的东西（由DM来判断），受术者必须通过意志豁免检定对抗正常DC，未通过则被震慑一轮。如果你吃掉能使你受伤的东西，受术者不会受到伤害，但必须通过对抗正常DC的豁免检定，未通过则震慑1d2轮。同样的，如果你连接视觉并被凝视攻击，则受术者也受到此次攻击。
　
Intrusive Sense Link
　　Telepathy (Cha) [Mind-Affecting]
　　Level: Psion 2
　　Power Points: 3
　　As sense link, except the subject creature senses what you sense (one sense only). For example, if you link taste and then eat something particularly foul (DM’s discretion), the subject creature must make another Will save against the original DC or be stunned for 1 round. If you eat something that causes you damage, the subject creature takes no damage but must make a saving throw against the original DC or be stunned for 1d2 rounds. Likewise, if you link sight and are subject to a gaze attack, so is the subject.
　
隐形术(Invisibility)
　　心灵转化系(体质)
　　等级：心灵术士2
　　异象：无
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：个人 或 接触
　　目标：自己 或 一个重量不超过100磅/等级的生物或物体
　　持续时间：10分钟/等级 (解消)
　　豁免检定：意志，通过则无效 (无害、物体)
　　异能抗力：可 (无害、物体)
　　灵能点：3
　　你接触到的生物或物体从视线（包括黑暗视觉）中消失。如果受术者带着装备，他的装备也一同消失。如果你对他人展现本异能，你和你的盟友都将看不见目标，除非你原本就能看见隐形的事物或使用灵能做到这点。
　　从被隐形的生物身上掉下或放下的物品将显形，被该生物捡起并塞进穿在身上的衣服或口袋里的物体会隐形。虽然光源可以隐形，但光本身决不会隐形（因而，效果就是有光却看不见光源）。目标携带的物体的任何延伸到远离他10找陨现处的部分将会显形，例如拖着的绳子。
　　当然，目标并非受到魔法沉默效果，某些其他情况会导致受术者被侦测到（例如踏足泥浆）。目标攻击任何生物都将导致本异能结束。对本异能而言，“攻击”包括以敌人或包括敌人的区域为目标的异能。（谁是敌人严格按照隐形人物的感知而定。）针对无人持有的物品的行动不会结束本异能。间接导致伤害也不算攻击。因而，隐形生物可以开门、交谈、进食、爬楼、塑造星质构装体并令其替自己进攻、切断正有敌人通过的索桥的吊绳、远程触发陷阱、开闸放恶犬等等。然而如果他直接进行攻击，就会立即连同装备一起显形。注意只影响盟友而不影响敌人的异能在这里不算攻击，即使敌人被包括在异能影响区域内。
　　隐形的攻击者的攻击骰获得+2加值（只对单次攻击有效，不管是近战还是远程，这在显形前生效），对抗隐形攻击的防御者失去任何对防御等级的敏捷加值。
　
Invisibility
　　Psychokinesis (Con)
　　Level: Psion 2
　　Display: None
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: Personal or touch
　　Target: You or a creature or object weighing no more than 100 lb./level
　　Duration: 10 minutes/level (D)
　　Saving Throw: Will negates (harmless, object)
　　Power Resistance: Yes (harmless, object)
　　Power Points: 3
　　The creature or object touched vanishes from sight, even from darkvision. If the recipient is a creature carrying gear, the gear vanishes, too. If you manifest the power on someone else, neither you nor your allies can see the subject, unless you can normally see invisible things or employ psionics to do so.
　　Items dropped or put down by an invisible creature become visible; items picked up disappear if tucked into the clothing or pouches worn by the creature. Light, however, never becomes invisible, although a source of light can become so (thus, the effect is that of a light with no visible source). Any part of an item that the subject carries but that extends more than 10 feet from her becomes visible, such as a trailing rope.
　　Of course, the subject is not magically silenced, and certain other conditions can render the recipient detectable (such as stepping in a puddle). The power ends if the subject attacks any creature. For purposes of this power, an “attack” includes any power targeting a foe or whose area or effect includes a foe. (Exactly who is a foe depends on the invisible character’s perceptions.) Actions directed at unattended objects do not negate the power. Causing harm indirectly is not an attack. Thus, an invisible being can open doors, talk, eat, climb stairs, fashion an astral construct and have it attack for her, cut the ropes holding a rope bridge while enemies are on the bridge, remotely trigger traps, open a portcullis to release attack dogs, and so on. If she attacks directly, however, she immediately becomes visible along with all her gear. Note that powers that specifically affect allies but not foes are not attacks for this purpose, even when they include foes in their area.
　　An invisible attacker gains a +2 bonus on his attack roll (for the single attack, either melee or ranged, that he is allowed before becoming visible), and the defender against such an attack loses any Dexterity bonus to Armor Class.
　
消除隐形(Invisibility Purge)
　　心灵预言系(感知)
　　等级：心灵术士3
　　异象：视觉
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：个人
　　目标：自己
　　持续时间：1分钟/等级 (解消)
　　灵能点：5
　　环绕着你的半径为每显能者等级5涨蛐瘟Τ∠解一切形式的隐形。任何隐形者在异能影响区域内都将显形。
　
Invisibility Purge
　　Clairsentience (Wis)
　　Level: Psion 3
　　Display: Vi
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: Personal
　　Target: You
　　Duration: 1 minute/level (D)
　　Power Points: 5
　　You surround yourself with a sphere of power with a radius of 5 feet per manifester level that negates all forms of invisibility. Anything invisible becomes visible while in the area.
　
钢铁身躯(Iron Body)
　　心灵自塑系(力量)
　　等级：心灵术士8
　　异象：听觉
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：个人
　　目标：自己
　　持续时间：1分钟/等级 (解消)
　　灵能点：15
　　本异能将你的身体变为活生生的钢铁，这给予你以下几项抗力与能力。
　　你获得伤害减免50/+3。你对目盲、重击、属性伤害（除了心灵战斗所导致的属性伤害）、耳聋、疾病、溺水、毒素、震慑以及所有影响你的生理系统与呼吸的异能、法术或攻击免疫，因为在本异能持续期间你不具有任何生理构造，也没有呼吸。你只受一半强酸和火焰伤害，无论其来源。但你也容易被任何能影响钢铁魔像的特殊攻击所影响。
　　你的力量得到+6增强加值，但是你的敏捷受到-6增强减值（敏捷值最低为1）。你的速度降为正常的一半。你无法喝水（因此无法使用药水），也不能吹奏管乐器。
　　你的徒手攻击造成1d6点正常伤害（小体型的显能者造成1d4伤害），并且你的徒手攻击被视为“武装”的。
　　你的体重增加为原来的10倍，这使你在水中会如同石块一样沉没。但是，你仍然可以在海底的巨大压力与无空气状态下存活――――至少在本异能结束之前。
　
Iron Body
　　Psychometabolism (Str)
　　Level: Psion 8
　　Display: Au
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: Personal
　　Target: You
　　Duration: 1 minute/level (D)
　　Power Points: 15
　　This power transforms your body into living iron, which grants you several powerful resistances and abilities.
　　You gain damage reduction 50/+3. You are immune to blindness, critical hits, damage to ability scores (except if that damage comes as a result of psionic combat), deafness, disease, drowning, poison, stunning, and all powers, spells or attacks that affect your physiology or respiration, because you have no physiology or respiration while this power is in effect. You only suffer half damage from acid and fire of all kinds. However, you also become vulnerable to all special attacks that affect iron golems.
　　You gain a +6 enhancement bonus to your Strength score but you suffer a -6 enhancement penalty to Dexterity as well (to a minimum Dexterity score of 1), and your speed is reduced to half normal. You cannot drink (and thus can’t use potions), nor play wind instruments.
　　Your unarmed attacks deal 1d6 points of normal damage, and you are considered “armed” when making unarmed attacks (a small manifester instead deals 1d4 points of damage).
　　Your weight increases by a factor of 10, causing you to sink like a stone in water. However, you could survive the crushing pressure and lack of air at the bottom of the ocean― at least until the power expires.
异能详述-K、L字头系列
 敲击术(Knock)
　　心灵传送系(敏捷)
　　等级：心灵术士2
　　异象：物质
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：中距 (100+10/等级)
　　目标：面积不超过10平方/等级的一扇门、一个箱子或盒子
　　持续时间：立即 (见说明)
　　豁免检定：无
　　异能抗力：不可
　　灵能点：3
　　异能“敲击术”可以打开卡住，闩住，锁住或以灵能锁住的门（以及以魔法固定或以“秘法锁”锁住的门，除非使用变体规则“灵能异于魔法”），它也可以打开密门、锁住的箱子或盒子。同时也可以将熔接、铐住或拴住的部分松开（如果它们被用来锁住容器）。如果用来打开被“灵能锁”锁住的门，它不会移除“灵能锁”，而只是使其停止作用10分钟。除此之外，其他的门都不会自行再锁上或卡住。“敲击术”不能抬起被闩住的城门或类似障碍（如铁闸门），也不会影响绳索、藤蔓等物。4级显能者可以对面积不超过40盏拿耪瓜帧扒没魇酢保每展现一次可以去除两种闭门法。例如：同时被锁住，闩住，封住的门需要两次“敲击术”才能打开。
　
Knock
　　Psychoportation (Dex)
　　Level: Psion 2
　　Display: Ma
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: Medium (100 ft. + 10 ft./level)
　　Target: One door, box, or chest with an area of up to 10 sq. ft./level
　　Duration: Instantaneous (see text)
　　Saving Throw: None
　　Power Resistance: No
　　Power Points: 3
　　The knock power opens stuck, barred, locked, or psionically locked doors (and magically held and arcane locked doors, unless the Psionics Are Different option is in use). It opens secret doors, as well as locked or trick-opening boxes or chests. It also loosens welds, shackles, or chains (provided they serve to hold closures shut). If used to open a psionically locked door, the power does not remove the psionic lock but simply suspends its functioning for 10 minutes. In all other cases, the door does not relock itself or becomes stuck again on its own. Knock does not raise barred gates or similar impediments (such as a portcullis), nor does it affect ropes, vines, and the like. Note that the effect is limited by the area. A 4th-level manifester can manifest knock on a door of 40 square feet or less. Each power can undo up to two means of preventing egress through a portal. Thus if a door is locked, barred, and held, or quadruple locked, opening it requires two knock powers.
　
指北术(Know Direction)
　　心灵预言系(感知)
　　等级：心灵术士0、心灵武士0
　　异象：精神
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：个人
　　目标：自己
　　持续时间：立即
　　灵能点：1
　　你能立即知道哪个方向是北。如果位于磁力线不能指明北方的地方，你可能会得知某显著地标的方向，这由DM决定。你只在展现本异能後的那一瞬间知道北的方向。你随後的移动可能再次导致迷失方向。
　
Know Direction
　　Clairsentience (Wis)
　　Level: Psion 0/Psychic Warrior 0
　　Display: Me
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: Personal
　　Target: You
　　Duration: Instantaneous
　　Power Points: 1
　　You instantly know which way is north. If in a place where magnetic field lines do not specify north, you may know the direction of a prominent landmark, at the DM’s discretion. You only know the direction of north immediately after manifesting this power. Subsequent movement on your part could confuse matters once again.
　
明了位置(Know Location)
　　心灵预言系(感知)
　　等级：心灵术士1
　　异象：精神
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：个人
　　目标：自己
　　持续时间：立即
　　灵能点：1
　　你大致知道你在哪里。本异能对于常常由传送、“异界之门”或通过其他位面的旅行者很有用。本异能揭示你的位置的一般信息。该信息通常只包括参照本地显著地标的相对位置，例如“灰鹰城西北西约20哩”。如果附近没有显著位置，像“漂泊在阴森之海(Sunless Sea)上”这样的答案也是可能的，这至少提供了一些关于位置的信息。你随後的移动可能再次导致迷失方向。
　
Know Location
　　Clairsentience (Wis)
　　Level: Psion 1
　　Display: Me
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: Personal
　　Target: You
　　Duration: Instantaneous
　　Power Points: 1
　　You generally know where you are. This power is useful to characters who frequently travel via teleportation, gates, or via other planes of existence. The power reveals general information about the character’s location. The information is usually no more detailed than a summary that locates you according to a prominent local landmark, such as “approximately 20 miles west-northwest of Greyhawk City.” If no prominent locations are nearby, answers such as “adrift on the Sunless Sea” are also possible, which at least provide some information about location. Subsequent movement on your part could confuse matters once again.
　
次级身体调节(Lesser Body Adjustment)
　　心灵自塑系(力量)
　　等级：心灵术士1
　　灵能点：1
　　如同“身体调节”，但你能够自疗1d8生命值，或使你对抗毒素或疾病的下一次强韧检定得到+1加值，又或者治疗1点暂时属性伤害。你不能通过一次展现同时得到以上三项益处。
　
Lesser Body Adjustment
　　Psychometabolism (Str)
　　Level: Psion 1
　　Power Points: 1
　　As body adjustment, except you cure yourself of 1d8 hit points, or gain just a +1 bonus on your next Fortitude save against poison or disease, or heal 1 point of temporary ability damage. You don’t gain all three benefits simultaneously for a single manifestation.
　
次级冲击波(Lesser Concussion)
　　心灵转化系(体质)
　　等级：心灵术士1
　　灵能点：1
　　如同“冲击波”，但“次级冲击波”造成1d6点伤害。
　
Lesser Concussion
　　Psychokinesis (Con)
　　Level: Psion 1
　　Power Points: 1
　　As concussion, except lesser concussion deals 1d6 points of damage.
　
次级支配术(Lesser Domination)
　　心灵附魔系(魅力)[胁迫、影响心灵、依赖语言]
　　等级：心灵术士3
　　灵能点：5
　　如同支配术，但如果你与受术者没有共通语言，本异能将完全无效。
　
Lesser Domination
　　Telepathy (Cha) [Compulsion, Mind-Affecting, Language-Dependent]
　　Level: Psion 3
　　Power Points: 5
　　As domination, except that if no common language is shared between you and the subject, the power does not function at all.
　
次级强化武器(Lesser Metaphysical Weapon)
　　心灵创造系(智力)
　　等级：心灵术士1、心灵武士1
　　灵能点：1
　　如同“强化武器”，但你的武器在攻击和伤害检定上获得+1增强加值。
　
Lesser Metaphysical Weapon
　　Metacreativity (Int)
　　Level: Psion 1/Psychic Warrior 1
　　Power Points: 1
　　As metaphysical weapon, except the weapon gains a +1 enhancement bonus on attack and damage rolls.
　
次级连心术(Lesser Mindlink)
　　心灵附魔系(魅力)
　　等级：心灵术士1
　　异象：物质
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：近距 (25+5/2等级)
　　目标群：你和另一个开始时相距不超过30盏纳物
　　持续时间：10分钟/等级
　　豁免检定：无
　　异能抗力：不可
　　灵能点：1
　　你创造出与另一生物的心灵链接，受术者的智力值必须至少为6。此链接只能设立于自愿的受术者，因此他不会得到豁免检定或者利用异能抗性。你可以通过此链接与受术者心灵沟通，即使并无共通语言。此链接并无其他的能力或影响。链接被建立後，便没有任何距离限制（不过仍然不能跨越位面作用）。
　
Lesser Mindlink
　　Telepathy (Cha)
　　Level: Psion 1
　　Display: Ma
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: Close (25 ft. + 5 ft./2 levels)
　　Targets: You and one other creature who is initially no more than 30 ft. away
　　Duration: 10 minutes/level
　　Saving Throw: None
　　Power Resistance: No
　　Power Points: 1
　　You forge a telepathic bond with another creature, which must have an Intelligence score of 6 or higher. The bond can be established only with a willing subject, who therefore receives no saving throw and gains no benefit from power resistance. You can communicate telepathically through the bond even if you do not share a common language. No special power or influence is established as a result of the bond. Once the bond is formed, it works over any distance (although nor from one plane to another).
　
次级天生护甲(Lesser Natural Armor)
　　心灵自塑系(力量)
　　等级：心灵术士0
　　异象：嗅觉、物质
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：个人
　　目标：自己
　　持续时间：1分钟
　　灵能点：1
　　你的皮肤长出粗厚的皱褶，使你的防御等级得到+1天生防御加值。与普通装甲不同，“天生护甲”没有盔甲检定减值和速度降低。
　
Lesser Natural Armor
　　Psychometabolism (Str)
　　Level: Psion 0
　　Display: Ol, Ma
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: Personal
　　Target: You
　　Duration: 1 minute
　　Power Points: 1
　　Your skin grows thick ridges, providing a +1 natural armor bonus to your AC. Unlike mundane armor, natural armor entails no armor check penalty or speed reduction.
　
浮空术(Levitate)
　　心灵传送系(敏捷)
　　等级：心灵术士2、心灵武士2
　　异象：嗅觉
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：个人 或 近距 (25+5/2等级)
　　目标：自己 或 自愿的单一生物 或 单一物品 (总重量至多100磅/等级)
　　持续时间：10分钟/等级 (解消)
　　豁免检定：无
　　异能抗力：不可
　　灵能点：3
　　“浮空术”可以使你任意垂直移动自己、另一生物或物品。如果要移动该生物，该生物必须自愿。如果要移动物品，该物品必须是无人持有或持有者愿意的物品。你每轮可以移动目标物垂直移动20眨这属于移动等效动作。你无法控制目标物水平移动，但受术者可以攀上悬崖或贴着天花板慢慢挪动（速度为基本速度的一半）。
　　一个浮空的生物无法稳定的使用近战武器或远程武器。他的第一次攻击会受到-1减值，第二次攻击会受到-2减值，以此类推，最多受到-5减值。如果该生物花费一整轮来恢复平衡，他下一次攻击的减值会从-1开始重新计算。
　
Levitate
　　Psychoportation (Dex)
　　Level: Psion 2/Psychic Warrior 2
　　Display: Ol
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: Personal or close (25 ft. + 5 ft./2 levels)
　　Target: You or one willing creature or one object (total weight up to 100 lb./level)
　　Duration: 10 minutes/level (D)
　　Saving Throw: None
　　Power Resistance: No
　　Power Points: 3
　　Levitate allows you to move yourself, another creature, or an object up and down as you wish. A creature must be willing to be levitated, and an object must be unattended or possessed by a willing creature. You can mentally direct the recipient to move up or down up to 20 feet each round; doing so is a move-equivalent action. You cannot move the recipient horizontally, but the recipient could clamber along the face of a cliff, for example, or push against a ceiling to move laterally (generally at half its base speed).
　　A levitating creature who attacks with a melee or ranged weapon finds himself increasingly unstable; the first attack has an attack roll penalty of -1, the second C2, and so on, up to a maximum penalty of -5. A full round spent stabilizing allows the creature to begin again at -1.
异能详述-M字头系列
 高等造物术(Major Creation)
　　心灵创造系(智力)
　　等级：心灵术士5
　　显能时间：10分钟
　　距离：近距 (25+5/2等级)
　　持续时间：见说明
　　灵能点：9
　　如同“次级造物术”，但你可以塑造矿物：石头、水晶、金属等。所造物品的持续时间根据其硬度和稀有程度而改变：
　
──────────────────
硬度以及稀有度范例　　持续时间
──────────────────
植物　　　　　　　　　２小时／等级
石头、水晶、基本金属　１小时／等级
贵重金属　　　　　　　２０分钟／等级
宝石　　　　　　　　　１０分钟／等级
密银＊　　　　　　　　２轮／等级
精金※　　　　　　　　１轮／等级
──────────────────
＊包括类似的稀有金属。密银制品比相同的钢制品轻５０％。
※精金制品只有相同钢制品重量的７５％。硬度较高而且不易磨损。所以精金打造的防具具有AC加值，而武器则有命中与伤害加值。（即使它并非魔法物品或灵能物品）详细描述参见《地下城主指南》。
　
Major Creation
　　Metacreativity (Int)
　　Level: Psion 5
　　Manifestation Time: 10 minutes
　　Range: Close (25 ft. + 5 ft./2 levels)
　　Duration: See text
　　Power Points: 9
　　As minor creation, except you can also create an object of mineral nature: stone, crystal, metal, and so on. The duration of the created item varies with its relative hardness and rarity:
　
───────────────────────
Hardness and
Rarity Examples　　　　　　　Duration
───────────────────────
Vegetable matter　　　　　　 2 hours/level
Stone, crystal; base metals　1 hour/level
Precious metals　　　　　　　20 minutes/level
Gems　　　　　　　　　　　　 10 minutes/level
Mithral*　　　　　　　　　　 2 rounds/level
Adamantine**　　　　　　　　 1 round/level
───────────────────────
*Includes similar rare metals. Items made of mithral are 50% lighter than similar items made of steel.
**Items made of adamantine weigh 75% as much as similar items made of steel. They are also harder and better capable of retaining an edge, so armor and shields provide higher AC and weapons allow a bonus on attack and damage rolls (although the
　
　　Items are not psionic or magical). See the DUNGEON MASTER’s Guide for details.
　
集体星质茧(Mass Cocoon)
　　心灵创造系(智力)
　　等级：心灵术士7
　　异象：物质
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：近距 (25+5/2等级)
　　区域：体积等于棱长10盏牧⒎教宓募
　　持续时间：2小时/等级
　　豁免检定：无
　　异能抗力：不可
　　灵能点：13
　　如同“星质茧”，但你可以把几个生物（或者一个占据10毡叱さ牧⒎教宓拇笮蜕物）裹进一团扭动的、紧密的星质中。并且，目标不能进行豁免。在此范围内目标被绑缚并裹住，除非它们与茧的容量相比过大了。传送与其他形式的移动能力提供了一种逃脱的手段。但茧延伸至以太位面，阻止借助以太位面的移动。集体星质茧能抵抗“消解异能”，但它可以被解离或被强力所毁掉（它具有25点硬度与100点生命值）。
　
Mass Cocoon
　　Metacreativity (Int)
　　Level: Psion 7
　　Display: Ma
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: Close (25 ft. + 5 ft./2 levels)
　　Area: A 10-ft. cube-sized cocoon
　　Duration: 2 hours/level
　　Saving Throw: None
　　Power Resistance: No
　　Power Points: 13
　　As ectoplasmic cocoon, except you can cocoon several creatures (or a single large creature that fits in a 10-foot cube) in a mass of writhing, tightening ectoplasm. Also, no saving throw is granted; targets within the area are caught and cocooned unless they are too big to fit inside. Teleport and other forms of travel provide a means of escape, but the cocoon extends into the Ethereal Plane, blocking ethereal travel The mass cocoon resists negate psionics, but it can be disintegrated or destroyed through brute force (it has hardness 25 and 100 hit points).
　
集体冲击波(Mass Concussion)
　　心灵转化系(体质)
　　等级：心灵术士4
　　异象：物质
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：远距 (400+40/等级)
　　区域：半径20盏那蛐畏段
　　持续时间：立即
　　豁免检定：无
　　异能抗力：可
　　灵能点：7
　　如同“冲击波”，但爆裂的念动压力影响区域内所有的生物，对生物和无人持用的物体造成7d4点伤害。
　
Mass Concussion
　　Psychokinesis (Con)
　　Level: Psion 4
　　Display: Ma
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: Long (400 ft. + 40 ft./level)
　　Area: 20-ft. radius sphere
　　Duration: Instantaneous
　　Saving Throw: None
　　Power Resistance: Yes
　　Power Points: 7
　　As concussion, except telekinetic pressure causes all creatures and objects within the area to explosively rupture, dealing 7d4 points of damage to creatures and unattended objects.
　
集体支配术(Mass Domination)
　　心灵附魔系(魅力)[胁迫、影响心灵]
　　等级：心灵术士7
　　目标群：一个生物/等级，其中任何两个相距不可超过30
　　灵能点：13
　　如同“支配术”，但你可以影响更多生物并且可以控制没有共通语言的受术者。你可以给每个生物不同的指示。
　
Mass Domination
　　Telepathy (Cha) [Compulsion, Mind-Affecting]
　　Level: Psion 7
　　Targets: One creature/level, no two of which can be more than 30 ft. apart
　　Power Points: 13
　　As domination, except you can affect more creatures and can control a subject with whom you do not share a common language. You can give different directions to different creatures.
　
集体暗示(Mass Suggestion)
　　心灵附魔系(魅力)[胁迫、影响心灵、依赖语言]
　　等级：心灵术士6
　　距离：中距 (100+10/等级)
　　目标群：一个生物/等级，其中任何两个相距不可超过30
　　灵能点：11
　　如同“暗示”，但本异能可以影响多个目标。所有受影响的生物会得到同一条暗示。
　
Mass Suggestion
　　Telepathy (Cha) [Compulsion, Mind-Affecting, Language-Dependent]
　　Level: Psion 6
　　Range: Medium (100 ft. + 10 ft./level)
　　Targets: One creature/level, no two of which can be more than 30 ft. apart
　　Power Points: 11
　　As suggestion, except that it can affect more creatures. The same suggestion applies to all these creatures.
　
物质激灼(Matter Agitation)
　　心灵转化系(体质)
　　等级：心灵术士1
　　异象：听觉、物质
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：近距 (25+5/2等级)
　　区域：一个物体或生物的2平方盏谋砻媲域
　　持续时间：专注，最长2轮/等级
　　豁免检定：无
　　异能抗力：可
　　灵能点：1
　　你可以激发非魔法物体的结构，使其随时间流逝而加热至燃点。如果你切换你的注意力到另一个物体上，第一个物体将冷却而第二个物体将被加热。
　　第一轮：非常易燃的材料（纸、干草、火绒、火把）点燃。皮肤变红（1点伤害）。
　　第二轮：木材闷燃并发烟，金属摸起来滚烫，皮肤起水泡（1d4点伤害），毛发闷烧，油漆起皱，水沸腾。
　　第三轮：木材点燃，金属烤焦（握持金属物体者受到1d4点伤害），皮肤烧伤且毛发点燃（1d6点伤害），铅熔化。
　　只要保持专注，你可以继续激灼所选的表面区域，但你只能对活物或亡灵目标造成最多1d6点伤害。
　
Matter Agitation
　　Psychokinesis (Con)
　　Level: Psion 1
　　Display: Au, Ma
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: Close (25 ft. + 5 ft./2 levels)
　　Area: 2 sq. ft. of surface area of an object or creature
　　Duration: Concentration, up to 2 rounds/level
　　Saving Throw: None
　　Power Resistance: Yes
　　Power Points: 1
　　You can excite the structure of a nonmagical object, heating it to the point of combustion over time. If you shift your focus to another object, the first object cools and the second object begins to heat up.
　　1st Round: Readily flammable materials (paper, dry grass, tinder, torches) ignite. Skin reddens (1 point of damage).
　　2nd Round: Wood smolders and smokes, metal becomes hot to the touch, skin blisters (1d4 points of damage), hair smolders, paint shrivels, water boils.
　　3rd Round: Wood ignites, metal scorches (1d4 points of damage for those holding metallic objects). Skin burns and hair ignites (1d6 points of damage), lead melts.
　　You can continue to agitate a chosen surface area up to the duration of the power if concentration holds, but you can only deal a maximum of 1d6 points of damage against a living or undead subject.
　
物质重塑(Matter Manipulation)
　　心灵转化系(体质)
　　等级：心灵术士8
　　异象：听觉、精神
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：近距 (25+5/2等级)
　　区域：1立方/等级的非活化物质
　　持续时间：立即
　　豁免检定：无
　　异能抗力：可
　　灵能点：15，消耗经验值
　　你可以削弱或巩固组成物体或结构的物质。你可以影响平凡的和魔法的无生命材料。削弱物体的物质将减少其硬度和生命值，而巩固则将增加其硬度和生命值。你至多可以将物体的硬度增加或减少5点(见《玩家手册》第八章的表8-12、表8-13和表8-15)。物体（或物体的部分）每增加一点硬度，就获得每己穸3点的生命值，而物体（或物体的部分）每减少一点硬度，就失去每己穸2点的生命值（每己穸戎辽倩嵊1点生命值）。你不能使硬度已经为0的物体减少硬度（或生命值）。例如，你可以将一伎淼纳子的硬度从0增加到5，同时使其总生命值变成17。你也可以将石墙的硬度减少到3，同时使其每己穸壬命值减少到5，使受影响的区域更容易被打破。
　　物质重塑：对物体或其部分的硬度的改变是永久的。如果铁锭的硬度被增加到15，它们将拥有秘银的强度特性（而且生命值还更多）。如果秘银的硬度被重塑成20，它将拥有精金打造的武器的特殊性质（尽管看起来像秘银）。将精金淬炼成25点硬度是可以的，但这除了更高硬度和每己穸扔懈多生命值外没有其他好处。你还可以巩固或削弱打造好的武器、防具或其他成品。
　　经验值费用：物品的最终硬度×100点经验值。
　
Matter Manipulation
　　Psychokinesis (Con)
　　Level: Psion 8
　　Display: Au, Me
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: Close (25 ft. + 5 ft./2 levels)
　　Area: 1 cu. ft./level of inanimate material
　　Duration: Instantaneous
　　Saving Throw: None
　　Power Resistance: Yes
　　Power Points: 15, XP cost
　　You can weaken or strengthen the substance of an object or structure. You can affect both mundane and magical inanimate material. Weakening an object’s substance decreases its hardness and hit points, and strengthening it increases its hardness and hit points. You can increase or decrease an object’s hardness by up to 5 from its base hardness (see Table 8-12, Table 8-13, and Table 8-15 in Chapter 8 of the Player’s Handbook). When hardness increases, the object (or portion of an object) gains 3 hit points per inch of thickness per increased hardness. When hardness decreases, the object (or portion of an object) loses 2 hit points per inch of thickness per decreased hardness (to a minimum of 1 hit point/inch of thickness). You can’t decrease the hardness (or the hit points) of an object that already has a hardness of 0. For instance, you can increase the hardness of a 1-inch-thick rope from 0 to 5, at the same time giving it a total of 17 hit points. You could also reduce the hardness of a stone wall to 3 and its hit points/inch of thickness to 5, making the affected area much more easily breached.
　　Working Manipulated Metals: An object or portion thereof whose hardness is decreased or increased is permanently changed. If several ingots of iron were increased to hardness 15, they would possess the strength qualities of mithral (although having more hit points). If mithral were manipulated to hardness 20, it would share the special characteristics of a weapon or armor forged of adamantine (though it would look like mithral). Hardening adamantine to 25 is possible, but this confers no benefits other than a higher hardness and more hit points/inch of thickness. You can also harden or weaken a preforged weapon, armor, or other finished item.
　　XP Cost: The item’s final hardness x 100 XP.
　
物质重组(Matter Rearrangement)
　　心灵转化系(体质)
　　等级：心灵术士5
　　异象：物质
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：近距 (25+5/2等级)
　　目标：若干总重量不超过1/10磅的非魔法金属物体，彼此相距不超过1
　　持续时间：立即
　　豁免检定：无
　　异能抗力：不可
　　灵能点：9，消耗经验值
　　你可以将一种金属转换成另一种。你每次展现本异能都可以影响一个或多个总重量不超过1/10磅的金属物体。在实践中，1/10磅相当于五枚硬币（5铜币、5银币、5金币等等）。
　　经验值费用：经验值的费用等于以金币为单位的转换後的金属价格，或至少1点经验值。例如，将5枚铜币转化为5枚金币的费用是5点经验值，而将5枚铜币转化为5枚铂币的费用就是50点经验值。
　
Matter Rearrangement
　　Psychokinesis (Con)
　　Level: Psion 5
　　Display: Ma
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: Close (25 ft. + 5 ft./2 levels)
　　Target: Nonmagical metal objects weighting up to a total of 1/10 pound, each no more than 1 inch from another
　　Duration: instantaneous
　　Saving Throw: None
　　Power Resistance: No
　　Power Points: 9, XP cost
　　You can transmute one metal into another. Each time you manifest the power, you affect a metal object up to 1/10 pound, or several metal objects whose total weight does not exceed 1/10 pound. In practical terms, 1/10 pound equals five standard coins (5 cp, 5 sp, 5 gp, and so on).
　　XP Cost: The XP cost equals the gp value of the newly transmuted metal, or a minimum of 1 XP. For instance, if you transmute 5 copper coins into 5 gold coins, the cost is 5 XP. If you transmute 5 copper coins to 5 platinum coins, the cost is 50 XP.
　
超能共鸣(Metaconcert)
　　心灵附魔系(魅力)[影响心灵]
　　等级：心灵术士5
　　异象：视觉 (见说明)
　　显能时间：1分钟
　　距离：10
　　目标：自己 和 最多十五名也懂得“超能共鸣”的其他心灵术士
　　持续时间：1轮/等级 (解消)
　　豁免检定：无
　　异能抗力：不可
　　灵能点：9
　　你将自己的精神力与其他心灵术士相连，创造出比参与者的简单加总强大的多的实体。所有参与者（最多16个，包括自己）都必须是自愿的，因此，豁免检定和异能抗力不起作用。一旦连接成功，你所有的异能点都将汇入共享的灵能储备，此灵能储备的储量将比参与者储量的总和多20%。因此，如果10个心灵术士每人贡献10点灵能点，则初始的共享灵能储量将为120。当本异能被展现後，一个个体将会被所有成员共同选出作为领导意志。在本异能结束之前，这个“领导者” 指挥团队的行动。在视觉上，雾状的炽热灵能线把所有成员的额头连接到一个复杂并不断变形的图样上。
　　由“超能共鸣”创造出的精神实体知道其参与者所知的全部异能。此实体并不能比一般个体做更多动作，但是它展现的异能更为强大。每个参与构成此实体的心灵术士都为展现异能时（也包括在使用心灵战斗模式时）所设置的DC和对抗异能时（包括对抗心灵战斗模式的意志豁免）所做出的豁免检定提供可累加的+1加值。如果精神实体由于心灵战斗而受到暂时属性伤害，则伤害总数将按照成员的共同意愿被分配在个体上（所以如果一个十人心灵术士团体受到3点暂时属性伤害，他们可以选择三个不同的成员，每个成员只受到1 点伤害）。
　　连接一旦建立，所有成员必须留在20罩本肚域内，并且只能以集体形式按10盏乃俣纫贫。成员可以自愿的在“超能共鸣”结束之前离去，但是他们离开时将不会恢复灵能点数。偶然或强制移出本异能范围的成员也会以0点灵能点状态从本异能离开。
　　当“超能共鸣”正常结束或被解散，剩余的灵能储量将被平分给所有的成员（向下取整）。你不可能在离开时得到比参加“超能共鸣”时更多的灵能点数――多出的点数将化为弧光而消散。
　
Metaconcert
　　Telepathy (Cha) [Mind-Affecting]
　　Level: Psion 5
　　Display: Vi (see text)
　　Manifestation Time: 1 minute
　　Range: 10 feet
　　Target: You and up to fifteen other psions who also know metaconcert
　　Duration: 1 round/level (D)
　　Saving Throw: None
　　Power Resistance: No
　　Power Points: 9
　　You link your psychic might with other psions, creating an entity more powerful than the sum of its parts. All participants (up to sixteen total, including you) must be willing; thus, saving throws and power resistance do not reply. Once linked, all your power points flow into a collective pool, the total of which is 20% more than the sum of the participants’ pools. Thus, if ten psions each contribute 10 power points, the initial total of the pooled power points is 120. When the power is manifested, one individual is chosen as the lead mind by mutual consent of the other participants. Until the power ends, this “conductor” directs the efforts of the group. Visually, misty strands of glowing power link the brows of all the participants in a complex and shifting pattern.
　　All the powers of each participant are known to the mental entity constructed by metaconcert. This entity can’t take any more actions than a normal individual, but it manifests all its powers more effectively. Each individual psion making up the entity provides a cumulative +1 bonus to DCs set when manifesting a power (including using a psionic attack mode) and a cumulative +1 bonus when making saving throws against powers (including will saves against psionic attack modes). If the psionic entity takes temporary ability damage from a psionic attack, the total is divided up among all the members as they see fit (so if a ten-psion group took 3 points of ability damage, they could select three different participants to each take only 1 point).
　　Once linked, the participants must remain within a 20-foot-diameter area, and as a group may only move at a speed of 10 feet. Participants can willingly drop out before the overall metaconcert ends, but they come away with 0 power points. Participants who accidentally move beyond the range of the power or who are forcibly removed also end up with 0 power points.
　　When metaconcert ends normally or is dismissed, remaining power points in the pool are evenly divided among all the participants (round down). You do not leave a metaconcert with more power points than you joined with --- extra power points are lost in bright arcs of light.
　
超感术(Metafaculty)
　　心灵预言系(感知)
　　等级：心灵术士9
　　异象：视觉、嗅觉、精神
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：个人
　　目标：自己
　　持续时间：专注，最长10分钟/等级 (解消)
　　豁免检定：无 (见说明)
　　异能抗力：见说明
　　灵能点：17，消耗经验值
　　你对之前由其他心灵预言系或心灵附魔系异能侦测到的任何个人或生物获得超常洞察力。就本异能而言，“超常洞察力”包括姓名、目标的精神映像、目标的阵营以及目标的位置（目标当前位置的图像，足以如同“极有研究”般地传送过去）。异能、特殊能力、法术都无法阻挡“超感术”查明真相，即使是“心灵屏障”或 “许愿术”这样的法术也不行。
　　经验值费用：你支出的经验值数等于你关注的个体的等级(或生命骰数)×500。因此，获得对10级或10HD目标的超常洞察力需要支出5000点经验值。你使用“超感术”时不能支出多到会让你降级的经验值。在这种情况下，“超感术”仅仅是失败（这本身也提供了一些信息）。
　
Metafaculty
　　Clairsentience (Wis)
　　Level: Psion 9
　　Display: Vi, Ol, Me
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: Personal
　　Target: You
　　Duration: Concentration, up to 10 minutes/level (D)
　　Saving Throw: None (see text)
　　Power Resistance: See text
　　Power Points: 17, XP cost
　　You gain exceptional insight concerning any individual or creature whom you have previously detected via any other Clairsentience or Telepathy power. For purposes of this power, “exceptional insight” includes a name, a mental image of the subject, the subject’s alignment, and the subject’s location (an image of the subject’s current location that is good enough to teleport to as if studied carefully). Powers, special abilities, and spells do not protect against metafaculty’s ability to find the truth, not even mind blank or spells such as wish.
　　XP Cost: You expend a number of XP equal to the total level (or HD) of the individual you focus on x 500. Thus, you would expend 5,000 XP to gain exceptional insight about a 10th-level or 10-HD subject. You can never expend so much XP using metafaculty that you would lose a level. If that would be the case, metafaculty simply fails to work (which provides some information by itself).
　
超态变化(Metamorphosis)
　　心灵自塑系(力量)
　　等级：心灵术士5
　　异象：物质、嗅觉
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：个人
　　目标：自己
　　持续时间：1小时/等级 (解消)
　　灵能点：9
　　如同“变形自己”，但你可以像变为其他生物一样变为无生命的物体。因此，你可以把自己变为一块石子（不得小于微型），也可以变成一块巨石（不得大于你的体形）。如同“变形自己”，你每一轮都可以选择你的形态。你可以变形为你所能想到的大多数东西，例如椅子、宝剑或地毯，但是如果你打算变为一个复杂的物品，你必须通过与之对应的技能检定。例如，如果你要变成一副漂亮的油画，你必须做一个手艺（绘画）检定通过由你的DM决定的DC来确定油画的质量。与之类似的，你无法变形为复杂的钟表或机械装置，除非你具有与之相关的技能。你无法变化为灵能强化或附魔的材料或物品，也不能变为任何具有15点或更高硬度的物品。你同样不能变为被灵能活化的装置或由星质构成的物品。
　　当你变为死物，你失去所有的活动能力。但是你仍保留原有的显能能力。如果你在物品状态下受到伤害，你也会受到伤害（但是受到此物品具有的硬度的保护）。
　
Metamorphosis
　　Psychometabolism (Str)
　　Level: Psion 5
　　Display: Ma, Ol
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: Personal
　　Target: You
　　Duration: 1 hour/level (D)
　　Power Points: 9
　　As polymorph self, except you can also assume the form of inanimate objects as well as creatures. Thus, you could change yourself into a rock (if no smaller than Diminutive size), or a boulder (if no more than one size larger than your normal size). As with polymorph self, you can switch forms each round. You can take the shape of most any object you can think of, such as a chair, a sword, or a rug, but if you attempt to take the form of a complex object, you must make an appropriate skill check. For instance, if you take the form of a beautiful painting, you must make a Craft (painting) check against a DC set by your DM to determine the quality of the painting. Likewise, you cannot take the form of a complex clockwork or mechanical mechanism unless you have some sort of skill associated with the object. You cannot metamorphose into inherently psionic or magical materials or objects, or any object with a hardness of 15 or greater. You also cannot take the form of a psionically animated mechanism or any sort of object formed of ectoplasm.
　　As an inanimate object, you lose all mobility; however, you retain your ability to manifest powers normally. If you take damage as an object, you also take damage (but the objects natural hardness, if any, protects you).
　
强化武器(Metaphysical Weapon)
　　心灵创造系(智力)
　　等级：心灵术士3、心灵武士3
　　异象：视觉 (见说明)
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：近距 (25+5/2等级)
　　目标：单个武器 或 50只弹射体(在显能时弹射体必须彼此接触)
　　持续时间：1小时/等级
　　豁免检定：意志，通过则无效 (无害、物体)
　　异能抗力：可 (无害、物体)
　　灵能点：5
　　武器的攻击检定与伤害检定获得+3增强加值。受到增强的武器发出银白色的光（不够提供照明），增强加值与精制品的+1攻击命中加值不累计。
　　或者，你也可以影响至多50只箭、矢或弹丸。这些弹射体必须属于同一种类，并且它们必须放在一起作为一个整体（比如放在同一个箭袋中）。弹射体（不包括投掷武器）在使用後将失去它们的增强加值。
　
Metaphysical Weapon
　　Metacreativity (Int)
　　Level: Psion 3/Psychic Warrior 3
　　Display: Vi (see text)
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: Close (25 ft. + 5 ft./2 levels)
　　Target: One weapon or fifty projectiles (all of which must be in contact with each other at the time of manifestation)
　　Duration: 1 hour/level
　　Saving Throw: Will negates (harmless, object)
　　Power Resistance: Yes (harmless, object)
　　Power Points: 5
　　A weapon gains a +3 enhancement bonus on attack and damage rolls. The enhanced weapon glows with pale silver radiance (not sufficient to provide illumination). An enhancement bonus does not stack with a masterwork weapon’s +1 bonus on attacks.
　　Alternatively, you can affect up to fifty arrows, bolts, or bullets. The projectiles must all be of the same type, and they have to be together in one group (such as in the same quiver). Projectiles (but not thrown weapons) lose their enhancement when used.
　
幻境术(Microcosm)
　　心灵附魔系(魅力)[魅惑、影响心灵]
　　等级：心灵术士9
　　异象：物质
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：近距 (25+5/2等级)
　　目标或区域：单一活物 或 半径15盏那蛐吻域内的若干生物
　　持续时间：立即
　　豁免检定：无
　　异能抗力：可
　　灵能点：17
　　在展现“幻境术”时，你可以选择目标为单个生物或是区域。
　　指定目标：如果“幻境术”是针对单个生命值不超过100的生物，则该生物的所有感觉都将从真实世界中被剪除。受术者的感受将完全由它自己的意志产生，虽然它并不会意识到这一点。而在现实中，受术者将会毫无生气的躺着，流着口水并呜咽着，并在无援情况下最终死于口渴与饥饿。受术者将活在完全由自己编造的世界里直到他的真实身体死亡。
　　区域效果：如果“幻境术”以区域效果展现，它将15瞻刖赌诘纳物送入它们自己（互不联系）的幻境中。它只会影响具有30点生命值或更少的生物，并且受影响的生物的生命值总和不得超过300。本异能将首先影响生命值最少的生物，直到下一个生物就会使生命值总数高过 300为止（具有负生命值的生物视为生命值为0）。
　　对同一受术者再次展现“幻境术”将会再次回到现实世界。否则，只有极为强大的心灵异能或类似的效果（比如“心灵手术”或者法术“高等复原术”）能恢复这种执着于幻境的精神错乱。
　
Microcosm
　　Telepathy (Cha) [Charm, Mind-Affecting]
　　Level: Psion 9
　　Display: Ma
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: Close (25 ft. + 5 ft./2 levels)
　　Target or Area: One living creature or one or more creatures within a 15-foot-radius sphere
　　Duration: Instantaneous
　　Saving Throw: None
　　Power Resistance: Yes
　　Power Points: 17
　　When microcosm is manifested, you can target either a single creature or a group.
　　Targeted: If microcosm targets a single creature, that creature’s senses are pinched off from the real world if it has 100 or fewer hit points. The subject’s senses are all completely fabricated from within its own mind, though it may not realize this. In reality, the subject sprawls limply, drooling and mewling, and will eventually die of thirst and starvation without aid. However, the subject lives within its own madeup world until the time of its actual death.
　　Area Effect: If microcosm is manifested as an area effect, it sends creatures in a 15-foot-radius sphere into their own (unlinked) catatonias. It affects only creatures that have 30 or fewer hit points, and only up to a total of 300 hit points of such creatures. The power affects creatures with the lowest hit point totals first until the next creature would put the total over the 300 hit point limit. (Creatures with negative hit points count as having 0 hit points.)
　　Manifesting microcosm a second time on a subject can turn its sensory pathways outward once more. Otherwise, only very powerful psionic powers or similar effects (such as psychic chirurgery or the spell greater restoration) can undo the mental crosswiring that creates a private world.
　
心灵屏障(Mind Blank)
　　心灵附魔系(魅力)
　　等级：心灵术士8
　　异象：嗅觉
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：近距 (25+5/2等级)
　　目标：单一生物
　　持续时间：1天
　　豁免检定：意志，通过则无效 (无害)
　　异能抗力：可 (无害)
　　灵能点：15
　　本异能保护受术者完全不被任何侦测、影响和阅读情绪与思想的装置或异能所影响。本异能可以针对所有影响心灵的异能与效果，以及搜集情报的预言系异能或效果（除了“极化认知”）进行防护。“心灵屏障”甚至能够阻止超凡的异能与法术（例如“有限许愿术”、“奇迹术”、“许愿术”），只要它们被用来以前述方式影响受术者的心智或搜集其情报。当使用“遥视术”或者“探知”被保护生物所在区域时，这些异能仍然有效但是被保护生物完全不被探知。特别针对受术者的“遥视术”与“侦测”完全失效。
　　“心灵屏障”对心灵攻击模式无效。
　
Mind Blank
　　Telepathy (Cha)
　　Level: Psion 8
　　Display: Ol
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: Close (25 ft. + 5 ft./2 levels)
　　Target: One creature
　　Duration: 1 day
　　Saving Throw: Will negates (harmless)
　　Power Resistance: Yes (harmless)
　　Power Points: 15
　　The subject is totally protected from all devices and power that detect, influence, or read emotions or thoughts. This protects against all mind-affecting powers and effects, as well as information gathering by Clairsentience powers or effects (except metafaculty). Mind blank even foils extraordinary powers and spells (such as limited wish, miracle, and wish) when they are used in such a way as to affect the subject’s mind or to gain information about him. In the case of remote viewing or scrying that scans an area that the creature is in, the power works but the creature simply isn’t detected. Remote viewing and scrying attempts that are targeted specifically at the subject do not work at all.
　　Mind blank is not effective against psionic attack modes.
　
心智探针(Mind Probe)
　　心灵附魔系(魅力)[魅惑]
　　等级：心灵术士5
　　异象：视觉、物质、听觉
　　显能时间：1分钟
　　距离：近距 (25+5/2等级)
　　目标：单一活物
　　持续时间：1分钟/等级
　　豁免检定：强韧，通过则无效
　　异能抗力：可
　　灵能点：9
　　从心中最深的角落存留的回忆到仍然能轻易想起的那些，受术者的全部知识和记忆全部对你敞开。你每个回合能得到一个问题的答案，这个答案由受术者的全部知识给出。你也可以窥视睡着的目标，虽然受术者在每个问题之後都将进行意志豁免对抗“心智探针”的DC，通过则会醒来。不愿意被刺探的受术者可以尝试离开本异能的有效距离，除非他以某种方式被阻挡。你以传心术提问，而这些问题的答案将直接传入你的大脑。你和受术者不必使用同一种语言，虽然低智能的生物可能只能提供一些相关的视觉影像作为你问题的答案。
　　被“心灵屏障”保护的生物不受“心智探针”的影响。
　
Mind Probe
　　Telepathy (Cha) [Charm]
　　Level: Psion 5
　　Display: Vi, Ma, Au
　　Manifestation Time: 1 minute
　　Range: Close (25 ft. + 5 ft./2 levels)
　　Target: One living creature
　　Duration: 1 minute/level
　　Saving Throw: Fortitude negates
　　Power Resistance: Yes
　　Power Points: 9
　　All the subject’s memories and knowledge are accessible to you, from memories deep below the surface to those still easily called to mind. You can learn the answer to one question per round, to the best of the subject’s knowledge. You can also probe a sleeping subject, though the subject may make a Will save against the DC of the mind probe to wake after each question. Subjects who do not wish to be probed can attempt to move beyond the power’s range, unless somehow hindered. You pose the questions telepathically, and the answers to those questions are imparted directly to your mind. You and the subject do not need to speak the same language, though less intelligent creatures may yield up only appropriate visual images in answer to your questions.
　　Creatures protected by mind blank are immune to mind probe.
　
心智魔种(Mind Seed)
　　心灵附魔系(魅力)[魅惑、影响心灵]
　　等级：心灵术士8
　　异象：物质
　　显能时间：3轮
　　距离：5
　　目标：一个体型不超过中型的类人生物
　　持续时间：立即
　　豁免检定：意志，通过则无效
　　异能抗力：可
　　灵能点：15，消耗经验值
