　　你将你的全部心智印入受术者的潜意识。如果灌输成功，你心智的种子将会在一星期後“发芽”。在这个时期内，受术者将会无意识的呈现出你的特殊习惯。比如，如果你习惯于咕哝“是的，当然，没错”，这种同样的冗长咕哝声不久後就会被受术者的嘴唇说出，虽然这绝不是出于自觉。七天的最终期限之前的任何时候， “心智魔种”都可以被“心灵手术”或者法术“高等复原术”从受术者的心中清除（再次施展“心智魔种”也会净化受术者的心智）。
　　当同化完成（七天之後），受术者变为具有你展现本异能时心智的你，但是他会比你低8个等级。他没有你的身体属性和装备，但是他会拥有你8个等级前具有的智力、感知和魅力值。受术者也知道你你在此等级时所知的所有异能。
　　在受术者成为你精神上的副本之後，两个人格将立即开始分离。虽然受术者由你的经验出发，他仍然保留他原本的“灵魂”和物质身体，并能够根据他自己的感受自由的发展个性。因此，受术者并非你的奴隶或是仆人，而是一个凭自由意志行动且具有你的早期记忆的NPC。
　　“防护邪恶”或者类似的法术与异能能够保护你不被植入“心智魔种”。
　　经验值费用：3000点经验值。
　
Mind Seed
　　Telepathy (Cha) [Charm, Mind-Affecting]
　　Level: Psion 8
　　Display: Ma
　　Manifestation Time: 3 rounds
　　Range: 5 feet
　　Target: One humanoid of Medium-size or smaller
　　Duration: Instantaneous
　　Saving Throw: Will negates
　　Power Resistance: Yes
　　Power Points: 15, XP cost
　　You impress the totality of your psyche into a subject’s subconscious. If successfully implanted, the seed of your mind “germinates” over a period of one week. During this time, the subject begins to unconsciously take on your mannerisms. For instance, if you habitually mutter, “Sure, sure, sure,” this same litany will soon be heard from the subject’s lips, though never consciously. Any time before the sevenday deadline, the mind seed can be purged from the subject’s mind with psychic chirurgery or the spell greater restoration (manifesting mind seed again also cleanses the mind).
　　When integration is complete (after seven days), the subject becomes you in mind as you were when you manifested the power but eight levels lower in experience. He does not possess any of your physical statistics or equipment, but does possess your ability scores in Intelligence, Wisdom, and Charisma as they were eight levels earlier. The subject also knows the powers you knew at the appropriate level.
　　As soon as the subject becomes your mental duplicate, the two personalities begin to diverge. Although the subject starts off with your experiences, he possesses his original “soul” and physical body and is free to develop his own personality based on its own experiences. Thus, the subject is not your slave or servant, but instead an NPC in his own right who shares your earlier memories.
　　Protection from evil or a similar spell or power can prevent you from implanting mind seed.
　　XP Cost: 3,000 XP.
　
储存心智(Mind Store)
　　心灵创造系(智力)
　　等级：心灵术士8
　　异象：物质 (见说明)
　　显能时间：10分钟
　　距离：接触
　　效果：一个水晶储存器
　　持续时间：立即
　　豁免检定：无
　　异能抗力：不可
　　灵能点：15
　　本异能制造出一个贮藏着你心智原质的储存水晶（本异能无法作用于一个已死亡的目标）。在你死亡或与之类似的时刻到来之前，储存水晶都是完全静止的。如果将来的某一日你被杀害，你的灵魂将转移进储存水晶中，此水晶将开始发出朦胧的光。在转移的基础上，你的物质剩余（它们将存留下来）变为惰性物质并在此之後无法被复活。从被杀的躯体到储存水晶的灵魂转移过程可以通过任意距离，在同一位面或跨越位面发生作用，除非一些特殊位面的特性阻止这种转移。
　　当你的身体死亡，储存水晶被激活，你具备相应等级的灵晶仆能力，加上你在展现“储存心智”时所有的已知异能和拥有的灵能点数，但等级会低1级。你有30天时间去得到一个新的身体，超过该期限後若你仍未进入一个新身体，你的知觉将消退，你的灵魂也将消失。
　　要培养一个身体，你（在储存水晶内）必须花费完全不被打扰的10天。身体的组成部分将从星界抽取星质，然後慢慢成形并转化成一具活生生的逼真的身体，此身体是你展现“储存心智”时的身体的精确副本（水晶本身慢慢的破碎并成为新的有机身体的一部分）。当十天期满，你完全的移居到新的身体中。你拥有比你展现 “储存心智”时的全部能力，除了等级少1，不过你没有任何装备。如果培养中的身体受到任何数量的伤害，它将被毁而你的灵魂将消失。
　　另一种可能是，你可以展现“心智互换”来利用一个临时躯体。不过只有邪恶的心灵术士会打破埋藏着他人心智的储存水晶来永久的占据受术者的身体（除非受术者本身就是不可救药的恶人）。
　
Mind Store
　　Metacreativity (Int)
　　Level: Psion 8
　　Display: Ma (see text)
　　Manifestation Time: 10 minutes
　　Range: Touch
　　Effect: One storage crystal
　　Duration: Instantaneous
　　Saving Throw: None
　　Power Resistance: No
　　Power Points: 15
　　This power makes a storage crystal containing the essence of your living mind (this power can’t be used on a dead subject). Until such time as you perish, the storage crystal is utterly inert. If you are slain at some later date, your soul transfers into the storage crystal, which begins to dimly glow. Upon transference, your physical remains (should they still exist) become inert matter and cannot thereafter be restored to life. The transfer from the slain body to the storage crystal works over any distance, physical or extradimensional, unless some sort of special planar geometry supersedes the transfer.
　　Once the storage crystal is activated by your physical body’s demise, you have the abilities of a psicrystal of the appropriate level, plus all the powers you knew and the power points you possessed when mind store was manifested but at one level lower. You have thirty days to grow an organic body, after which time your sentience fades and your soul passes on if it hasn’t entered a new body.
　　To grow a body, you (in the storage crystal) must spend ten days in uninterrupted solitude. The body’s constituent parts are pulled as ectoplasm from the Astral Plane, and slowly molded and transformed into a living, breathing body that is an exact duplicate of your body at the time you manifested mind store (the crystal itself slowly breaks down and becomes a part of the new organic body). When the ten days are completed, you completely and totally inhabit the new body. You possess all the abilities you possessed when mind store was manifested, at one level lower, but you have none of your equipment. If the growing body is struck for any amount of damage, it is destroyed and your soul passes on.
　　 Conceivably, you could manifest mind switch to utilize a temporary body, but only an evil psion would smash the storage crystal with an imbedded mind in order to permanently usurp the subject’s organic body (unless the subject is, itself, irredeemably evil).
　
心智互换(Mind Switch)
　　心灵附魔系(魅力)
　　等级：心灵术士6
　　异象：视觉
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：中距 (100+10/等级)
　　目标：自己和另一个体型不超过中型的生物
　　持续时间：直到你回到自己的身体为止
　　豁免检定：意志，通过则无效 (见说明)
　　异能抗力：可
　　灵能点：11
　　你可以尝试控制附近的一个生物，迫使它的心智（和灵魂）进入你的身体。你随时都可以让自己的心智返回自己的身体（同时也会把受术者的心智送回它的身体）。当你的意识回到你的身体内，本异能即告结束。
　　尝试互换心智是整轮动作。防护邪恶和类似的魔法与灵能的防护会阻挡“心智互换”。除非受术者成功通过意志豁免检定，否则你将占据该生物的身体，并迫使它的心智进入你的身体。
　　如果互换成功，你的生命力将占领寄主的身体，同时寄主的生命力也接管你的。你能够使用寄主生物基础的天生的知识，但得不到它後天学习到的知识（它对于你的身体也是一样）。比如，你不能自动掌握该生物所知的语言或异能。你与寄主都将保留自己的阵营、智力、感知和魅力值、职业、等级、技能、基本攻击加值、基本豁免加值、生命值（忽略新的体质值）、灵能点（如果有）和异能抗力（如果有）。双方都会得到新身体的力量、体质和敏捷值（包括这些属性的调整值），同时也获得对方的（非魔法的）天生防御。双方都无法获得对方的特殊能力。
　　你可以以一个标准动作回到你自己的身体，只要身体在异能范围内（这将结束本异能）。
　　如果你的新身体死亡而你的身体又在异能范围内，你将回到自己的身体，而寄主的生命力将消失。如果新身体被杀时不在异能范围内，你将死亡，而被转换的生物将永远的活在你的身体内。如果你的身体在被受术者占据时死亡，它将死亡，而你将会永远占据新的身体。脱离身体的生命力将会消失。
　　如果两个身体间距离不超过异能范围，对两个身体中的任一个成功展现“消解异能”都会把双方的心智送回原有身体。如果不在范围内，那么“消解异能”无效。
　
Mind Switch
　　Telepathy (Cha)
　　Level: Psion 6
　　Display: Vi
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: Medium (100 ft. + 10 ft./level)
　　Target: You and one other living Medium-size or smaller creature
　　Duration: Until you return to your body
　　Saving Throw: Will negates (see text)
　　Power Resistance: Yes
　　Power Points: 11
　　You can attempt to take control of a nearby living creature, forcing its mind (and soul) into your body. You may move your mind back into your own body whenever your desire (which returns the subject’s mind to its own body). The power ends when you send your mind back to your own body.
　　Attempting to switch minds is a full-round action. It is blocked by protection from evil or a similar magical or psionic ward. You possess the body and force the creature’s mind into your body unless it succeeds at a Will save.
　　If successful, your life force occupies the host body, and the host’s life force takes over yours. You can call on rudimentary or instinctive knowledge of the subject creature, but not upon its real or acquired knowledge (as can it in your body). For example, you do not automatically know the language or powers of the creature. You each retain your own alignment, Intelligence, Wisdom, and Charisma scores, class, level, skills, base attack bonus, base saving throw bonuses, hit points (regardless of new Constitution score), power points (if any), and power resistance (if any). You each gain the new body’s Strength, Constitution, and Dexterity scores (including modifiers based on these abilities), as well as natural (but not magical) armor. Neither of you gains the other’s special abilities.
　　As a standard action, you can return to your own body, if within range (which ends the power).
　　If your new body is slain, you return to your own body, if within range, and the life force of the original body departs. If your new body is slain beyond the range of the power, you die, but the switched creature lives on in your body permanently. If your body is slain while inhabited by the power’s subject, it dies, and you continue to inhabit the new body permanently. Any life force with nowhere to go is treated as slain.
　　A successful targeted negate psionics manifested on either switched body causes both minds to return to their original bodies, if within range. If they are out of range, negate psionics has no effect.
　
连心术(Mindlink)
　　心灵附魔系(魅力)
　　等级：心灵术士3
　　目标群：一个生物/等级，其中任何两个相距不可超过30
　　灵能点：5
　　如同“次级连心术”，但你可以连接包括你自己的多个生物。
　
Mindlink
　　Telepathy (Cha)
　　Level: Psion 3
　　Targets: One creature/level, no two of which are initially more than 30 ft. apart
　　Power Points: 5
　　As lesser mindlink, except you can link more than just yourself and one other creature.
　
洗脑术(Mindwipe)
　　心灵附魔系(魅力)
　　等级：心灵术士4
　　异象：视觉、物质、听觉
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：近距 (25+5/2等级)
　　目标：单一活物
　　持续时间：立即
　　豁免检定：强韧，通过则无效
　　异能抗力：可
　　灵能点：7
　　你把受害者的一部分经历从他的脑海中抹去，每两个显能者等级给予受术者一个负向等级（最多5个负向等级）。
　　如果受术者得到的负向等级等于或多于其HD，则立即死亡。每个负向等级都将为此生物带来以下减值：命中检定-1减值、豁免检定、技能检定、属性检定以及有效等级（用于决定异能、法术和特殊能力的强度、持续时间、DC和其他细节）。生物也会因此失去5点生命值。除此之外，灵能人物或生物将会失去一个他可用的最高能级异能（施法者则失去一个可用的最高能级法术或法术栏位）。负向等级可以累计。
　　假如受术者幸免一死，他将在每显能者等级一小时之後重新获得失去的等级。通常，负向等级有可能造成永久性的等级吸取，但是由“洗脑术”造成的负向等级不会久到产生这种情况。
　
Mindwipe
　　Telepathy (Cha)
　　Level: Psion 4
　　Display: Vi, Ma, Au
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: Close (25 ft. + 5 ft./2 levels)
　　Target: One living creature
　　Duration: Instantaneous
　　Saving Throw: Fortitude Negates
　　Power Resistance: Yes
　　Power Points: 7
　　You partially wipe your victim’s mind of past experiences, bestowing one negative level per two manifester levels (maximum five negative levels).
　　If the subject has at least as many negative levels as HD, he dies. Each negative level gives a creature the following penalties: -1 penalty on attack rolls, saving throws, skill checks, ability checks, and effective level (for determining the power, duration, DC, and other details of power, spells, or special abilities). The creature also loses 5 hit points. Additionally, a psionic character or creature loses one power from her highest available level (a spellcaster loses one spell or spell slot from her highest available level). Negative levels stack.
　　Assuming the subject survives, he regains lost levels after a number of hours equal to your manifester level. Usually, negative levels have a chance of permanently draining the subject’s levels, but the negative levels from mindwipe don’t last long enough to do so.
　
次级造物术(Minor Creation)
　　心灵创造系(智力)
　　等级：心灵术士1、心灵武士1
　　异象：物质
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：0
　　效果：一个无人持有的、非魔法的、以无生命植物为原料的物体，体积至多1立方/等级
　　持续时间：1小时/等级
　　豁免检定：无
　　异能抗力：不可
　　灵能点：1
　　你创造出一个的非魔法非灵能的以无生命植物原料的无人持有物品：亚麻布衣服、麻绳、木梯等等。创造物的体积不得超过每显能者等级1立方铡Ｄ惚匦胪ü相应的技能检定来创造复杂的物品，例如通过一个“手艺（制弓）”检定来创造一枝笔直的箭杆。
　　试图利用任何创造物作为法术的施法材料将导致法术失败。
　
Minor Creation
　　Metacreativity (Int)
　　Level: Psion 1/Psychic Warrior 1
　　Display: Ma
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: 0 ft.
　　Effect: An unattended, nonmagical object of nonliving plant matter, up to 1 cu. ft./level
　　Duration: 1 hour/level
　　Saving Throw: None
　　Power Resistance: No
　　Power Points: 1
　　You create a nonmagical, nonpsionic, unattended object of nonliving, vegetable matter: linen clothes, a hemp rope, a wooden ladder, and so on. The volume of the item created cannot exceed 1 cubic foot per manifester level. You must succeed at an appropriate skill check to make a complex item, such as a Craft (bowmaking) check to make straight arrow shafts.
　　Attempting to use any created object as a material component in a spell causes the spell to fail.
　
心灵短讯(Missive)
　　心灵附魔系(魅力)
　　等级：心灵术士0
　　异象：视觉
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：近距 (25+5/2等级)
　　目标：单一活物
　　效果：传递给受术者的精神短讯
　　豁免检定：意志，通过则无效
　　异能抗力：可
　　灵能点：1
　　你可以向异能范围内的任何活物送出一条不超过10个单词的心灵短讯。此短讯是单向的，只能由你向受术者发出。如果你与受术者没有共通语言，受术者仅能“听见”毫无意义的音节。
　
Missive
　　Telepathy (Cha)
　　Level: Psion 0
　　Display: Vi
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: Close (25 ft. + 5 ft./2 levels)
　　Target: One living creature
　　Effect: Mental message delivered to subject
　　Saving Throw: Will negates
　　Power Resistance: Yes
　　Power Points: 1
　　You send a telepathic message of up to ten words to any living creature within range. Missive is strictly a one-way exchange from you to the subject. If you do not share a common language, the subject “hears” meaningless mental syllables.
　
支配怪物术(Monster Domination)
　　心灵附魔系(魅力)[胁迫、影响心灵]
　　等级：心灵术士9
　　目标：单一活物
　　持续时间：1天/等级
　　灵能点：17
　　如同“支配术”，但你可以支配任何种类的生物，无论其种类与体型（虽然它必须是活着的）。
　
Monster Domination
　　Telepathy (Cha) [Compulsion, Mind-Affecting]
　　Level: Psion 9
　　Target: One living creature
　　Duration: 1 day/level
　　Power Points: 17
　　As domination, except any kind of creature can be dominated, regardless of size or type (though it must be alive).
　
照明术(My Light)
　　心灵转化系(体质)[光明]
　　等级：心灵术士0
　　异象：听觉、视觉
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：个人 和 20
　　目标：自己 和 20兆蹲捶段
　　持续时间：10分钟/等级 (解消)
　　灵能点：1
　　你的眼中向前射出20盏墓庾丁Ｄ愫推渌生物可以靠此光亮正常观察。如果你进入灵能或魔法黑暗区域，只要你待在其中，“照明术”就会暂时无效。
　
My Light
　　Psychokinesis (Con) [Light]
　　Level: Psion 0
　　Display: Au, Vi
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: Personal and 20 ft.
　　Target: You and 20-ft. cone
　　Duration: 10 minutes/level (D)
　　Power Points: 1
　　Your eyes beam forth a 20-foot-long cone of light. You and other creatures can see normally in the light. If you walk into an area filled with psionic or magical darkness, my light goes dark while you stay within it.
异能详述-N、O、P字头系列
 天生护甲(Natural Armor)
　　心灵自塑系(力量)
　　等级：心灵术士4
　　持续时间：1小时/等级 (解消)
　　灵能点：7
　　如同“次级天生护甲”，但你的防御等级得到+4天生防御加值。并且持续时间也更久。
　
Natural Armor
　　Psychometabolism (Str)
　　Level: Psion 4
　　Duration: 1 hour/level (D)
　　Power Points: 7
　　As lesser natural armor, but you gain a +4 natural armor bonus to AC. Also, the duration is considerably longer.
　
消解灵能(Negate Psionics)
　　心灵转化系(体质)
　　等级：心灵术士3
　　异象：视觉
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：中距 (100+10/等级)
　　目标或区域：单个灵能人物、生物或物品 或 半径30盏谋发范围
　　持续时间：立即
　　豁免检定：无
　　异能抗力：不可
　　灵能点：5
　　你可以用“消解灵能”来终止展现在生物或物体上的正在生效的异能、暂时压制灵能物品的心灵能力或终止正在区域内生效的异能（至少终止其效果）。被消解的异能如同持续时间结束一样终止。“消解灵能”可以消解（但不能反制）超自然能力的效果，如同消解心灵异能一样。“消解灵能”也能如同影响异能（和法术）一样地消解类法术能力。你不能用“消解灵能”持续时间为“立即”的异能造成的效果。
　　你在“消解灵能”的两种用法间选择其一：目标性消解和区域性消解。
　　目标性消解：本异能的目标是单个物体、生物或异能。你针对该异能或是物体或生物上正在生效的每道异能进行消解检定。消解检定为 1d20 + 显能者等级(至多+10)，对抗的DC为 11 + 欲消解的异能的显能者等级。
　　如果你以灵能物品为目标，你必须针对该物品的显能者等级进行消解检定。如果检定成功，该物品的所有灵能属性被压制1d4轮，之後物品恢复正常。灵能物品在被压制期间变成非灵能物品。
　　针对自己所展现的异能的消解检定将自动成功。
　　区域性解除：本异能影响30瞻刖赌诘乃有事物。
　　对每个带有一道或多道异能的生物，你对其所带的显能者等级最高的异能进行消解检定。如果失败，则对显能者等级次高的异能进行检定，以此类推，直到成功消解一道异能（这道“消解灵能”对此目标再无他效）或全部检定都失败。生物所拥有的灵能物品不受影响。
　　对每个带有一道或多道异能的物体，以对生物同样的方式进行消解检定。灵能物品不受区域性消解的影响。
　　对每道有效区域的中心位于“消解灵能”有效区域内的正在生效的异能，你针对该异能进行消解检定以消解之。
　　对每道有效区域和消解区域交迭的异能，你针对该异能进行消解检定，但只能消解交迭区域的效果。
　
Negate Psionics
　　Psychokinesis (Con)
　　Level: Psion 3
　　Display: Vi
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: Medium (100 ft. + 10 ft./level)
　　Target or Area: One psionic character or creature, or one object; or 30-ft.-radius burst
　　Duration: Instantaneous
　　Saving Throw: None
　　Power Resistance: No
　　Power Points: 5
　　You can use negate psionics to end ongoing powers that are manifested on a creature or object, to temporarily suppress the psionic abilities of a psionic item, or to end ongoing power (or at least their effects) within an area. A negated power ends as if its duration had expired. Negate psionics can negate (but not counter) the ongoing effects of supernatural abilities as well as psionic powers. Negate psionics affects spelllike abilities just as it affects powers (and spells). You can’t use negate psionics to undo the effects of any power with instantaneous duration.
　　You choose to use negate psionics in one of two ways: a targeted negation or an area negation:
　　Targeted Negation: One object, creature, or power is the target of the power. You make a negation check against the power or against each ongoing power currently in effect on the object or creature. A negation check is 1d20 + 1 per manifester level (maximum +10) against a DC of 11 + the power-to-be-negated’s manifester level.
　　If the object that you target is a psionic item, you make a negation check against the item’s manifester level. If you succeed, all the item’s psionic properties are suppressed for 1d4 rounds, after which the item recovers on its own. A suppressed item becomes nonpsionic for the duration of the effect.
　　You automatically succeed in your negation check against any power that you manifest yourself.
　　Area Negation: The power affects everything within a 30-foot radius.
　　For each creature that is the target of one or more powers, you make a negation check against the power with the highest manifester level. If that fails, you make negation checks against progressively weaker powers until you negate one power (which discharges the negate psionics so far as that target is concerned) or fail all your checks. The creature’s psionic items are not affected.
　　For each object that is the target of one or more powers, you make negation checks as with creatures. Psionic items are not affected by area negations.
　　For each ongoing power with an area centered within the negate psionics target area, you make a negation check to negate the power.
　　For each ongoing power whose area overlaps with that of the negation, you make a negation check to end the effect but only within the area of the negate psionics.
　
回避侦测(Nondetection)
　　心灵预言系(感知)
　　等级：心灵术士3
　　异象：无
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：接触
　　目标：接触到的生物或物体
　　持续时间：1小时/等级
　　豁免检定：意志，通过则无效 (无害、物体)
　　异能抗力：可 (无害、物体)
　　灵能点：5
　　受保护的生物或物体变得难以用诸如“锐耳术/鹰眼术”和“遥视术”这样的心灵预言系异能或者让他人能从远处观察目标的灵能和魔法物品侦测。如果有人尝试对受保护的生物或物品展现心灵预言系异能，则必须通过显能者等级检定(1d20 + 显能者等级)，DC为 11 + 展现“回避侦测”者的显能者等级。如果你是对自己或自己的持有物展现的“回避侦测”，那么该DC为 15 + 你的显能者等级。
　　如果对生物展现该异能，“回避侦测”除了保护该生物本身，还保护该生物的装备。
　
Nondetection
　　Clairsentience (Wis)
　　Level: Psion 3
　　Display: None
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: Touch
　　Target: Creature or object touched
　　Duration: 1 hour/level
　　Saving Throw: Will negates (harmless, object)
　　Power Resistance: Yes (harmless, object)
　　Power Points: 5
　　The warded creature or object becomes difficult to detect by Clairsentience powers such as clairaudience/clairvoyance and remote viewing, or psionic and magic items that allow others to view the subject from afar. If a Clairsentience power is attempted against the warded creature or item, the manifester of the Clairsentience power must succeed at a manifester level check (1d20 + manifester level) with a DC of 11 + the manifester level of the psionic creature or character who manifested nondetection. If you manifested nondetection on yourself or on an item currently in your possession, the DC is 15 + your manifester level.
　　If manifested on a creature, nondetection wards the creature’s gear as well as the creature itself.
　
反灵能力场(Null Psionics Field)
　　心灵转化系(体质)
　　等级：心灵术士6
　　异象：视觉、听觉
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：10
　　区域：以你为中心，半径10盏拿致范围
　　持续时间：10分钟/等级 (解消)
　　豁免检定：无
　　异能抗力：见说明
　　灵能点：11
　　隐形屏障环绕着你并随你移动。屏障内的空间不受大多数灵能效果影响。同样地，其内的任何灵能物品和心灵异能也都失效。该力场对任何在其内使用、带入其内或对其内部使用的异能或灵能效果都有禁制作用，但并不会消解它们。例如，被支配的生物在力场内时不被支配，但只要他离开力场，支配就会重新生效。异能受禁制的时间依然计入其持续时间。
　　进入力场（或在创造力场时位于其内）的星界构装体会消失，直到力场不再覆盖其消失的地点时才在同一地点重新出现。消失期间正常计入制造该生物的异能的持续时间。如果构装体有异能抗力，你在展现“反灵能力场”时必须针对构造体的PR进行显能者等级检定(1d20 + 显能者等级)以使其消失。
　　灵能剑在异能影响区域内灵能效果无效，但仍是一把剑（而且是精制品）。在创造过程中注入灵能，但完成後即自行活动的构装生物（和只在异能持续期间存在的星质构装体不同）则不受本异能影响。亡灵及外位面者也同样不受影响（除非是召唤而来的）。然而这些生物的心灵异能、类法术能力和超自然能力会暂时被力场废除。
　　“消解灵能”无法移除本力场。两个或多个“反灵能力场”彼此并无影响。神器、圣迹(relics)和半神或更高位阶的生物不受此种凡间灵能的影响。
　　注意：若你的体型大于力场覆盖的区域，则超出范围的身体部位不受力场影响。
　
Null Psionics Field
　　Psychokinesis (Con)
　　Level: Psion 6
　　Display: Vi, Au
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: 10 ft.
　　Area: A 10-ft.-radius emanation, centered on you
　　Duration: 10 minutes/level (D)
　　Saving Throw: None
　　Power Resistance: See text
　　Power Points: 11
　　An invisible barrier surrounds you and moves with you. The space within this barrier is totally impervious to most psionic effects. Likewise, it prevents the functioning of any psionic items or psionic powers within its confines. The field suppresses any powers or psionic effects used within, brought into, or manifested into the area, but does not negate them. A dominated creature, for example, is not dominated while inside the field, but the power resumes functioning when it leaves the field. Time spent within a null psionics field counts against the suppressed power’s duration.
　　Astral constructs wink out if they enter the field (or are inside one when it is created). The construct reappears in the same spot once the null psionics field no longer covers the spot where the construct was. Time spent winked out counts normally against the duration of the power that’s maintaining the creature. If the construct has power resistance, when you manifest the null psionics field you must make a manifester level check (1d20 + manifester level) against the construct’s PR to make it wink out.
　　A psionic sword does not function psionically within the area, but it is still a sword (and a masterwork sword at that). The power has no effect on constructs that are imbued with psionics during their creation process and are thereafter selfsupporting (unlike astral constructs that persist only so long as a power’s duration). Undead and outsiders are likewise unaffected (unless summoned). These creatures’ psionic powers, spell-like abilities, or supernatural abilities, however, may be temporarily nullified by the field.
　　A negate psionics power does not remove the field. Two or more null psionics fields have no appreciable effect on each other. Artifacts, relics, and creatures of demigod or higher status are unaffected by mortal psionics such as this.
　　Note: Should you be larger than the area enclosed by the field, any part of your person that lies outside the field is unaffected by the field.
　
橡木身躯(Oak Body)
　　心灵自塑系(力量)
　　等级：心灵术士7
　　异象：听觉
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：个人
　　目标：自己
　　持续时间：1分钟/等级 (解消)
　　灵能点：13
　　如同“钢铁身躯”，但本异能是将你的身体变为活生生的橡木。
　　你得到伤害减免20/+1。你对目盲、属性伤害、耳聋、疾病、溺水、毒素、震慑以及所有影响你的生理系统与呼吸的异能、法术或攻击免疫，因为在本异能持续期间你不具有任何生理构造，也没有呼吸。你只受到3/4的强酸与寒冷伤害，无论其来源。但你也容易被任何能影响木制品的特殊攻击所影响。
　　你的力量得到+3增强加值，但是你的敏捷受到-3增强减值（敏捷值最低为1）。你的速度降为正常的一半。你无法喝水（因此无法使用药水），也不能吹奏管乐器。
　　你的徒手攻击造成1d6点正常伤害（小体型的显能者造成1d4伤害），并且你的徒手攻击被视为“武装”的。
　　你的体重增加为原来的5倍，但是你能漂浮在水面上。
　
Oak Body
　　Psychometabolism (Str)
　　Level: Psion 7
　　Display: Au
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: Personal
　　Target: You
　　Duration: 1 minute/level (D)
　　Power Points: 13
　　As iron body, but this power transforms your body into living oak.
　　You gain damage reduction 20/+1. You are immune to blindness, damage to ability scores, deafness, disease, drowning, poison, stunning, and all powers, spells, or attacks that affect your physiology or respiration, because you have no physiology or respiration while this power is in effect. You only suffer three-quarters damage from acid and cold of all kinds. However, you also become vulnerable to all special attacks that affect wood.
　　You gain a +3 enhancement bonus to Strength, but you suffer a -3 enhancement penalty to Dexterity as well (to a minimum score of 1), and your speed is reduced to half normal. You cannot drink (and thus can’t use potions), nor play wind instruments.
　　Your unarmed attacks deal 1d6 points of normal damage, and you are considered “armed” when making unarmed attacks (a Small manifester instead deals 1d4 points of damage).
　　Your weight increases by a factor of five, but you float in water.
　
阅读物体(Object Reading)
　　心灵预言系(感知)
　　等级：心灵术士1
　　异象：听觉、物质
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：接触
　　目标：单一物体
　　持续时间：专注，最长10分钟/等级 (解消)
　　豁免检定：无
　　异能抗力：可
　　灵能点：1
　　你能获悉无生命物体以前的主人的详细资料。物体上积聚着的以前的主人留下的精神痕迹可以被本异能读取。揭示的信息量取决于你对特定物体研究了多久。
　　第一轮：前一任主人的种族。
　　第二轮：前一任主人的性别。
　　第三轮：前一任主人的年龄。
　　第四轮：前一任主人的阵营。
　　第五轮：前一任主人如何得到和失去该物体。
　　第六轮及以後：前前任主人的种族，依此类推。
　　以前没有主人的物品不会揭示出信息。只要异能持续，你可以继续依次追溯前任主人列表并获悉他们的详细资料。如果你再次阅读同样的物体，你不会接着上次在前任主人列表中中断的位置继续。
　
Object Reading
　　Clairsentience (Wis)
　　Level: Psion 1
　　Display: Au, Ma
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: Touch
　　Target: One object
　　Duration: Concentration, up to 10 minutes/level (D)
　　Saving Throw: None
　　Power Resistance: Yes
　　Power Points: 1
　　You can learn details of an inanimate object’s previous owner. Objects accumulate psychic impressions left by their previous owners, which can be read by use of this power. The amount of information revealed depends on how long you study a particular object.
　　1st Round: Last owner’s race.
　　2nd Round: Last owner’s gender.
　　3rd Round: Last owner’s age.
　　4th Round: Last owner’s alignment.
　　5th Round: How last owner gained and lost the object.
　　6th+ Round: Previous-to-last owner’s race, and so on.
　　An object without any previous owners reveals no information. You can continue to run down the list of previous owners and learn details about them as long as the power’s duration lasts. If you read the same object again, you do not pick up where you left off in the list of previous owners.
　
痛苦之触(Painful Touch)
　　心灵自塑系(力量)
　　等级：心灵术士2、心灵武士2
　　异象：视觉、物质
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：个人
　　目标：自己
　　持续时间：1轮/等级 (解消)
　　灵能点：3
　　你的徒手攻击造成额外的伤害。当你成功的进行徒手攻击并造成伤害（或配合“牙”与“爪”系列的异能使用），你对目标造成额外的1d6点淤伤。
　
Painful Touch
　　Psychometabolism (Str)
　　Level: Psion 2/Psychic Warrior 2
　　Display: Vi, Ma
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: Personal
　　Target: You
　　Duration: 1 round/level (D)
　　Power Points: 3
　　Your unarmed attacks cause additional pain. When you make a successful unarmed attack that deals damage (or in conjunction with any bite or claw powers), you deal an additional 1d6 points of subdual damage to the target.
　
相位门(Phase Door)
　　心灵传送系(敏捷)
　　等级：心灵术士7
　　异象：视觉
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：接触
　　效果：一个5铡8盏囊蕴位面通道，深度1/等级
　　持续时间：使用一次/2等级
　　豁免检定：无
　　异能抗力：不可
　　灵能点：13
　　本异能可以在木墙、土墙或石墙上打开一个以太位面通道，对其他材质的墙壁无效。“相位门”是隐形的，而且只有你可以看到并使用它。一旦踏入“相位门”你就会消失，直到从另一端离开才会再度出现。如果你愿意，也可以带一个体型不超过中型的生物同行，但视为使用两次。光线、声音、灵能和法术效果都无法穿过此门。所以你也没法看到门对面的东西。展现“相位门”是个逃跑的好办法，但某些生物（例如相位蜘蛛）还是能轻易的追上你。灵能或魔法“真知术”效果可以揭示 “相位门”，但他人还是无法使用此门。
　　“消解灵能”可以解除已经存在的“相位门”。如果此时有生物正在门内，该生物会由最近的出口弹出，就如同在魔法通道内那样。
　　展现“异能恒定术”可以使一个“相位门”永远存在。你可以在门上设定一些触发条件，使别人也能使用此门。这些条件可以很简单也可以很繁杂。你可以设定有形特质为触发条件，如名字、身份或阵营等，但不能用等级、职业、HD或生命值等无形特质作为条件。
　
Phase Door
　　Psychoportation (Dex)
　　Level: Psion 7
　　Display: Vi
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: Touch
　　Effect: Ethereal 5-ft. x 8-ft. opening, 1 ft./level deep
　　Duration: One usage/2 levels
　　Saving Throw: None
　　Power Resistance: No
　　Power Points: 13
　　You create an ethereal passage through wooden, plaster, or stone walls, but not other materials. The phase door is invisible and inaccessible to all creatures except you, and only you can use the passage. You disappear when you enter the phase door and appear when you exit. If you desire, you can take one other creature (Medium-size or smaller) through the door. This counts as two uses of the door. The door does not allow light, sound, psionic effects, or spell effects through it, nor can you see through it without using it. Thus, the power can provide an escape route, though certain creatures, such as phase spiders, can follow with ease. True seeing psionics or magical effects reveal a phase door but do not allow its use.
　　A phase door is subject to negate psionics. If anyone is within the passage when it is negated, she is harmlessly ejected just as if she were inside a magical passwall effect.
　　A phase door can be made permanent with a incarnate power. You can allow other creatures to use the phase door by setting some triggering condition for the door. Such conditions can be as simple or elaborate as you desire. They can be based on a creature’s name, identity, or alignment, but otherwise must be based on observable actions or qualities. Intangibles such as level, class, HD, and hit points don’t qualify.
　
位面传送(Plane Shift)
　　心灵传送系(敏捷)
　　等级：心灵术士7
　　异象：听觉、精神
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：接触
　　目标：接触到的生物 或 至多八个手牵手的生物
　　持续时间：立即
　　豁免检定：意志，通过则无效
　　异能抗力：可
　　灵能点：13
　　你可以把自己或其他生物传送到另一个位面或次元。如果至多八个自愿的受术者手牵手围成一个环，则受术者可以同时被“位面传送”影响。你可以从主物质位面传送至任何位面，但要准确的到达指定的地点近乎不可能，你出现的距离会距离你原本目的地5到500哩（5个百分骰的总和）。
　　注意：位面传送完成後，异能立即结束。如果想回去的话，必须用其他方法。
　
Plane Shift
　　Psychoportation (Dex)
　　Level: Psion 7
　　Display: Au, Me
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: Touch
　　Target: Creature touched, or up to eight willing creatures joining hands
　　Duration: Instantaneous
　　Saving Throw: Will negates
　　Power Resistance: Yes
　　Power Points: 13
　　You move yourself or some other creature to another plane of existence or alternate dimension. If several willing persons link hands in a circle, up to eight can be affected by the plane shift at the same time. Pinpoint accuracy as to a particular arrival location on the intended plane is nigh impossible. From the Material Plane, you can reach any other plane, though you appear 5 to 500 miles (5d%) from your intended destination.
　　Note: Plane shift transports the creatures instantaneously and then ends. The creatures need to find other means if they are to travel back.
　
感知毒性(Poison Sense)
　　心灵预言系(感知)
　　等级：心灵术士3
　　异象：嗅觉
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：30
　　目标：以你为中心，半径30盏睦┥⒎段
　　持续时间：10分钟/等级 (解消)
　　豁免检定：无
　　异能抗力：不可
　　灵能点：5
　　你能觉察到临近场所的毒素的存在。当异能持续时，你能意识到30漳诘亩舅氐拇嬖诩捌浯笾挛恢谩＠如，如果你走向一扇隐藏着毒针陷阱的门，你能觉察到毒素和这扇门有关系。感知检定(DC=16)成功便可以确定毒素的类型。会“炼金术”技能的人物还可以额外尝试进行“炼金术”检定(DC=16)。
　　注意：本异能可以穿透障碍，但会被3蘸竦氖头、3己竦钠胀金属、1己竦那或者6蘸竦哪就坊蚰嗤磷璧病
　
Poison Sense
　　Clairsentience (Wis)
　　Level: Psion 3
　　Display: Ol
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: 30 ft.
　　Target: 30-ft.-radius spread, centered on you
　　Duration: 10 minutes/level (D)
　　Saving Throw: None
　　Power Resistance: No
　　Power Points: 5
　　You sense poison’s presence in your immediate locale. While the duration lasts you become aware of the presence of poison within 30 feet of you, and its general location. For instance, if you walk up to a door with a hidden poison needle trap, you sense that poison is somehow associated with the door. You can determine the exact type of poison with a successful Wisdom check (DC 16). A character with the Alchemy skill may additionally try an Alchemy check (DC 16).
　　Note: The power can penetrate barriers of up to 3 feet of stone, 3 inches of common metal, 1 inch of lead, or 6 feet of wood or dirt.
　
变形自己(Polymorph Self)
　　心灵自塑系(力量)
　　等级：心灵术士4、心灵武士4
　　异象：物质、嗅觉
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：个人
　　目标：自己
　　持续时间：1小时/等级 (解消)
　　灵能点：7
　　你可以把自己变形为另外一种生物。变形後生物的体型最小是微型，最大仅能比你的体型大一级。变形後的HD不能高过你的HD，并且无论如何最高不能超过15HD。你不能变为构装体、元素生物、异界生物或亡灵生物，除非你本来就属于这种类型。
　　变形後，你将恢复受损的生命值，如同你休息了一整天（但无法恢复暂时属性伤害，也不会得到休息一天所带来的其他好处。而且变回原型时不会再得到生命值）。如果变形时被杀，你会变回原型，但不会复活。
　　你获得新形体的肉体和天生能力：体型、身体相关属性（力量、敏捷、体质的种族平均值）、天生防御、天生武器（比如爪抓或者啮咬，但不包括石化、喷吐、能量吸取、能量攻击等），以及类似的肉体特性（有无翅膀、手脚数目等）。拥有更多的手足并不能使你得到比平时更多的攻击次数（发动双武器攻击时也不会较有利）。天生能力包括一般移动能力（比如走路、游泳与用翅膀飞翔）。
　　你并不获得新形体的超自然能力、特异能力或类法术能力。你也不能变成变体生物（例如半龙食人魔）也不能变成虚体或气态生物。
　　你保留你的智力、感知、魅力、职业与等级、生命值（因体质造成的改变不计）、阵营、基本攻击加值与基本豁免加值（新的力量、敏捷与体质会影响最终的攻击加值与豁免加值）。你保留你的特异能力和类法术能力，但不保留超自然能力（如果有的话）。你可以展现异能，或施展能够满足其成分的法术，你要能够发出类人的声音才可以念咒语，要有像人的手才能施展含有姿势成分的法术。
　　如果你的新形体是精类生物、巨人、类人生物、变形怪或亡灵生物，则你的装备也会变成合适的形式。否则，它将变为新身体的一部分并失去效用。变形後的法术材料与器材都不能用来施法。如果装备或者身体的一部分与身体分离的话，会立即变为原型。
　　你可以指定新形态的身体特征（比如毛色、高度和性别），但不能超出该生物应有的正常范围。你能够轻易的易容为该种族的一员。如果你展现本异能来进行易容，则“易容”检定可以得到+10加值。
　
Polymorph Self
　　Psychometabolism (Str)
　　Level: Psion 4/Psychic Warrior 4
　　Display: Ma, Ol
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: Personal
　　Target: You
　　Duration: 1 hour/level (D)
　　Power Points: 7
　　You change your form to that of another creature. The new form can range in size from Diminutive to one size category larger than your normal form. It can have no more Hit Dice than you have, and in any case the assumed form cannot have more than 15 Hit Dice. You cannot change into a construct, elemental, outsider, or undead unless you are already are that type.
　　Upon changing, you regain lost hit points as if having rested for a day (though this healing does not restore temporary ability damage and provide other benefits of resting for a day; and changing back does not heal you further). If slain, you revert to your original form, though you remain dead.
　　You acquire the physical and natural abilities of the new form: natural size, physical ability scores (average Strength, Dexterity, and Constitution for your new form's kind), natural armor, natural weapons (such as claws or bite, but not petrification, breath weapons, energy drain, energy effects, or the like), and similar gross physical qualities (presence or absence of wings, number of extremities, and so forth). A body with extra limbs does not allow you to make more attacks (or more advantageous two-weapon attacks) than normal. Natural abilities also include mundane movement capabilities, such as walking, swimming, and flight with wings.
　　You do not acquire the extraordinary, supernatural, or spell-like abilities of your new form. You cannot change into a variant form of a creature, such as a half-dragon ogre. Incorporeal or gaseous forms cannot be assumed.
　　You retain your Intelligence, Wisdom, and Charisma scores, level and class, hit points (despite any change to your Constitution score), alignment, base attack bonus, and base save bonuses. (New Strength, Dexterity, and Constitution scores may affect final attack and save bonuses.) You retain your extraordinary abilities, spells, and spell-like abilities, but not your supernatural abilities (if any). You can manifest powers, or cast spells for which you have components, but you need a humanlike voice for verbal components and humanlike hands for somatic components.
　　If your new form is a fey, giant, humanoid, shapechanger, or undead, your equipment changes to match the new form and retains its properties. Otherwise, it melds into the new form and becomes nonfunctional. Melded material components and focuses cannot be used to cast spells. Any part of the body or piece of equipment that is separated from the whole reverts to its original form.
　　You choose your form's physical qualities (such as hair color, height, and gender), but they must fall within the normal ranges for the form. You are effectively disguised as an average member of the new form's race. If you use this power to create a disguise, you get a +10 bonus on your Disguise check.
　
异能抗力(Power Resistance)
　　心灵预言系(感知)
　　等级：心灵术士5
　　异象：物质、视觉
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：接触
　　目标：接触到的生物
　　持续时间：1分钟/等级
　　豁免检定：意志，通过则无效 (无害)
　　异能抗力：可 (无害)
　　灵能点：9
　　你给予目标等于 12 + 你的显能者等级 的异能抗力(PR)。
　　欲对有异能抗力的生物使用异能，显能者必须掷 1d20 + 显能者等级，结果不低于该生物的异能抗力才能生效。有异能抗力的生物可以自愿降低异能抗力以接受灵能效果。
　
Power Resistance
　　Clairsentience (Wis)
　　Level: Psion 5
　　Display: Ma, Vi
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: Touch
　　Target: Creature touched
　　Duration: 1 minute/level
　　Saving Throw: Will negates (harmless)
　　Power Resistance: Yes (harmless)
　　Power Points: 9
　　You grant the subject a power resistance (PR) equal to 12 + your manifester level.
　　In order to affect a creature that has power resistance with a power, roll the creature’s power resistance or higher on 1d20 + manifester level A creature with power resistance may voluntarily lower it in order to accept a psionic effect.
　
异能反转(Power Turning)
　　心灵转化系(体质)
　　等级：心灵术士7
　　异象：视觉、精神
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：个人
　　目标：自己
　　持续时间：直到耗尽或10分钟/等级
　　灵能点：13
　　以你为目标的异能（或类法术效果）将弹回原先的显能者身上。本异能只反转以你为目标的异能。效果型和区域型异能不受影响。“异能反转”也不能有效距离为 “接触”的异能。因而，对你展现的“魅惑人类”异能将被反转并可能将显能者魅惑，但“苍火”和“体验命运”就无法反转。
　　可反转的异能能级总和为1d4+6（总共7至10个能级），由DM秘密掷骰确定。每道被反转的异能都将使剩余的可反转能级减少该异能能级。
　　若剩余的可反转能级不够，可能只部分反转某道异能。从该异能能级中减去剩余的可反转能级，所得的差除以该异能能级，这就是该异能对你生效的比例。对于伤害性异能，你和原先的显能者各自按此比例受到伤害。对于非伤害性异能，这就是你们各自的被影响几率。{Andor注：投一个百分骰(或其他更合适的骰子) 决定。}
　　如果你和攻击者都正在受到“异能反转”效果的保护，则会产生共振场。掷百分骰确定结果：
　
─────────────────────────
百分骰　　　　效果
─────────────────────────
０１─７０　　异能未产生效果便衰竭。
７１─８０　　异能对你们双方都完全生效。
８１─９７　　致使双方的反转效果均无效１ｄ４分钟。
９８─１００　双方都进入另一位面。
─────────────────────────
　
Power Turning
　　Psychokinesis (Con)
　　Level: Psion 7
　　Display: Vi, Me
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: Personal
　　Target: You
　　Duration: Until completely expended or 10 minutes/level
　　Power Points: 13
　　Powers (and spell-like effects) targeted against you rebound on the original manifester. This power only turns psionic powers that have you as a target. Effect and area powers are not affected. Power turning also fails to affect touch range powers. Thus, a charm person power manifested at you could be turned back upon and possibly charm the manifester, but whitefire could not be turned back, and neither could destiny dissonance.
　　From 7 to 10 (1d4+6) power levels are affected by the turning. The DM secretly rolls the exact number. Each power turned subtracts its level from the amount of power turning left.
　　A power might be only partially turned. Subtract these from the power level of the incoming psionic power. Divide the number of the remaining levels of the incoming power by the power level of the incoming power to see what fraction of the effect gets through. For damaging power, you and the original manifester each suffer a fraction of the damage. For nondamaging powers, each of you has a proportional chance to be affected.
　　If you and an attacker are both warded by power turning effects in operation, a resonating field is created. Roll randomly to determine the result:
　
─────────────────────────────────────
d%　　　 Effect
─────────────────────────────────────
01--70　 Power drains away without effect.
71--80　 Power affects both of you equally at full effect.
81--97　 Both turning effects are rendered non-functional for 1d4 minutes.
98--100　Both of you go through a rift into another plane.
─────────────────────────────────────
　
预知术(Precognition)
　　心灵预言系(感知)
　　等级：心灵术士6
　　异象：视觉、听觉
　　显能时间：10分钟
　　距离：个人
　　目标：自己
　　持续时间：1分钟/等级 (解消)
　　灵能点：11
　　类似“预言术”但更强，“预知术”异能可对将来一年内发生的关于一个特定目标、事件或行动的问题提供有用的景象。景象可能是有意义的图像的简短闪现，也可能是持续数分钟的无删节的梦景形式。
　　例如，假设问题是“下面这一年里我等面对的最大危险是什么？”DM最终决定让PC们对抗一条他准备了多时的黑龙，并且他认为这最可能成为队伍“命中注定”的最大威胁。因此“预知术”的回应可能是这样的景象：“你看见你和同伴们站在高大的、黑暗的洞口前。洞口被散发着蒸汽的强酸池挡住了，而周围的石头尽被强酸烧焦，并且有着只有巨大的爪子才能造成的撕裂。”无论如何，DM控制着你得到的信息。注意，如果你的队伍没有根据情报行动，条件的改变可能导致情报变得无用。
　　正确预知的基本几率是80%加每显能者等级1%。若环境需要DM可调整该几率（例如，针对心灵预言系异能的特别防范的存在）。如果掷骰失败，你将知道异能失败了，除非制造虚假信息的特殊灵能或魔法正在生效。
　　与“预言术”相同，同一显能者对同一问题多次使用“预知术”，都将得到和第一次同样的回答。
　
Precognition
　　Clairsentience (Wis)
　　Level: Psion 6
　　Display: Vi, Au
　　Manifestation Time: 10 minutes
　　Range: Personal
　　Target: You
　　Duration: 1 minute/level (D)
　　Power Points: 11
　　Similar to divination but more powerful, the precognition power provides you with a useful vision in reply to a question concerning a specific goal, event, or activity that is to occur within a year. The vision can be as simple as a short glimpse of a meaningful image, or it might take the form of a fulllength dream lasting several minutes.
　　 For example, suppose the question is “What is the greatest danger our party will face in the coming year?” The DM eventually wants to pit the player characters against a black dragon he has long prepared, and he considers this is in all likelihood the worst threat that “fate” has in store for the party. Therefore the precognition response might be this vision: “You see you and your comrades standing before the mouth of a high, dark cave-mouth. The entrance is blocked by a steaming pool of acid, while the rock all around is scorched by acid and lacerated by what can only be gargantuan claws.” In all cases, the DM controls what information you receive. Note that if your party doesn’t act on the information, the conditions may change so that the information is no longer useful.
　　The base chance for a correct precognition is 80%, plus 1% per manifester level. The DM adjusts the chance if unusual circumstances require it (if, for example, unusual precautions against Clairsentience powers have been taken). If the dice roll fails, you know the power failed, unless specific psionics or magic yielding false information is at work.
　　As with divinations, multiple precognitions about the same action by the same manifester use the same die roll result as the first precognition and yield the same answer each time.
　
星界旅行(Probability Travel)
　　心灵传送系(敏捷)
　　等级：心灵术士9
　　异象：无
　　显能时间：1分钟
　　距离：接触
　　目标群：自己，每2等级再增加一个接触到的生物
　　持续时间：见说明
　　豁免检定：无
　　异能抗力：可
　　灵能点：17
　　如同“星界投射”，但你和你的伙伴（如果有的话）按你的意愿，可以用真实身体代替星界体进入星界。通过“星界旅行”，你不再拥有“银线”并因此而不再受到那些能切断它的袭击的威胁。不过，如果你在星界中被杀死，你会真的死去，如同你在原属位面被杀一样。
　
Probability Travel
　　Psychoportation (Dex)
　　Level: Psion 9
　　Display: None
　　Manifestation Time: 1 minute
　　Range: Touch
　　Targets: You plus one additional creature touched per two levels
　　Duration: See text
　　Saving Throw: None
　　Power Resistance: Yes
　　Power Points: 17
　　As astral projection, except you and your companions, if any, traverse the Astral Plane as you will physically instead of with an astral surrogate. With probability travel, you possess no silver cord and thus are not vulnerable to those who might sever it. However, if you perish while out journeying amid the planes, you are just as dead as if you had perished in your home plane.
　
卓越战技(Prowess)
　　心灵预言系(感知)
　　等级：心灵武士3
　　异象：精神
　　显能时间：见说明
　　距离：个人
　　目标：自己
　　灵能点：5
　　即使你已经用尽了本轮的借机攻击次数（通常是1次），如果敌人的动作会引发借机攻击，你仍可以进行借机攻击。本异能无法使你在一轮内对同一个目标进行两次借机攻击，除非目标引发了两次独立的借机攻击。
　　你可以即时展现本异能，快到足够让你在本轮内获得额外的借机攻击。展现本异能是即时动作，如同展现瞬发异能，这将计入每轮可使用的瞬发异能限制。
　
Prowess
　　Clairsentience (Wis)
　　Level: Psychic Warrior 3
　　Display: Me
　　Manifestation Time: See text
　　Range: Personal
　　Target: You
　　Power Points: 5
　　If an enemy provokes an attack of opportunity, you can take it, even if you’ve already taken your allotted number of attacks of opportunity this round (usually one). You may not make two attacks of opportunity against the same target in one round even if using this power, unless the target provokes two separate attacks.
　　You can manifest this power instantly, quickly enough to gain an extra attack of opportunity in the same round. Manifesting the power is a free action, like manifesting a quickened power, and it counts toward the normal limit of one quickened power per round.
　
灵能锁(Psionic Lock)
　　心灵传送系(敏捷)
　　等级：心灵术士2
　　异象：物质
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：接触
　　目标：面积不超过30平方盏拿拧⑾渥踊蛉肟
　　持续时间：永久
　　豁免检定：无
　　异能抗力：不可
　　灵能点：3
　　将“灵能锁”展现于门、箱子或入口上将使它们被灵能锁住。你可以自由的越过你自己的锁而不触发它；其他人就只能以暴力，或成功的“消解灵能”或者异能 “敲击术”来打开它。要撞开受“灵能锁”锁上的门时，DC+10。注意：“敲击术”并不能解除“灵能锁”，而只是使它失效10分钟。
　
Psionic Lock
　　Psychoportation (Dex)
　　Level: Psion 2
　　Display: Ma
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: Touch
　　Target: The door, chest, or portal touched, up to 30 square ft./level in size
　　Duration: Permanent
　　Saving Throw: None
　　Power Resistance: No
　　Power Points: 3
　　A psionic lock power manifested upon a door, chest, or portal psionically locks it. You can freely pass your own lock without affecting it; otherwise, a door or object secured with psionic lock can be opened only by breaking in or by a successful negate psionics or knock power. Add +10 to the normal DC to bash open a door or portal affected by this power. Note that knock does not remove psionic lock; it only suppresses it for 10 minutes.
　
心灵手术(Psychic Chirurgery)
　　心灵附魔系(魅力)
　　等级：心灵术士9
　　异象：视觉、听觉、精神
　　显能时间：10分钟
　　距离：近距 (25+5/2等级)
　　目标：单一活物
　　持续时间：立即
　　豁免检定：意志，通过则无效
　　异能抗力：可
　　灵能点：17，消耗经验值 (见说明)
　　你可以修补精神损伤。你也可以授予其他生物你所知道的异能。
　　修补损伤：你可以移除任何强迫与魅惑（比如“呼吸危机”和“厌世术”），甚至那些高于六级的（比如“真实支配术”和“奴役术”）。事实上，你可以利用“心灵手术”移除任何由心灵异能造成的正在持续的或永久的效果，除了生命值的损伤以外。
　　你也可以恢复受术者所有被吸取的等级（或者解除所有负向等级），无论他是怎样失去这些等级的，受术者将被恢复至他以前达到过的最高等级。这些被吸取的等级只有在失去後不超过每显能者等级一小时的时间内才能被恢复。与“改造灵光”不同，这些效果在异能展现完毕後立即停止或被解除，不需要再进行豁免检定。你也可以解除所有伤害受术者属性的异能效果，治愈所有的暂时属性伤害并且恢复所有的永久属性吸取。“心灵手术”同样移除所有形式的精神错乱、困惑以及类似效果，但是它不能恢复因死亡而丧失的等级或体质值。
　　传授知识：如果愿意，你可以直接把你所知的一个异能传授给另一个灵能人物。你无法传授比受术者所能展现的异能更高级的异能。但是你可以传授本来不在此人物的异能列表中的异能。通过“心灵手术”传授的异能不计入人物每等级可知的异能数。
　　经验值费用：每次向另一生物传授一道异能，你需要支付的经验值等于 3000×所传授异能的能级。
　
Psychic Chirurgery
　　Telepathy (Cha)
　　Level: Psion 9
　　Display: Vi, Au, Me
　　Manifestation Time: 10 minutes
　　Range: Close (25 ft. + 5 ft./2 levels)
　　Target: One living creature
　　Duration: Instantaneous
　　Saving Throw: Will negates
　　Power Resistance: Yes
　　Power Points: 17, XP cost (see text)
　　You can repair psychic damage. You can also grant another creature knowledge of powers you know.
　　Repair Damage: You can remove any compulsions ant charms (such as crisis of breath and fatal attraction), even those higher than 6th level (such as true domination and thrall). In fact, you can remove any ongoing or permanent effect caused by a psychic power with psychic chirurgery, save for hit points.
　　You can also restore all drained levels (or disperse all negative levels) afflicting the subject, regardless of how he lost those levels, restoring him to the highest level he had previously achieved. The drained levels are restored only if the time since the subject lost the level is no more than 1 hour per manifester level. Unlike aura alteration, these effects end or are reversed as soon as the manifestation time is completed without need for another saving throw. You can also remove all psionic effects penalizing the subject’s abilities, heal all temporary damage to all ability _ and restore all points permanently drained from all ability scores. Psychic chirurgery also removes all forms of insanity, confusion, and so on, but it does not restore levels or Constitution points lost due to death.
　　Transfer Knowledge: If desired, you can directly transfer knowledge of a power you know to another psionic character. You can’t give a character knowledge of a psionic power of a level higher than she could normally manifest, but you could give her knowledge of a power that is not normally on the character’s power list. Knowledge of powers granted through psychic chirurgery does not count toward the maximum number of powers a character can know per level.
　　XP Cost: Each time you use psychic chirurgery to implant knowledge of a power in another creature, you pay an XP cost equal to 3,000 x the level of the power implanted.
　
心力吸取(Psychic Vampire)
　　心灵转化系(体质)
　　等级：心灵术士5、心灵武士5
　　异象：视觉 (见说明)、精神
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：接触
　　目标：接触到的生物
　　持续时间：1轮/等级
　　豁免检定：强韧，通过则无效
　　异能抗力：可
　　灵能点：9
　　本异能用可以吸取对手灵能的黑暗裹住你的手。成功的近战接触攻击将从对手处吸取2灵能点/等级并立即转化为你的。你无法获得超过每日可用点数的灵能点。吸来的灵能点始终保留在你的馀量中，直到被正常用掉。附着异能的接触攻击被视为武装攻击。
　　对抗没有灵能点的灵能生物（例如灵能点馀量为空的灵能人物或是免费显能的灵能怪物）时，你的接触攻击改为造成1点暂时智力、感知或魅力伤害（由你选择）。你从这次吸取中获得1点灵能点。对于非灵能对手也是同样的效果。
　
Psychic Vampire
　　Psychokinesis (Con)
　　Level: Psion 5/Psychic Warrior 5
　　Display: Vi (see text), Me
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: Touch
　　Target: Creature touched
　　Duration: 1 round/level
　　Saving Throw: Fortitude negates
　　Power Resistance: Yes
　　Power Points: 9
　　This power shrouds your hand with darkness that you can use to drain an opponent’s power. Your successful melee touch attack drains 2 power points/level from your foe and transfers them immediately to you. You can’t gain more power points than you normally have available in a day. The stolen power points remain in your reserve until used normally. Your touch attack, charged with a psionic power, is armed as an armed attack.
　　Against psionic beings who have no power points (such as a psionic character with an empty power point reserve, or a psionic monster that freely manifests its powers), your touch instead deals 1 point of temporary Intelligence, Wisdom, or Charisma damage (your choice). You gain 1 power point from this drain. You have the same effect on nonpsionic opponents.
　
心力回馈(Psychofeedback)
　　心灵自塑系(力量)
　　等级：心灵术士4、心灵武士4
　　异象：视觉
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：个人
　　目标：自己
　　持续时间：1分钟 (解消)
　　灵能点：7
　　你能够利用灵能点来增强你的力量、敏捷和体质调整值，这是即时动作。在异能持续期间，你每轮都能使用灵能点来增强你本轮内的属性调整值（并不是属性值），增强的数量等于你在该轮花费的灵能点数量的一半。比如，你可以将你的力量调整值增加8点（如果你花费16点灵能点）。除非你在下一轮内又花费16 点，否则你的力量修正值将恢复到原有的较低水平。只要你花费所需要的灵能点费用的总和，你也可以同时改变两项属性值，或者同时改变全部三项。你并不需要持续的增强任何属性调整值来维持本异能――只要在异能持续时间内，你就能够在任何回合增强属性调整值。
　
Psychofeedback
　　Psychometabolism (Str)
　　Level: Psion 4/Psychic Warrior 4
　　Display: Vi
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: Personal
　　Target: You
　　Duration: 1 minute (D)
　　Power Points: 7
　　You can use power points to boost your Strength, Dexterity, and Constitution modifiers as a free action. While the duration lasts, you can use power points on a round-by-round basis to boost any or all of your ability score modifiers (not the actual ability score) by a number equal to half the power points you expend for that round as a free action. For example, you can boost your Strength modifier by as much as 8 points (if you spend 16 power points). Unless you again spend 16 power points the following round, though, your Strength modifier returns to its former lower level. You could simultaneously boost two scores, or all three, as long as you pay the total power point cost. You don’t have to boost an ability modifier every round to keep the power in effect―as long as the duration lasts, you have the potential to boost your ability modifiers on any round you choose.
　
银光术(Psycholuminescence)
　　心灵创造系(智力)
　　等级：心灵术士1
　　异象：视觉 (见说明)、听觉
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：接触
　　目标：接触到的物体
　　持续时间：10分钟/等级
　　豁免检定：无
　　异能抗力：不可
　　灵能点：1
　　被碰触的物体发出银色的光，散布于20瞻刖赌凇Ｔ谇抗庀率艿郊踔档纳物若暴露在银光中将受到同样的减值。本异能无法被展现在生物上。如果本异能被展现于一个小物品上，而该物品被挡光的东西完全遮住，则本异能的效果被阻碍，直到遮盖物被移开为止。
　　被带入魔法黑暗的银光（反之亦然）将暂时的被抵消，所以两者效果重叠的区域将保持原有的光亮度（除非使用变体规则“灵能异于魔法”）。
　
Psycholuminescence
　　Metacreativity (Int)
　　Level: Psion 1
　　Display: Vi (see text), Au
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: Touch
　　Target: Object touched
　　Duration: 10 minutes/level
　　Saving Throw: None
　　Power Resistance: No
　　Power Points: 1
　　The object touched begins to glow with a silvery light, shedding in a 20-foot radius. Creatures who suffer penalties in bright light suffer them while exposed to this psycholuminescence. The power cannot be manifested on a creature. If the power is manifested on a small object that is then inside or under a lightproof covering, the power’s effects are blocked until the covering is removed.
　　Psycholuminescence brought into an area of magical darkness (or vice versa) is temporarily negated, so that the orherwise prevailing light conditions exist in the overlapping areas (unless the Psionics Are Different option is in force).
异能详述-Q、R、S字头系列

 萃取术(Quintessence)
　　心灵创造系(智力)
　　等级：心灵术士4
　　异象：物质 (见说明)
　　显能时间：1轮
　　距离：近距 (25+5/2等级)
　　效果：1盎司“精粹” (见说明)
　　持续时间：立即
　　豁免检定：无
　　异能抗力：不可
　　灵能点：7
　　你能够瓦解连续时间中的一小块，形成一团1贾本兜呐ǔ淼慕鹤次铮这被称为“精粹”。从某些角度观察，“精粹”如同银镜一样反射微光，而从另一些角度观测则是完全透明的。它接触到的皮肤首先会感到冰冷的震动而後慢慢转为完全的麻木。你可以把一小团“精粹”涂在任何小物品的表面，例如一把钥匙，一枚戒指，一张封条或者一枚勋章。
　　被封闭于精粹之中的物品不受时间流逝的影响；用术语来讲，它们进入了一个停滞的空间。仅有部分接触到“精粹”的活物肉体也将部分的从时光流动中拉出来。这种分裂将在部分接触开始的10轮後导致每轮1点伤害。
　　“精粹”可以被手工从受保护物体上擦去，将它重新投入时间流动中去。抹去保护膜有75%的机会使“精粹”蒸发并重新回到连续时间中。或者，它将重新结合成一个一贾本兜乃珠形，可以被再度使用。
　　大量的“精粹”集中起来理论上可以保存大型物品或建筑物（或甚至一个完整的活物，如此它将不会受到部分接触造成的伤害）。不过，灵能人物和生物一般不愿意这样做，因为一磅以上的“精粹”团会产生一半强度的“抑能术”效果（DC=16，影响半径5眨包括显能者在内的所有人都将受到影响）。
　
Quintessence
　　Metacreativity (Int)
　　Level: Psion 4
　　Display: Ma (see text)
　　Manifestation Time: 1 round
　　Range: Close (25 ft. + 5 ft./2 levels)
　　Effect: 1 ounce dollop of quintessence (see text)
　　Duration: Instantaneous
　　Saving Throw: None
　　Power Resistance: No
　　Power Points: 7
　　You can collapse a bit of time from the continuum, forming a 1-inch-diameter dollop of thick, gooey material called quintessence. Quintessence shimmers like a silver mirror from some angles but is transparent from others. It brings a cool shock that slowly fades to complete numbness after contact with the skin. You can smooth a dollop of quintessence around any small object, such as a key, a ring, a seal, or an insignia.
　　Objects sealed within quintessence are protected from the effects of time; in practical terms, they enter a state of stasis. Living flesh with only partial contact with quintessence is also partially pulled out of the timestream. This disruption deals 1 point of damage per round beginning 10 rounds after partial contact begins.
　　Quintessence can be manually scraped away from a protected object, freeing it to rejoin the time stream. Removing the protective film is 75% likely to force the quintessence to evaporate back into the continuum. Otherwise, it coalesces again into a 1-inch-diameter bead, available for later usage.
　　Large quantities of quintessence could theoretically be gathered to preserve large items or structures (or even a complete living creature, which would prevent the damage taken from partial contact). However, psionic characters and creatures are generally loath to do so because accumulations of quintessence weighing 1 pound or more generate a halfstrength catapsi effect (DC 16, radius 5 feet, all are affected, including caster).

 体验剧痛(Recall Agony)
　　心灵预言系(感知)
　　等级：心灵术士5
　　灵能点：9
　　如同“体验痛苦”，但折叠的时间展示出的伤害更严重：对手遭受9d6点伤害。
　
Recall Agony
　　Clairsentience (Wis)
　　Level: Psion 5
　　Power Points: 9
　　As recall pain, except the wounds revealed by folding the fourth dimension are worse: The foe takes 9d6 points of damage.
　
体验死亡(Recall Death)
　　心灵预言系(感知)[死亡]
　　等级：心灵术士8
　　距离：近距 (25+5/2等级)
　　豁免检定：意志，通过则部分生效
　　灵能点：15
　　如同“体验痛苦”，但折叠的时间展示出的伤害是致命的。目标可以进行意志豁免以尝试在此攻击下生还。如果豁免成功，他将只受到3d6+15点伤害。
　
Recall Death
　　Clairsentience (Wis) [Death]
　　Level: Psion 8
　　Range: Close (25 ft. + 5 ft./2 levels)
　　Saving Throw: Will partial
　　Power Points: 15
　　As recall pain, except the wounds revealed by folding the fourth dimension are mortal. The target is entitled to a Will save to survive the attack. If she succeeds, she instead sustains 3d6+15 points of damage.
　
体验痛苦(Recall Pain)
　　心灵预言系(感知)
　　等级：心灵术士2
　　异象：物质
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：中距 (100+10/等级)
　　目标：单一活物
　　持续时间：立即
　　豁免检定：意志，通过则效果减半
　　异能抗力：可
　　灵能点：3
　　时间的构造按你的意愿断裂，展示出对手曾经（或将会）受到的创伤。该对手由于过去（或未来）对现在的暂时冲击而遭受3d6点的伤害。
　
Recall Pain
　　Clairsentience (Wis)
　　Level: Psion 2
　　Display: Ma
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: Medium (100 ft. + 10 ft./level)
　　Target: One living creature
　　Duration: Instantaneous
　　Saving Throw: Will half
　　Power Resistance: Yes
　　Power Points: 3
　　The fabric of time parts to your will, revealing wounds your foe has received in the past (or has yet to receive). That foe takes 3d6 points of damage as the past (or future) impinges briefly on the present.
　
异能回弹(Reddopsi)
　　心灵转化系(体质)
　　等级：心灵术士7
　　异象：听觉、嗅觉、精神
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：个人
　　目标：自己
　　持续时间：直到耗尽或10分钟/等级
　　灵能点：13
　　当你展现“异能回弹”时，以你为目标的心灵异能（不包括攻击模式）将弹回给原先的显能者。本异能只回弹以你为目标的异能。效果型和区域型异能不受影响。“异能回弹”也不会回应距离为“接触”的异能。
　　“异能回弹”可以反转任何异能，但反转後便结束，不管被反转的异能多么弱。如果你将某异能反转给了也受到“异能反弹”影响的显能者，那么该异能再次回弹给你。
　
Reddopsi
　　Psychokinesis (Con)
　　Level: Psion 7
　　Display: Au, Ol, Me
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: Personal
　　Target: You
　　Duration: Until expended or 10 minutes/level
　　Power Points: 13
　　When you manifest reddopsi [red-ob-sigh], psionic powers (excluding attack modes) targeted against you rebound on the original manifester. This reverses only powers that have you as a target. Area powers and those that target effects are not affected. Reddopsi also fails to reflect touch range powers.
　　Reddopsi can reverse any power, but ends as soon as it has done so, no matter how minor the power. Should you reverse a power back on a manifester who also is affected by reddopsi, the power rebounds once more upon you.
　
回春术(Rejuvenation)
　　心灵自塑系(力量)
　　等级：心灵术士3
　　异象：听觉
　　显能时间：1分钟
　　距离：个人
　　目标：自己
　　持续时间：10小时
　　灵能点：5
　　“回春术”每小时都可以治疗1点暂时属性伤害，直到治愈或治疗10点为止。本异能并不能恢复永久性属性吸取（比如缚灵的碰触造成的属性伤害）。
　
Rejuvenation
　　Psychometabolism (Str)
　　Level: Psion 3
　　Display: Au
　　Manifestation Time: 1 minute
　　Range: Personal
　　Target: You
　　Duration: 10 hours
　　Power Points: 5
　　Rejuvenation cures 1 point of temporary ability damage per hour, up to a maximum of 10 points. It does not restore permanent ability drain (such as from a wraith’s touch).
　
遥视陷阱(Remote View Trap)
　　心灵预言系(感知)
　　等级：心灵术士6
　　异象：视觉、精神
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：个人
　　目标：自己
　　持续时间：24小时 + 1小时/等级
　　豁免检定：无
　　异能抗力：不可
　　灵能点：11
　　当他人使用“锐耳术/鹰眼术”、“遥视术”或其他从远处观察你的方法时，你准备好的陷阱将给他们一个可怕的意外。在尝试从远处观察你之前，遥视者和你立即进行“遥视”对抗检定，但你的检定获得+10洞察加值。（没有“遥视”技能的生物以智力检定代替。如果对抗魔法探知，则以“遥视”检定对抗对方的“探知”检定。）如果你的结果不低于遥视者，则你未被发现。此外，尝试遥视者从这次麻烦中受到4d4点生物电流（电击）伤害。你意识到有人尝试观察你，但不知道对方的身份及位置。
　
Remote View Trap
　　Clairsentience (Wis)
　　Level: Psion 6
　　Display: Vi, Me
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: Personal
　　Target: You
　　Duration: 24 hours + 1 hour/level
　　Saving Throw: None
　　Power Resistance: No
　　Power Points: 11
　　When others use clairaudience/clairvoyance, remote viewing, or other means of observing you from afar, your prepared trap gives them a nasty surprise. Prior to an attempt to view you from afar, you and the remote viewer immediately make opposed Remote View checks, but you gain a +10 insight bonus on your check. (A Remote View check is the same as an Intelligence check for a creature without the Remote View skill. If opposing a magical scrying, your Remote View check is opposed by the opponent’s Scry check.) If you meet or beat the remote viewer’s result, you are undetected. Moreover, the would-be observer takes 4d14 points of bioelectrical (electricity), damage for his trouble. You are aware of the attempt to view you, but not of the perpetrator or the perpetrator’s location.
　
遥视术(Remote Viewing)
　　心灵预言系(感知)
　　等级：心灵术士3
　　异象：听觉、视觉 (见说明)
　　显能时间：1小时
　　距离：见说明
　　效果：灵能感应场
　　持续时间：1分钟/等级
　　豁免检定：无
　　异能抗力：不可
　　灵能点：5
　　你能看见和听见任意距离外的生物，但必须通过“遥视”检定才行。难度取决于你对目标的了解程度以及你拥有（如果拥有的话）的关于目标的实体线索的类型。此外，若目标在其他位面，你的“遥视”检定得到-5减值。
　
─────────────────────
了解程度　　　　　　　　　“遥视”检定ＤＣ
─────────────────────
一无所知＊　　　　　　　　２０
间接了解（你听说过目标）　１５
直接了解（你遇见过目标）　１０
熟悉（你很了解目标）　　　５
─────────────────────
＊当你对目标生物一无所知时，必须有某种线索才行。
　
─────────────────────
线索　　　　　　　　　　　“遥视”检定加值
─────────────────────
肖像或图片　　　　　　　　＋５
私人物品或衣物　　　　　　＋８
身体部位、毛发、指甲等等　＋１０
─────────────────────
　
　　本异能在目标附近创造一个难以觉察的透明映像（和你大体相似，但不足以识别）。任何智力值不低于12的生物可进行“遥视”技能检定（或智力检定，DC=20），通过则将注意到映像。
　　可能通过“遥视术”展现“心灵短讯”和“黑暗视觉”。“观察灵光”也可以通过“遥视术”展现，但只有每显能者等级5%的几率正常运作。
　
Remote Viewing
　　Clairsentience (Wis)
　　Level: Psion 3
　　Display: Au, Vi (see text)
　　Manifestation Time: 1 hour
　　Range: See text
　　Effect: Psionic sensor
　　Duration: 1 minute/level
　　Saving Throw: None
　　Power Resistance: No
　　Power Points: 5
　　You can see and hear some creature, who may be at any distance. You must succeed at a Remote View check to do so. The difficulty of the task depends on how well you know the subject and what sort of physical connection (if any) you have to that creature. Furthermore, if the subject is on another plane, you get a -5 penalty on the Remote View check.
　
────────────────────────────
　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　Remote View
Knowledge　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　 Check DC
────────────────────────────
None*　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　 20
Secondhand (You have heard of the subject)　15
Firsthand (You have met the subject)　　　　10
Familiar (You know the subject well)　　　　5
────────────────────────────
*You must have some sort of connection to a creature whom you have no knowledge of.
　
────────────────────────────────
　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　Remote View
Connection　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　Check Bonus
────────────────────────────────
Likeness or picture　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　 +5
Possession or garment　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　 +8
Body part, lock of hair, nail clippings, and so on　+10
────────────────────────────────
　
　　This power creates a barely detectable translucent image (roughly similar to your own, but not enough to allow recognition) located near the subject. Any creature with an intelligence score of 12 or higher can notice the image with a successful Remote View check (or Intelligence check against DC 20).
　　Missive and darkvision can be manifested through remote viewing. Aura sight can be manifested through remote viewing but with only a 5% chance per manifester level of operating correctly.
　
回收术(Retrieve)
　　心灵传送系(敏捷)[传送]
　　等级：心灵术士6
　　异象：视觉
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：中距 (100+10/等级)
　　目标：一个你可以用手抓住的，重量不超过10磅/等级的物体
　　持续时间：立即
　　豁免检定：无 (见说明)
　　异能抗力：不可
　　灵能点：11
　　你可以把异能有效距离内你可以看到的物体直接传送到你的手里。如果该物体正被对手占有或持用，你需要尝试以远程攻击加值来卸除武器，如同你正在使用与对手所用相同尺寸的武器。这不会导致借机攻击(参见《玩家手册》第八章中的“卸除武器”)。此时你的攻击检定得到+12能力加值。如果你成功，则你可以“回收”该物品。
　
Retrieve
　　Psychoportation (Dex) [Teleportation]
　　Level: Psion 6
　　Display: Vi
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: Medium (100 ft. + 10 ft./level)
　　Target: One object you could hold in one hand, weighing up to 10 lb./level
　　Duration: Instantaneous
　　Saving Throw: None (see text)
　　Power Resistance: No
　　Power Points: 11
　　You can teleport an item you can see within range directly to your hand. If the object is in the possession of or held by an opponent, you make a disarm attempt using a ranged attack, as if with a weapon the same size as your opponent's. This does not draw an attack of opportunity (see Disarm in Chapter 8 of the Player's Handbook). You gain a +12 competence bonus on your attack roll. If you win, you successfully retrieve the contended object.
　
心智分裂(Schism)
　　心灵附魔系(魅力)
　　等级：心灵术士3
　　异象：视觉、听觉
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：个人
　　目标：自己
　　持续时间：1轮/等级 (解消)
　　灵能点：5
　　你的心智分裂成两个独立的部分。每个部分都完全自主的行动，就好像一个身体中有两个人格一样。新分裂出来的心智无法控制身体，但是可以每轮进行一个纯思维的部分动作（比如展现异能）。两个心智可以以传心术互相沟通。两个都可以使用心灵异能，甚至可以同时使用，虽然双方的灵能点都来自同一个储备。由新分裂出的心智展现的异能将比标准费用多花费2点。
　　这个效果使你每轮可以多做一个部分动作，你可以在标准动作之前或之後做出，只要这个动作是展现异能或其他纯精神活动。在威胁区域内展现异能仍然会引起借机攻击。
　　如果你在分裂期间受到暗示，你可以在第一次豁免检定失败之後再做一次豁免检定。如果你两次豁免均失败，那么你结束分裂状态并且如常受到这个异能的影响。如果你有一次未通过，另外一个心智仍然可以正常行动。
　　注意：法术“加速术”无法作用于“精神分裂”的生物，这是由于它的片断状思维。其他DM所指定的法术与异能同样未必能够生效，或者在最好的情况下，能影响到一个人格。
　
Schism
　　Telepathy (Cha)
　　Level: Psion 3
　　Display: Vi, Au
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: Personal
　　Target: You
　　Duration: 1 round/level (D)
　　Power Points: 5
　　Your mind splits into two independent parts. Each part functions in complete autonomy, like two characters in one body. The newly partitioned mind does not control the body physically but is free to take one partial action each round that is completely mental (such as manifesting a power). Both minds communicate with each other telepathically. Both can use psionic powers, even at the same time, although both draw from the same power point pool. All powers manifested by the newly partitioned personality cost a number of power points equal to their standard cost + 2.
　　This effect allows you to take an extra partial action each round, either before or after your regular action, as long as that action is the manifestation of a power or some other nonphysical activity. Manifesting powers in threatened areas still provokes attacks of opportunity.
　　If you are subjected to a compulsion or charm effect while you are of two minds, make a second saving throw if you fail the first. If you fail both, then schism ends and you are affected normally by the power. If you fail one, the other part of your mind is still free to act normally.
　　 Note: The spell haste does not function on a “split-minded” creature due to its fragmented consciousness. Other spells and powers designated by the DM are likewise unlikely to function, or at the very best, to affect only one of the personalities.
　
识破隐形(See Invisibility)
　　心灵预言系(感知)
　　等级：心灵术士2
　　异象：视觉
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：中距 (100+10/等级)
　　区域：锥状
　　持续时间：10分钟/等级 (解消)
　　豁免检定：无
　　异能抗力：不可
　　灵能点：3
　　你能看见任何隐形的物体或生物，还有星界体和以太体，如同他们是正常可见的。
　　本异能无法揭示隐形的方法，不过有银线的星界旅行者很容易识别。本异能无法揭示幻术或让你看穿不透明的物体。本异能无法揭示躲藏、隐蔽或其他难以发现的生物。
　
See Invisibility
　　Clairsentience (Wis)
　　Level: Psion 2
　　Display: Vi
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: Medium (100 ft. + 10 ft./level)
　　Area: Cone
　　Duration: 10 minutes/level (D)
　　Saving Throw: None
　　Power Resistance: No
　　Power Points: 3
　　You see any objects or beings that are invisible, as well as any that are astral or ethereal, as if they were normally visible.
　　The power does not reveal the method used to obtain invisibility, although an astral traveler is easy to identify if he has a silver cord. It does not reveal illusions or enable you to see through opaque objects. It does not reveal creatures that are simply hiding, concealed, or otherwise hard to see.
　
观声术(See Sound)
　　心灵自塑系(力量)
　　等级：心灵术士1、心灵武士1
　　异象：视觉
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：个人
　　目标：自己
　　持续时间：10分钟/等级 (解消)
　　灵能点：1
　　如同“感声术”，但你透过视觉（看到）感受声音。你必须具有正常视力或正受到“感光术”的作用。你的眼睛将声音转化为光：即使在黑暗中你也能“看见”声音，与此同时某些噪声可能会让物品变形。完全安静的环境会让你“目盲”。你的视力范围没有变化。
　　如果你的耳朵正常，扩展後的听觉给予你的“聆听”技能+1增强加值。如果本异能与“感光术”共用，则增强加值为+2。
　
See Sound
　　Psychometabolism (Str)
　　Level: Psion 1/Psychic Warrior 1
　　Display: Vi
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: Personal
　　Target: You
　　Duration: 10 minutes/level (D)
　　Power Points: 1
　　As feel sound, except you experience sound translated through visual sensation (by sight). You must be able to see normally or also have feel light active. Your eyes convert sound to light: You can see sound even in darkness, as long as some noise is present to give objects shape. You are “blinded” in complete silence. Your range of sight does not change.
　　If your ears are working normally, the expanded reception gives you a +1 enhancement bonus on all Listen checks. If used in conjunction with feel light, the bonus is +2.
　
短讯术(Sending)
　　心灵传送系(敏捷)
　　等级：心灵术士5
　　异象：精神
　　显能时间：10分钟
　　距离：见说明
　　目标：单一生物
　　持续时间：1轮 (见说明)
　　豁免检定：无
　　异能抗力：不可
　　灵能点：9
　　你与一个你熟悉的生物联系并传送25字以内的短讯给对方。如果对方认识你，便能知道是你传的短信。他能以同样方式立即回复。即使智力只有1的生物也可以理解你短讯的内容，但反应能力却受到智力限制。即使对方收到讯息也不一定按照指示行动。
　　如果该生物与你在不同的位面，则讯息有5%的几率丢失。（该位面的环境状况可能使丢失的几率增加。这由DM决定）
　
Sending
　　Psychoportation (Dex)
　　Level: Psion 5
　　Display: Me
　　Manifestation Time: 10 minutes
　　Range: See text
　　Target: One creature
　　Duration: 1 round (see text)
　　Saving Throw: None
　　Power Resistance: No
　　Power Points: 9
　　You contact a particular creature with whom you are familiar and send a short message of twenty-five words or less to the subject. The subject recognizes you if it knows you. It can answer in like manner immediately. Creatures with Intelligence scores as low as 1 can understand the sending, though the subject’s ability to react is limited normally by its Intelligence. Even if the sending is received, the subject creature is not obligated to act upon it in any manner.
　　If the creature in question is not on the same plane of existence as you are, there is a 5% chance that the sending does not arrive. (Local conditions on other planes may worsen this chance considerably, at the DM’s option.)
　
感觉连接(Sense Link)
　　心灵附魔系(魅力)[影响心灵]
　　等级：心灵术士1
　　异象：视觉
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：中距 (100+10/等级)
　　目标：单一活物
　　持续时间：1分钟/等级 (解消)
　　豁免检定：意志，通过则无效
　　异能抗力：可
　　灵能点：1
　　你感觉到受术生物的感官知觉。你只能连接一种感觉，并且你不能在感受间切换。比如，你可以看到受术者能够看到的东西，或者听到它听到的，或尝到它尝到的等等。“感觉链接”一旦被展现，这种连接将保持作用，即使受术生物离开异能有效距离（但是连接无法跨越位面作用）。你无法控制该生物，也无法通过此异能与其交流。
　　你必须保持专注来使用“感觉链接”。如果你没有集中注意力，你的感觉将回到你周围的环境中。如果需要，本异能的受术生物也可以被其他异能或物品所增强，这将带给你加强後的感觉。如果受术者受到凝视攻击，则你也会成为其目标。针对你或被连接生物展现的成功的“消解灵能”将结束本异能。被连接生物是独立的感觉来源，与你自己的目盲、耳聋互不干扰（比如，即使你自己目盲，受术者也不会目盲，所以你仍然可以在异能持续时间内通过“感觉链接”看到东西）。当与受术者连接时，你按照自己的数值进行感觉类检定（比如“侦察”和“聆听”）而与受术者的“侦察”与“聆听”检定结果（如果有的话）无关。
　
Sense Link
　　Telepathy (Cha) [Mind-Affecting]
　　Level: Psion 1
　　Display: Vi
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: Medium (100 ft. + 10 ft./level)
　　Target: One living creature
　　Duration: 1 minute/level (D)
　　Saving Throw: Will negates
　　Power Resistance: Yes
　　Power Points: 1
　　You sense what the subject creature senses. Only one sense is linked, and you may not switch between senses with the same manifestation. For example, you could see what the subject sees, or hear what it hears, or taste what it tastes, and so on. Once sense link is manifested, the link persists even if the subject creature moves out of the original manifestation range (but the link does not work across planes). You do not control the creature, nor can you communicate with it via this power.
　　You must concentrate to access the sense link. If you do not concentrate, that sense returns to your own immediate surroundings. The powers of the subject creature’s senses could be enhanced by other powers or items, if desired, allowing you the same enhanced sense. You are subject to any gaze attack met by the subject creature. A successful negate psionics manifested on you or the linked creature ends the power. With respect to your own blindness, deafness, and so on, the linked creature is an independent sensory organ. (For example, it is not made blind if you are blinded yourself, so you could still see via the sense link while its duration lasts.) When linked to a subject, you make your own perception checks, such as Spot and Listen, regardless of the subject’s Spot and Listen results, if any.
　
感知灵能(Sense Psionics)
　　心灵附魔系(魅力)
　　等级：心灵术士5
　　异象：视觉
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：1哩/等级
　　区域：以你为中心，半径1哩/等级的弥漫范围
　　持续时间：1小时/等级
　　豁免检定：无
　　异能抗力：可 (见说明)
　　灵能点：9
　　你能侦测到范围内的所有灵能活动。你能够得知60漳诒皇褂玫囊炷艿姆较颉⒕嗬爰捌淠芟担但无法得到其他信息。“感知灵能”不够精细但是却很强大：所有不超过八级的异能都无法阻止“感知灵能”侦测灵能活动。
　
Sense Psionics
　　Telepathy (Cha)
　　Level: Psion 5
　　Display: Vi
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: 1 mile/level
　　Area: 1 mile/level radius emanation centered on you
　　Duration: 1 hour/level
　　Saving Throw: None
　　Power Resistance: Yes (see text)
　　Power Points: 9
　　You detect all psionic activity anywhere within range. You know direction and distance from you to within 60 feet and the discipline of the power being used, but no other information is revealed. Sense psionics is crude but strong: All powers of 8th level or less are ineffectual in preventing sense psionics from detecting psionic activity.
　
感知灵旅(Sense Psychoportation)
　　心灵传送系(敏捷)
　　等级：心灵术士2
　　异象：视觉
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：中距 (100+10/等级)
　　区域：以你为中心，以最大显能距离为半径的圆形范围
　　持续时间：1小时/等级 (解消)
　　豁免检定：无
　　异能抗力：不可
　　灵能点：3
　　你得知范围内正在作用的各种传送异能及类似法术。你可以感知不在视野内的传送过程。当你感觉到特定异能发生作用的时候，你将在生物使用它的时候确切的得知。特定的异能包括“任意门”、“空间滑动”、“以太漫步”、“以太化”、“飞行术”、“蛛行术”、“传送术”以及你的DM认可的其他异能。
　
Sense Psychoportation
　　Psychoportation (Dex)
　　Level: Psion 2
　　Display: Vi
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: Medium (100 ft. + 10 ft./level)
　　Area: A circle, centered on you, with a radius of 100 ft. +10 ft./level
　　Duration: 1 hour/level (D)
　　Saving Throw: No
　　Power Resistance: No
　　Power Points: 3
　　You sense the use of various Psychoportation powers and similar spells within the area. You sense the use of these powers whether or not you can directly see them. When you sense the use of a specified effect, you know exactly when the creature is using the power. Specified powers include dimension door, dimension slide, ethereal jaunt, etherealness, fly, spider climb, teleport, and possibly others your DM determines.
　
时间印记(Sensitivity to Psychic Impressions)
　　心灵预言系(感知)
　　等级：心灵术士2
　　异象：听觉、物质
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：近距 (25+5/2等级)
　　目标：以你为中心，以最大显能距离为半径的扩散范围
　　持续时间：专注，最长10分钟/等级 (解消)
　　豁免检定：无
　　异能抗力：不可
　　灵能点：3
　　你获得对特定区域的历史视觉。房间、街道、隧道和其他区域的情绪经历都会积聚下精神痕迹。这种痕迹提供你该区域过去的画面。
　　最容易留下精神痕迹的事件是那些引发强烈情绪的：战争和背叛、结婚和谋杀、出生和剧痛或其他受情绪支配的事情。日常事件不会留下可供显能者侦测的残余痕迹。
　　对事件的视觉是朦胧虚幻的。你不会获得和视觉相关的特殊认知，可是你能够阅读用你的语言写的大幅标语。例如，你在破碎的礼拜堂的广场展现“时间印记”。你获得的景象是：一群受惊的教民从前门和侧门甚至窗户逃离礼拜堂。同时，一个恶魔般的存在从广场的地下冲出并开始有条理地亵渎从前的神圣场所。你注意到的主要情绪是恐惧。
　　每专注一轮可以觉察到一个不同的事件，如果有的话。你的感觉向过去延伸的年数等于 100×你的等级。
　
Sensitivity to Psychic Impressions
　　Clairsentience (Wis)
　　Level: Psion 2
　　Display: Au, Ma
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: Close (25 ft. + 5 ft./2 levels)
　　Target: Area within a 25-ft. + 5 ft./2 levels-radius spread, centered on you
　　Duration: Concentration, up to 10 minutes/level (D)
　　Saving Throw: None
　　Power Resistance: No
　　Power Points: 3
　　You gain historical vision in a given location. Rooms, streets, tunnels, and other discrete locations accumulate psychic impressions left by powerful emotions experienced in a given area. These impressions offer you a picture of the location’s past.
　　The types of events most likely to leave psychic impressions are those that elicited strong emotions: battles and betrayals, marriages and murders, births and great pain, or any other event where one emotion dominates. Everyday occurrences leave no residue for the manifester to detect.
　　The vision of the event is dreamlike and shadowy. You do not gain special knowledge of those involved in the vision, though you might be able to read large banners or othen writing if they are in your language. For example, you manifest sensitivity to psychic impressions in the nave of a shattered chapel. The vision you gain is: A mob of terrified parishioners flees the chapel through front and side doors, and even through windows. Meanwhile, a demonic presence bursts through floor of the nave and systematically begins to desecrate the former holy site. The primary emotion noted by you is terror.
　　You can sense one distinct event per round of concentration, if any exist at all. Your sensitivity extends into the past a number of years equal to 100 x your level.
　
隔离术(Sequester)
　　心灵预言系(感知)
　　等级：心灵术士7
　　异象：无
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：接触
　　目标：一个接触到的生物或体积不超过棱长2/等级的立方体的物体
　　持续时间：1天/等级 (解消)
　　豁免检定：意志，通过则无效 (物体)
　　异能抗力：可 (物体)
　　灵能点：13
　　本异能不只保护受影响的生物或目标免于被心灵预言系异能侦测或定位，还能使受影响的生物或目标对任何形式的视觉隐形。（它还对预言系魔法有效，除非采用变体规则“灵能异于魔法”。）因此，“隔离术”可用来遮掩密门或宝库等等。本异能无法阻止通过触觉或使用装置（例如百眼法袍或遥视镶额眼）发现目标。受 “隔离术”影响的活物（甚至亡灵生物）会陷入昏睡，呈假死状态，直到异能结束或被消解。
　　注意：通过意志豁免地生物不会被隔离。用心灵预言系异能侦测被隔离的生物或物体时无法进行豁免检定。
　
Sequester
　　Clairsentience (Wis)
　　Level: Psion 7
　　Display: None
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: Touch
　　Target: One creature or one object (up to a 2-ft. cube/level) touched
　　Duration: 1 day/level (D)
　　Saving Throw: Will negates (object)
　　Power Resistance: Yes (object)
　　Power Points: 13
　　This power not only prevents Clairsentience powers from working to detect or locate the creature or object affected by sequester, it also renders the affected creature or object invisible to any form of sight or seeing. (It also shields against divination magic, unless the Psionics Are Different option is in use.) Thus, sequester can mask a secret door, a treasure vault, and so on. The power does not prevent the subject from being discovered through tactile means or through the use of devices (such as a robe of eyes or a third eye view). Living creatures (and even undead creatures) affected by sequester become comatose and are effectively in a state of suspended animation until the power wears off or is negated.
　　Note: The Will save prevents a character from being sequestered. There is no saving throw to see the sequestered creature or object or to detect it with a Clairsentience power.
　
隔绝术(Sever the Tie)
　　心灵转化系(体质)
　　等级：心灵术士2
　　异象：听觉、物质
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：中距 (100+10/等级)
　　区域：半径10盏谋发范围内的数个亡灵生物
　　持续时间：立即
　　豁免检定：意志，通过则效果减半
　　异能抗力：可
　　灵能点：3
　　你通过破坏亡灵生物和负能量位面的联结对其造成伤害。你的心灵“镰刀”对异能影响区域内的所有亡灵造成3d8点伤害。被此异能将生命值降到0或更低的亡灵无力地倒下并化为尘埃（如果是实体）或是慢慢消失（如果是虚体）。
　
Sever the Tie
　　Psychokinesis (Con)
　　Level: Psion 2
　　Display: Au, Ma
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: Medium (100 ft. + 10 ft./level)
　　Area: Several undead creatures within a 10-ft.-radius burst
　　Duration: Instantaneous
　　Saving Throw: Will half
　　Power Resistance: Yes
　　Power Points: 3
　　You disrupt an undead creature’s tie to the Negative Energy Plane, damaging or destroying the creature. Your psychokinetic “scythe” deals 3d8 points of damage to all undead within the area. Undead that are brought to 0 hit points or below by use of the power fall limply and molder into dust (if corporeal), or slowly disperse (if incorporeal).
　
阴影身躯(Shadow Body)
　　心灵自塑系(力量)
　　等级：心灵术士8
　　异象：听觉
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：个人
　　目标：自己
　　持续时间：1分钟/等级 (解消)
　　灵能点：15
　　你的身体以及你所有的装备都融进你的阴影里，这将给予你以下几项抗力与能力。
　　作为一个活着的阴影，你可以完全隐藏于任何阴影或黑暗中。你在光亮环境中看起来像是一个独立的阴影。你可以以正常速度移动，不过你可以在任何表面移动，包括墙壁和天花板、液面――甚至是瀑布的正面。
　　在阴影状态下，你会被能够侦测思想、生命力或存在的异能（包括“真知术”）所察觉，或因在光亮处的可疑行动而被发现。你无法造成任何物理伤害也不能操作任何物品，但是你仍然可以如常展现心灵异能。
　　展现心灵异能可能会引起注意，但如果你保持在阴影中，你的“躲藏”技能得到+15加值。你在黑暗环境中几乎不可能被发现（虽然某些异能的异像会短暂的暴露你的精确位置）。
　　你得到伤害减免50/+5。你对“钢铁身躯”中所述的所有伤害免疫，同时也不会受到针对钢铁魔像的攻击。
　
Shadow Body
　　Psychometabolism (Str)
　　Level: Psion 8
　　Display: Au
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: Personal
　　Target: You
　　Duration: 1 minute/level (D)
　　Power Points: 15
　　Your body and all your equipment are subsumed by your shadow, which grants you several powerful resistances and abilities.
　　As a living shadow, you blend perfectly into any other shadow and vanish in darkness. You appear as an unattached shadow in areas of full light. You can move at your normal speed, but you can move on any surface, including walls and ceilings, as well as across the surfaces of liquids―even up the face of a waterfall.
　　While in shadow form, you can be detected by powers that detect thoughts, life, or presences (including true seeing), or by suspicious movements in lighted areas. You cannot harm anyone physically or manipulate any object, but you can use your psionic powers normally.
　　Using psionic powers may attract notice, but if you remain in a shadowed area, you add +15 to your Hide checks. You are nearly undetectable in darkness (although certain power displays could briefly pinpoint your exact location).
　　You gain damage reduction 50/+5. You are immune to a11 things noted in iron body, as well as to things that would harm an iron golem.
　
形体变化(Shapechange)
　　心灵自塑系(力量)
　　等级：心灵术士9
　　异象：视觉、物质
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：个人
　　目标：自己
　　持续时间：10分钟/等级
　　灵能点：17
　　与“变形自己”相同，但本异能可以使你变为任一位阶低于神的生物（包括独特的龙类）或任何单一物品。新形体的体形不能小于跳蚤，其身高、体长或宽度也不能大于200铡Ｓ搿氨湫巫约骸辈煌的是，本异能可以变为虚体生物。
　　新形体的作用与“变形自己”相同。你仍然不能得到新形体的超自然能力、施法能力、心灵能力或类法术能力，不过你可以得到它的特异能力，同时也将保留你原有的特异能力。你的生物类别也将为新形体的生物类别（比如“龙”或“魔法兽”）所取代。你的装备或身体的部分就算与你分离也不会恢复原状。因此，新形态的剧毒啮咬可以正常作用。
　　你可以变成任何你熟悉的事物。你每轮都可以以一个自由动作变身一次。变身既可以发生在你的标准动作之前也可以在其後立即发生，不过不能在动作过程中发生。比如，你正在战斗中，并变形为一个鬼火。当此形体不再有用，你可以变形为一个石魔像然後走开。当你被追击，你可以变为一只跳蚤，躲在马匹上直到你可以安全跳走。你也可以变成一头龙、一只蚂蚁或者任何你熟悉的东西。
　　如果你利用本异能来进行易容，你的“易容”检定得到+10环境加值。
　
Shapechange
　　Psychometabolism (Str)
　　Level: Psion 9
　　Display: Vi, Ma
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: Personal
　　Target: You
　　Duration: 10 minutes/level
　　Power Points: 17
　　As polymorph self, except this power enables you to assume the form of any single creature of less than deity status (including unique dragon types, or the like) or any single object. The assumed form can be no smaller than a flea and no larger than 200 feet in its largest dimension. Unlike polymorph self, this power allows incorporeal forms to be assumed.
　　Your new form works like a polymorph self form. You still do not gain the supernatural, magical, psionic, or spell-like abilities of your new form, though you do gain its extraordinary abilities while keeping your own. You also gain the type of the new form (for example, “dragon” or “magical beast”) in place of your own. Parts of your body or pieces of equipment that are separated from you do not revert to their original forms. Thus, a new form’s poisonous bite is effective.
　　You can become just about anything you are familiar with. You can change form once each round as a free action. The change takes place either immediately before your regular action or immediately after it, but not during the action. For example, you are in combat and assume the form of a will o’ wisp. When this form is no longer useful, you change into a stone golem and walk away. When pursued, you change into a flea, which hides on a horse until it can hop off. From there, you can become a dragon, an ant, or just about anything you are familiar with.
　　If you use this power to create a disguise, you get a +10 circumstance bonus on your Disguise check.
　
谨慎之盾(Shield of Prudence)
　　心灵预言系(感知)
　　等级：心灵术士6、心灵武士6
　　异象：视觉、物质
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：个人
　　目标：自己
　　持续时间：1小时/等级 (解消)
　　豁免检定：无
　　异能抗力：不可
　　灵能点：11
　　你的警觉性延伸到不足一秒的将来，使你能够更好地规避敌人的攻击。你的AC获得+6洞察加值。如果你陷入措手不及，“谨慎之盾”仍能提供+4洞察加值。
　
Shield of Prudence
　　Clairsentience (Wis)
　　Level: Psion 6/Psychic Warrior 6
　　Display: Vi, Ma
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: Personal
　　Target: You
　　Duration: 1 hour/level (D)
　　Saving Throw: None
　　Power Resistance: No
　　Power Points: 11
　　Your awareness extends a few fractions of a second into the future, allowing you to better evade an opponent’s blows. You gain a +6 insight bonus to AC. lf you are caught flat-footed, shield of prudence still grants a +4 insight bonus to AC.
　
滑行术(Skate)
　　心灵传送系(敏捷)
　　等级：心灵术士1、心灵武士1
　　异象：视觉、物质
　　显能时间：单动作
　　距离：接触
　　目标：自己 或 自愿的单一生物 或 单一物品 (总重量至多100磅/等级)
　　持续时间：1分钟/等级 (解消)
　　豁免检定：无
　　异能抗力：不可
　　灵能点：1
　　你、另一个自愿生物或一个无人持有的物品可以在固体地面上滑行，犹如在光滑的冰面上滑行一般。如果“滑行术”被展现于自己或自愿生物，受术者仍旧依照他的意愿保持平衡，这使他可以优雅的在地面上滑行、转弯或急停。在持续时间内，受术者的基本速度增加15眨受术者可以在向上或向下倾斜的斜面上滑行，前提是该斜面是他平时可以安全行走的。上坡将使滑行者的速度降低到正常水平，而下坡将使滑行者的基本速度+30而不是+15。这些加值被视为增强加值。
　　如果本异能被展现于物体，则在沿地面拖动目标物体时它视为仅有原有重量的1/10。
　
Skate
　　Psychoportation (Dex)
　　Level: Psion 1/Psychic Warrior 1
　　Display: Vi, Ma
　　Manifestation Time: 1 action
　　Range: Touch
　　Target: You or one willing creature or one object (total weight up to 100 lb./level)
　　Duration: 1 minute/level (D)
　　Saving Throw: None
　　Power Resistance: No
　　Power Points: 1
　　You, another willing creature, or an unattended object can slide along solid ground as if on smooth ice. If skate is manifested on yourself or another creature, the subject of the power retains equilibrium by mental desire alone, allowing her to gracefully skate along the ground, turn, or stop suddenly as desired. The subject’s base speed is equal to her normal speed + 15 while the duration lasts.
